1855   // the fields array could be too long.  In that case the
1856   // fields array is trimed. Also unused slots that were reserved
1857   // for generic signature indexes are discarded.
1858   {
1859     int i = 0;
1860     for (; i < index * FieldInfo::field_slots; i++) {
1861       _fields->at_put(i, fa[i]);
1862     }
1863     for (int j = total_fields * FieldInfo::field_slots;
1864          j < generic_signature_slot; j++) {
1865       _fields->at_put(i++, fa[j]);
1866     }
1867     assert(_fields->length() == i, "");
1868   }
1869 
1870   if (_need_verify && length > 1) {
1871     // Check duplicated fields
1872     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
1873     NameSigHash** names_and_sigs = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
1874       THREAD, NameSigHash*, HASH_ROW_SIZE);
1875     initialize_hashtable(names_and_sigs);
1876     bool dup = false;
1877     const Symbol* name = NULL;
1878     const Symbol* sig = NULL;
1879     {
1880       debug_only(NoSafepointVerifier nsv;)
1881       for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
1882         name = fs.name();
1883         sig = fs.signature();
1884         // If no duplicates, add name/signature in hashtable names_and_sigs.
1885         if (!put_after_lookup(name, sig, names_and_sigs)) {
1886           dup = true;
1887           break;
1888         }
1889       }
1890     }
1891     if (dup) {
1892       classfile_parse_error("Duplicate field name \"%s\" with signature \"%s\" in class file %s",
1893                              name->as_C_string(), sig->as_klass_external_name(), CHECK);
1894     }
1895   }
1896 }
1897 
1898 
1899 const ClassFileParser::unsafe_u2* ClassFileParser::parse_exception_table(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
1900                                                                          u4 code_length,
1901                                                                          u4 exception_table_length,
1902                                                                          TRAPS) {
1903   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
1904 
1905   const unsafe_u2* const exception_table_start = cfs->current();
1906   assert(exception_table_start != NULL, "null exception table");
1907 
1908   cfs->guarantee_more(8 * exception_table_length, CHECK_NULL); // start_pc,
1909                                                                // end_pc,
1910                                                                // handler_pc,
1911                                                                // catch_type_index
1912 
1913   // Will check legal target after parsing code array in verifier.
1914   if (_need_verify) {
1915     for (unsigned int i = 0; i < exception_table_length; i++) {
1916       const u2 start_pc = cfs->get_u2_fast();
1917       const u2 end_pc = cfs->get_u2_fast();
1918       const u2 handler_pc = cfs->get_u2_fast();
1919       const u2 catch_type_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
1920       guarantee_property((start_pc < end_pc) && (end_pc <= code_length),
1921                          "Illegal exception table range in class file %s",
1922                          CHECK_NULL);
1923       guarantee_property(handler_pc < code_length,
1924                          "Illegal exception table handler in class file %s",
1925                          CHECK_NULL);
1926       if (catch_type_index != 0) {
1927         guarantee_property(valid_klass_reference_at(catch_type_index),
1928                            "Catch type in exception table has bad constant type in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
1929       }
1930     }
1931   } else {
1932     cfs->skip_u2_fast(exception_table_length * 4);
1933   }
1934   return exception_table_start;
1935 }
1936 
1937 void ClassFileParser::parse_linenumber_table(u4 code_attribute_length,
1938                                              u4 code_length,
1939                                              CompressedLineNumberWriteStream**const write_stream,
1940                                              TRAPS) {
1941 
1942   const ClassFileStream* const cfs = _stream;
1943   unsigned int num_entries = cfs->get_u2(CHECK);
1944 
1945   // Each entry is a u2 start_pc, and a u2 line_number
1946   const unsigned int length_in_bytes = num_entries * (sizeof(u2) * 2);
1947 
1948   // Verify line number attribute and table length
1949   check_property(
1950     code_attribute_length == sizeof(u2) + length_in_bytes,
1951     "LineNumberTable attribute has wrong length in class file %s", CHECK);
1952 
1953   cfs->guarantee_more(length_in_bytes, CHECK);
1954 
1955   if ((*write_stream) == NULL) {
1956     if (length_in_bytes > fixed_buffer_size) {
1957       (*write_stream) = new CompressedLineNumberWriteStream(length_in_bytes);
1958     } else {
1959       (*write_stream) = new CompressedLineNumberWriteStream(
1960         _linenumbertable_buffer, fixed_buffer_size);
1961     }
1962   }
1963 
1964   while (num_entries-- > 0) {
1965     const u2 bci  = cfs->get_u2_fast(); // start_pc
1966     const u2 line = cfs->get_u2_fast(); // line_number
1967     guarantee_property(bci < code_length,
1968         "Invalid pc in LineNumberTable in class file %s", CHECK);
1969     (*write_stream)->write_pair(bci, line);
1970   }
1971 }
1972 
1973 
1974 class LVT_Hash : public AllStatic {
1975  public:
1976 
1977   static bool equals(LocalVariableTableElement const& e0, LocalVariableTableElement const& e1) {
1978   /*
1979    * 3-tuple start_bci/length/slot has to be unique key,
1980    * so the following comparison seems to be redundant:
1981    *       && elem->name_cp_index == entry->_elem->name_cp_index
1982    */
1983     return (e0.start_bci     == e1.start_bci &&
1984             e0.length        == e1.length &&
1985             e0.name_cp_index == e1.name_cp_index &&
1986             e0.slot          == e1.slot);
1987   }
1988 
1989   static unsigned int hash(LocalVariableTableElement const& e0) {
1990     unsigned int raw_hash = e0.start_bci;
1991 
1992     raw_hash = e0.length        + raw_hash * 37;
1993     raw_hash = e0.name_cp_index + raw_hash * 37;
1994     raw_hash = e0.slot          + raw_hash * 37;
1995 
1996     return raw_hash;
1997   }
1998 };
1999 
2000 
2001 // Class file LocalVariableTable elements.
2002 class Classfile_LVT_Element {
2003  public:
2004   u2 start_bci;
2005   u2 length;
2006   u2 name_cp_index;
2007   u2 descriptor_cp_index;
2008   u2 slot;
2009 };
2010 
2011 static void copy_lvt_element(const Classfile_LVT_Element* const src,
2012                              LocalVariableTableElement* const lvt) {
2013   lvt->start_bci           = Bytes::get_Java_u2((u1*) &src->start_bci);
2014   lvt->length              = Bytes::get_Java_u2((u1*) &src->length);
2015   lvt->name_cp_index       = Bytes::get_Java_u2((u1*) &src->name_cp_index);
2016   lvt->descriptor_cp_index = Bytes::get_Java_u2((u1*) &src->descriptor_cp_index);
2017   lvt->signature_cp_index  = 0;
2018   lvt->slot                = Bytes::get_Java_u2((u1*) &src->slot);
2019 }
2020 
2021 // Function is used to parse both attributes:
2022 // LocalVariableTable (LVT) and LocalVariableTypeTable (LVTT)
2023 const ClassFileParser::unsafe_u2* ClassFileParser::parse_localvariable_table(const ClassFileStream* cfs,
2024                                                                              u4 code_length,
2025                                                                              u2 max_locals,
2026                                                                              u4 code_attribute_length,
2027                                                                              u2* const localvariable_table_length,
2028                                                                              bool isLVTT,
2029                                                                              TRAPS) {
2030   const char* const tbl_name = (isLVTT) ? "LocalVariableTypeTable" : "LocalVariableTable";
2031   *localvariable_table_length = cfs->get_u2(CHECK_NULL);
2032   const unsigned int size =
2033     (*localvariable_table_length) * sizeof(Classfile_LVT_Element) / sizeof(u2);
2034 
2035   const ConstantPool* const cp = _cp;
2036 
2037   // Verify local variable table attribute has right length
2038   if (_need_verify) {
2039     guarantee_property(code_attribute_length == (sizeof(*localvariable_table_length) + size * sizeof(u2)),
2040                        "%s has wrong length in class file %s", tbl_name, CHECK_NULL);
2041   }
2042 
2043   const unsafe_u2* const localvariable_table_start = cfs->current();
2044   assert(localvariable_table_start != NULL, "null local variable table");
2045   if (!_need_verify) {
2046     cfs->skip_u2_fast(size);
2047   } else {
2048     cfs->guarantee_more(size * 2, CHECK_NULL);
2049     for(int i = 0; i < (*localvariable_table_length); i++) {
2050       const u2 start_pc = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2051       const u2 length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2052       const u2 name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2053       const u2 descriptor_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2054       const u2 index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2055       // Assign to a u4 to avoid overflow
2056       const u4 end_pc = (u4)start_pc + (u4)length;
2057 
2058       if (start_pc >= code_length) {
2059         classfile_parse_error(
2060           "Invalid start_pc %u in %s in class file %s",
2061           start_pc, tbl_name, CHECK_NULL);
2062       }
2063       if (end_pc > code_length) {
2064         classfile_parse_error(
2065           "Invalid length %u in %s in class file %s",
2066           length, tbl_name, CHECK_NULL);
2067       }
2068       const int cp_size = cp->length();
2069       guarantee_property(valid_symbol_at(name_index),
2070         "Name index %u in %s has bad constant type in class file %s",
2071         name_index, tbl_name, CHECK_NULL);
2072       guarantee_property(valid_symbol_at(descriptor_index),
2073         "Signature index %u in %s has bad constant type in class file %s",
2074         descriptor_index, tbl_name, CHECK_NULL);
2075 
2076       const Symbol* const name = cp->symbol_at(name_index);
2077       const Symbol* const sig = cp->symbol_at(descriptor_index);
2078       verify_legal_field_name(name, CHECK_NULL);
2079       u2 extra_slot = 0;
2080       if (!isLVTT) {
2081         verify_legal_field_signature(name, sig, CHECK_NULL);
2082 
2083         // 4894874: check special cases for double and long local variables
2084         if (sig == vmSymbols::type_signature(T_DOUBLE) ||
2085             sig == vmSymbols::type_signature(T_LONG)) {
2086           extra_slot = 1;
2087         }
2088       }
2089       guarantee_property((index + extra_slot) < max_locals,
2090                           "Invalid index %u in %s in class file %s",
2091                           index, tbl_name, CHECK_NULL);
2092     }
2093   }
2094   return localvariable_table_start;
2095 }
2096 
2097 static const u1* parse_stackmap_table(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
2098                                       u4 code_attribute_length,
2099                                       bool need_verify,
2100                                       TRAPS) {
2101   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
2102 
2103   if (0 == code_attribute_length) {
2104     return NULL;
2105   }
2106 
2107   const u1* const stackmap_table_start = cfs->current();
2108   assert(stackmap_table_start != NULL, "null stackmap table");
2109 
2110   // check code_attribute_length first
2111   cfs->skip_u1(code_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2112 
2113   if (!need_verify && !DumpSharedSpaces) {
2114     return NULL;
2115   }
2116   return stackmap_table_start;
2117 }
2118 
2119 const ClassFileParser::unsafe_u2* ClassFileParser::parse_checked_exceptions(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
2120                                                                             u2* const checked_exceptions_length,
2121                                                                             u4 method_attribute_length,
2122                                                                             TRAPS) {
2123   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
2124   assert(checked_exceptions_length != NULL, "invariant");
2125 
2126   cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_NULL);  // checked_exceptions_length
2127   *checked_exceptions_length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2128   const unsigned int size =
2129     (*checked_exceptions_length) * sizeof(CheckedExceptionElement) / sizeof(u2);
2130   const unsafe_u2* const checked_exceptions_start = cfs->current();
2131   assert(checked_exceptions_start != NULL, "null checked exceptions");
2132   if (!_need_verify) {
2133     cfs->skip_u2_fast(size);
2134   } else {
2135     // Verify each value in the checked exception table
2136     u2 checked_exception;
2137     const u2 len = *checked_exceptions_length;
2138     cfs->guarantee_more(2 * len, CHECK_NULL);
2139     for (int i = 0; i < len; i++) {
2140       checked_exception = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2141       check_property(
2142         valid_klass_reference_at(checked_exception),
2143         "Exception name has bad type at constant pool %u in class file %s",
2144         checked_exception, CHECK_NULL);
2145     }
2146   }
2147   // check exceptions attribute length
2148   if (_need_verify) {
2149     guarantee_property(method_attribute_length == (sizeof(*checked_exceptions_length) +
2150                                                    sizeof(u2) * size),
2151                       "Exceptions attribute has wrong length in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
2152   }
2153   return checked_exceptions_start;
2154 }
2155 
2156 void ClassFileParser::throwIllegalSignature(const char* type,
2157                                             const Symbol* name,
2158                                             const Symbol* sig,
2159                                             TRAPS) const {
2160   assert(name != NULL, "invariant");
2161   assert(sig != NULL, "invariant");
2162 
2163   const char* class_note = "";
2164   if (is_value_type() && name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name()) {
2165     class_note = " (an inline class)";
2166   }
2167 
2168   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
2169   Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
2170       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
2171       "%s \"%s\" in class %s%s has illegal signature \"%s\"", type,
2172       name->as_C_string(), _class_name->as_C_string(), class_note, sig->as_C_string());
2173 }
2174 
2175 AnnotationCollector::ID
2176 AnnotationCollector::annotation_index(const ClassLoaderData* loader_data,
2177                                       const Symbol* name) {
2178   const vmSymbols::SID sid = vmSymbols::find_sid(name);
2179   // Privileged code can use all annotations.  Other code silently drops some.
2180   const bool privileged = loader_data->is_the_null_class_loader_data() ||
2181                           loader_data->is_platform_class_loader_data() ||
2182                           loader_data->is_unsafe_anonymous();
2183   switch (sid) {
2184     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(reflect_CallerSensitive_signature): {
2185       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2186       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2187       return _method_CallerSensitive;
2188     }
2189     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_vm_annotation_ForceInline_signature): {
2190       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2191       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2192       return _method_ForceInline;
2193     }
2194     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_vm_annotation_DontInline_signature): {
2195       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2196       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2197       return _method_DontInline;
2198     }
2199     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(java_lang_invoke_InjectedProfile_signature): {
2200       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2201       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2202       return _method_InjectedProfile;
2203     }
2204     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(java_lang_invoke_LambdaForm_Compiled_signature): {
2205       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2206       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2207       return _method_LambdaForm_Compiled;
2208     }
2209     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_vm_annotation_Hidden_signature): {
2210       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2211       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2212       return _method_Hidden;
2213     }
2214     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate_signature): {
2215       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2216       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2217       return _method_HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate;
2218     }
2219     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_vm_annotation_Stable_signature): {
2220       if (_location != _in_field)   break;  // only allow for fields
2221       if (!privileged)              break;  // only allow in privileged code
2222       return _field_Stable;
2223     }
2224     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_vm_annotation_Contended_signature): {
2225       if (_location != _in_field && _location != _in_class) {
2226         break;  // only allow for fields and classes
2227       }
2228       if (!EnableContended || (RestrictContended && !privileged)) {
2229         break;  // honor privileges
2230       }
2231       return _jdk_internal_vm_annotation_Contended;
2232     }
2233     case vmSymbols::VM_SYMBOL_ENUM_NAME(jdk_internal_vm_annotation_ReservedStackAccess_signature): {
2234       if (_location != _in_method)  break;  // only allow for methods
2235       if (RestrictReservedStack && !privileged) break; // honor privileges
2236       return _jdk_internal_vm_annotation_ReservedStackAccess;
2237     }
2238     default: {
2239       break;
2240     }
2241   }
2242   return AnnotationCollector::_unknown;
2243 }
2244 
2245 void ClassFileParser::FieldAnnotationCollector::apply_to(FieldInfo* f) {
2246   if (is_contended())
2247     f->set_contended_group(contended_group());
2248   if (is_stable())
2249     f->set_stable(true);
2250 }
2251 
2252 ClassFileParser::FieldAnnotationCollector::~FieldAnnotationCollector() {
2253   // If there's an error deallocate metadata for field annotations
2254   MetadataFactory::free_array<u1>(_loader_data, _field_annotations);
2255   MetadataFactory::free_array<u1>(_loader_data, _field_type_annotations);
2256 }
2257 
2258 void MethodAnnotationCollector::apply_to(const methodHandle& m) {
2259   if (has_annotation(_method_CallerSensitive))
2260     m->set_caller_sensitive(true);
2261   if (has_annotation(_method_ForceInline))
2262     m->set_force_inline(true);
2263   if (has_annotation(_method_DontInline))
2264     m->set_dont_inline(true);
2265   if (has_annotation(_method_InjectedProfile))
2266     m->set_has_injected_profile(true);
2267   if (has_annotation(_method_LambdaForm_Compiled) && m->intrinsic_id() == vmIntrinsics::_none)
2268     m->set_intrinsic_id(vmIntrinsics::_compiledLambdaForm);
2269   if (has_annotation(_method_Hidden))
2270     m->set_hidden(true);
2271   if (has_annotation(_method_HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate) && !m->is_synthetic())
2272     m->set_intrinsic_candidate(true);
2273   if (has_annotation(_jdk_internal_vm_annotation_ReservedStackAccess))
2274     m->set_has_reserved_stack_access(true);
2275 }
2276 
2277 void ClassFileParser::ClassAnnotationCollector::apply_to(InstanceKlass* ik) {
2278   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
2279   ik->set_is_contended(is_contended());
2280 }
2281 
2282 #define MAX_ARGS_SIZE 255
2283 #define MAX_CODE_SIZE 65535
2284 #define INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER 256
2285 
2286 /* Copy class file LVT's/LVTT's into the HotSpot internal LVT.
2287  *
2288  * Rules for LVT's and LVTT's are:
2289  *   - There can be any number of LVT's and LVTT's.
2290  *   - If there are n LVT's, it is the same as if there was just
2291  *     one LVT containing all the entries from the n LVT's.
2292  *   - There may be no more than one LVT entry per local variable.
2293  *     Two LVT entries are 'equal' if these fields are the same:
2294  *        start_pc, length, name, slot
2295  *   - There may be no more than one LVTT entry per each LVT entry.
2296  *     Each LVTT entry has to match some LVT entry.
2297  *   - HotSpot internal LVT keeps natural ordering of class file LVT entries.
2298  */
2299 void ClassFileParser::copy_localvariable_table(const ConstMethod* cm,
2300                                                int lvt_cnt,
2301                                                u2* const localvariable_table_length,
2302                                                const unsafe_u2** const localvariable_table_start,
2303                                                int lvtt_cnt,
2304                                                u2* const localvariable_type_table_length,
2305                                                const unsafe_u2** const localvariable_type_table_start,
2306                                                TRAPS) {
2307 
2308   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
2309 
2310   typedef ResourceHashtable<LocalVariableTableElement, LocalVariableTableElement*,
2311                             &LVT_Hash::hash, &LVT_Hash::equals> LVT_HashTable;
2312 
2313   LVT_HashTable* const table = new LVT_HashTable();
2314 
2315   // To fill LocalVariableTable in
2316   const Classfile_LVT_Element* cf_lvt;
2317   LocalVariableTableElement* lvt = cm->localvariable_table_start();
2318 
2319   for (int tbl_no = 0; tbl_no < lvt_cnt; tbl_no++) {
2320     cf_lvt = (Classfile_LVT_Element *) localvariable_table_start[tbl_no];
2321     for (int idx = 0; idx < localvariable_table_length[tbl_no]; idx++, lvt++) {
2322       copy_lvt_element(&cf_lvt[idx], lvt);
2323       // If no duplicates, add LVT elem in hashtable.
2324       if (table->put(*lvt, lvt) == false
2325           && _need_verify
2326           && _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
2327         classfile_parse_error("Duplicated LocalVariableTable attribute "
2328                               "entry for '%s' in class file %s",
2329                                _cp->symbol_at(lvt->name_cp_index)->as_utf8(),
2330                                CHECK);
2331       }
2332     }
2333   }
2334 
2335   // To merge LocalVariableTable and LocalVariableTypeTable
2336   const Classfile_LVT_Element* cf_lvtt;
2337   LocalVariableTableElement lvtt_elem;
2338 
2339   for (int tbl_no = 0; tbl_no < lvtt_cnt; tbl_no++) {
2340     cf_lvtt = (Classfile_LVT_Element *) localvariable_type_table_start[tbl_no];
2341     for (int idx = 0; idx < localvariable_type_table_length[tbl_no]; idx++) {
2342       copy_lvt_element(&cf_lvtt[idx], &lvtt_elem);
2343       LocalVariableTableElement** entry = table->get(lvtt_elem);
2344       if (entry == NULL) {
2345         if (_need_verify) {
2346           classfile_parse_error("LVTT entry for '%s' in class file %s "
2347                                 "does not match any LVT entry",
2348                                  _cp->symbol_at(lvtt_elem.name_cp_index)->as_utf8(),
2349                                  CHECK);
2350         }
2351       } else if ((*entry)->signature_cp_index != 0 && _need_verify) {
2352         classfile_parse_error("Duplicated LocalVariableTypeTable attribute "
2353                               "entry for '%s' in class file %s",
2354                                _cp->symbol_at(lvtt_elem.name_cp_index)->as_utf8(),
2355                                CHECK);
2356       } else {
2357         // to add generic signatures into LocalVariableTable
2358         (*entry)->signature_cp_index = lvtt_elem.descriptor_cp_index;
2359       }
2360     }
2361   }
2362 }
2363 
2364 
2365 void ClassFileParser::copy_method_annotations(ConstMethod* cm,
2366                                        const u1* runtime_visible_annotations,
2367                                        int runtime_visible_annotations_length,
2368                                        const u1* runtime_invisible_annotations,
2369                                        int runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
2370                                        const u1* runtime_visible_parameter_annotations,
2371                                        int runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length,
2372                                        const u1* runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations,
2373                                        int runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length,
2374                                        const u1* runtime_visible_type_annotations,
2375                                        int runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
2376                                        const u1* runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
2377                                        int runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
2378                                        const u1* annotation_default,
2379                                        int annotation_default_length,
2380                                        TRAPS) {
2381 
2382   AnnotationArray* a;
2383 
2384   if (runtime_visible_annotations_length +
2385       runtime_invisible_annotations_length > 0) {
2386      a = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_annotations,
2387                               runtime_visible_annotations_length,
2388                               runtime_invisible_annotations,
2389                               runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
2390                               CHECK);
2391      cm->set_method_annotations(a);
2392   }
2393 
2394   if (runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length +
2395       runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length > 0) {
2396     a = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_parameter_annotations,
2397                              runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length,
2398                              runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations,
2399                              runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length,
2400                              CHECK);
2401     cm->set_parameter_annotations(a);
2402   }
2403 
2404   if (annotation_default_length > 0) {
2405     a = assemble_annotations(annotation_default,
2406                              annotation_default_length,
2407                              NULL,
2408                              0,
2409                              CHECK);
2410     cm->set_default_annotations(a);
2411   }
2412 
2413   if (runtime_visible_type_annotations_length +
2414       runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length > 0) {
2415     a = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_type_annotations,
2416                              runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
2417                              runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
2418                              runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
2419                              CHECK);
2420     cm->set_type_annotations(a);
2421   }
2422 }
2423 
2424 
2425 // Note: the parse_method below is big and clunky because all parsing of the code and exceptions
2426 // attribute is inlined. This is cumbersome to avoid since we inline most of the parts in the
2427 // Method* to save footprint, so we only know the size of the resulting Method* when the
2428 // entire method attribute is parsed.
2429 //
2430 // The promoted_flags parameter is used to pass relevant access_flags
2431 // from the method back up to the containing klass. These flag values
2432 // are added to klass's access_flags.
2433 
2434 Method* ClassFileParser::parse_method(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
2435                                       bool is_interface,
2436                                       bool is_value_type,
2437                                       const ConstantPool* cp,
2438                                       AccessFlags* const promoted_flags,
2439                                       TRAPS) {
2440   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
2441   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
2442   assert(promoted_flags != NULL, "invariant");
2443 
2444   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
2445   // Parse fixed parts:
2446   // access_flags, name_index, descriptor_index, attributes_count
2447   cfs->guarantee_more(8, CHECK_NULL);
2448 
2449   int flags = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2450   const u2 name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2451   const int cp_size = cp->length();
2452   check_property(
2453     valid_symbol_at(name_index),
2454     "Illegal constant pool index %u for method name in class file %s",
2455     name_index, CHECK_NULL);
2456   const Symbol* const name = cp->symbol_at(name_index);
2457   verify_legal_method_name(name, CHECK_NULL);
2458 
2459   const u2 signature_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2460   guarantee_property(
2461     valid_symbol_at(signature_index),
2462     "Illegal constant pool index %u for method signature in class file %s",
2463     signature_index, CHECK_NULL);
2464   const Symbol* const signature = cp->symbol_at(signature_index);
2465 
2466   if (name == vmSymbols::class_initializer_name()) {
2467     // We ignore the other access flags for a valid class initializer.
2468     // (JVM Spec 2nd ed., chapter 4.6)
2469     if (_major_version < 51) { // backward compatibility
2470       flags = JVM_ACC_STATIC;
2471     } else if ((flags & JVM_ACC_STATIC) == JVM_ACC_STATIC) {
2472       flags &= JVM_ACC_STATIC | JVM_ACC_STRICT;
2473     } else {
2474       classfile_parse_error("Method <clinit> is not static in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
2475     }
2476   } else {
2477     verify_legal_method_modifiers(flags, is_interface, is_value_type, name, CHECK_NULL);
2478   }
2479 
2480   if (name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name()) {
2481     if (is_interface) {
2482       classfile_parse_error("Interface cannot have a method named <init>, class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
2483     } else if (!is_value_type && signature->is_void_method_signature()) {
2484       // OK, a constructor
2485     } else if (is_value_type && !signature->is_void_method_signature()) {
2486       // also OK, a static factory, as long as the return value is good
2487       bool ok = false;
2488       SignatureStream ss((Symbol*) signature, true);
2489       while (!ss.at_return_type())  ss.next();
2490       if (ss.is_reference()) {
2491         Symbol* ret = ss.as_symbol();
2492         const Symbol* required = class_name();
2493         if (is_unsafe_anonymous()) {
2494           // The original class name in the UAC byte stream gets changed.  So
2495           // using the original name in the return type is no longer valid.
2496           required = vmSymbols::java_lang_Object();
2497         }
2498         ok = (ret == required);
2499       }
2500       if (!ok) {
2501         throwIllegalSignature("Method", name, signature, CHECK_0);
2502       }
2503     } else {
2504       // not OK, so throw the same error as in verify_legal_method_signature.
2505       throwIllegalSignature("Method", name, signature, CHECK_0);
2506     }
2507     // A declared <init> method must always be either a non-static
2508     // object constructor, with a void return, or else it must be a
2509     // static factory method, with a non-void return.  No other
2510     // definition of <init> is possible.
2511     //
2512     // The verifier (in verify_invoke_instructions) will inspect the
2513     // signature of any attempt to invoke <init>, and ensures that it
2514     // returns non-void if and only if it is being invoked by
2515     // invokestatic, and void if and only if it is being invoked by
2516     // invokespecial.
2517     //
2518     // When a symbolic reference to <init> is resolved for a
2519     // particular invocation mode (special or static), the mode is
2520     // matched to the JVM_ACC_STATIC modifier of the <init> method.
2521     // Thus, it is impossible to statically invoke a constructor, and
2522     // impossible to "new + invokespecial" a static factory, either
2523     // through bytecode or through reflection.
2524   }
2525 
2526   int args_size = -1;  // only used when _need_verify is true
2527   if (_need_verify) {
2528     args_size = ((flags & JVM_ACC_STATIC) ? 0 : 1) +
2529                  verify_legal_method_signature(name, signature, CHECK_NULL);
2530     if (args_size > MAX_ARGS_SIZE) {
2531       classfile_parse_error("Too many arguments in method signature in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
2532     }
2533   }
2534 
2535   AccessFlags access_flags(flags & JVM_RECOGNIZED_METHOD_MODIFIERS);
2536 
2537   // Default values for code and exceptions attribute elements
2538   u2 max_stack = 0;
2539   u2 max_locals = 0;
2540   u4 code_length = 0;
2541   const u1* code_start = 0;
2542   u2 exception_table_length = 0;
2543   const unsafe_u2* exception_table_start = NULL; // (potentially unaligned) pointer to array of u2 elements
2544   Array<int>* exception_handlers = Universe::the_empty_int_array();
2545   u2 checked_exceptions_length = 0;
2546   const unsafe_u2* checked_exceptions_start = NULL; // (potentially unaligned) pointer to array of u2 elements
2547   CompressedLineNumberWriteStream* linenumber_table = NULL;
2548   int linenumber_table_length = 0;
2549   int total_lvt_length = 0;
2550   u2 lvt_cnt = 0;
2551   u2 lvtt_cnt = 0;
2552   bool lvt_allocated = false;
2553   u2 max_lvt_cnt = INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER;
2554   u2 max_lvtt_cnt = INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER;
2555   u2* localvariable_table_length = NULL;
2556   const unsafe_u2** localvariable_table_start = NULL; // (potentially unaligned) pointer to array of LVT attributes
2557   u2* localvariable_type_table_length = NULL;
2558   const unsafe_u2** localvariable_type_table_start = NULL; // (potentially unaligned) pointer to LVTT attributes
2559   int method_parameters_length = -1;
2560   const u1* method_parameters_data = NULL;
2561   bool method_parameters_seen = false;
2562   bool parsed_code_attribute = false;
2563   bool parsed_checked_exceptions_attribute = false;
2564   bool parsed_stackmap_attribute = false;
2565   // stackmap attribute - JDK1.5
2566   const u1* stackmap_data = NULL;
2567   int stackmap_data_length = 0;
2568   u2 generic_signature_index = 0;
2569   MethodAnnotationCollector parsed_annotations;
2570   const u1* runtime_visible_annotations = NULL;
2571   int runtime_visible_annotations_length = 0;
2572   const u1* runtime_invisible_annotations = NULL;
2573   int runtime_invisible_annotations_length = 0;
2574   const u1* runtime_visible_parameter_annotations = NULL;
2575   int runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length = 0;
2576   const u1* runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations = NULL;
2577   int runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length = 0;
2578   const u1* runtime_visible_type_annotations = NULL;
2579   int runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = 0;
2580   const u1* runtime_invisible_type_annotations = NULL;
2581   int runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = 0;
2582   bool runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = false;
2583   bool runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = false;
2584   bool runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_exists = false;
2585   const u1* annotation_default = NULL;
2586   int annotation_default_length = 0;
2587 
2588   // Parse code and exceptions attribute
2589   u2 method_attributes_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2590   while (method_attributes_count--) {
2591     cfs->guarantee_more(6, CHECK_NULL);  // method_attribute_name_index, method_attribute_length
2592     const u2 method_attribute_name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2593     const u4 method_attribute_length = cfs->get_u4_fast();
2594     check_property(
2595       valid_symbol_at(method_attribute_name_index),
2596       "Invalid method attribute name index %u in class file %s",
2597       method_attribute_name_index, CHECK_NULL);
2598 
2599     const Symbol* const method_attribute_name = cp->symbol_at(method_attribute_name_index);
2600     if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_code()) {
2601       // Parse Code attribute
2602       if (_need_verify) {
2603         guarantee_property(
2604             !access_flags.is_native() && !access_flags.is_abstract(),
2605                         "Code attribute in native or abstract methods in class file %s",
2606                          CHECK_NULL);
2607       }
2608       if (parsed_code_attribute) {
2609         classfile_parse_error("Multiple Code attributes in class file %s",
2610                               CHECK_NULL);
2611       }
2612       parsed_code_attribute = true;
2613 
2614       // Stack size, locals size, and code size
2615       cfs->guarantee_more(8, CHECK_NULL);
2616       max_stack = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2617       max_locals = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2618       code_length = cfs->get_u4_fast();
2619       if (_need_verify) {
2620         guarantee_property(args_size <= max_locals,
2621                            "Arguments can't fit into locals in class file %s",
2622                            CHECK_NULL);
2623         guarantee_property(code_length > 0 && code_length <= MAX_CODE_SIZE,
2624                            "Invalid method Code length %u in class file %s",
2625                            code_length, CHECK_NULL);
2626       }
2627       // Code pointer
2628       code_start = cfs->current();
2629       assert(code_start != NULL, "null code start");
2630       cfs->guarantee_more(code_length, CHECK_NULL);
2631       cfs->skip_u1_fast(code_length);
2632 
2633       // Exception handler table
2634       cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_NULL);  // exception_table_length
2635       exception_table_length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2636       if (exception_table_length > 0) {
2637         exception_table_start = parse_exception_table(cfs,
2638                                                       code_length,
2639                                                       exception_table_length,
2640                                                       CHECK_NULL);
2641       }
2642 
2643       // Parse additional attributes in code attribute
2644       cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_NULL);  // code_attributes_count
2645       u2 code_attributes_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2646 
2647       unsigned int calculated_attribute_length = 0;
2648 
2649       calculated_attribute_length =
2650           sizeof(max_stack) + sizeof(max_locals) + sizeof(code_length);
2651       calculated_attribute_length +=
2652         code_length +
2653         sizeof(exception_table_length) +
2654         sizeof(code_attributes_count) +
2655         exception_table_length *
2656             ( sizeof(u2) +   // start_pc
2657               sizeof(u2) +   // end_pc
2658               sizeof(u2) +   // handler_pc
2659               sizeof(u2) );  // catch_type_index
2660 
2661       while (code_attributes_count--) {
2662         cfs->guarantee_more(6, CHECK_NULL);  // code_attribute_name_index, code_attribute_length
2663         const u2 code_attribute_name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
2664         const u4 code_attribute_length = cfs->get_u4_fast();
2665         calculated_attribute_length += code_attribute_length +
2666                                        sizeof(code_attribute_name_index) +
2667                                        sizeof(code_attribute_length);
2668         check_property(valid_symbol_at(code_attribute_name_index),
2669                        "Invalid code attribute name index %u in class file %s",
2670                        code_attribute_name_index,
2671                        CHECK_NULL);
2672         if (LoadLineNumberTables &&
2673             cp->symbol_at(code_attribute_name_index) == vmSymbols::tag_line_number_table()) {
2674           // Parse and compress line number table
2675           parse_linenumber_table(code_attribute_length,
2676                                  code_length,
2677                                  &linenumber_table,
2678                                  CHECK_NULL);
2679 
2680         } else if (LoadLocalVariableTables &&
2681                    cp->symbol_at(code_attribute_name_index) == vmSymbols::tag_local_variable_table()) {
2682           // Parse local variable table
2683           if (!lvt_allocated) {
2684             localvariable_table_length = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2685               THREAD, u2,  INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2686             localvariable_table_start = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2687               THREAD, const unsafe_u2*, INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2688             localvariable_type_table_length = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2689               THREAD, u2,  INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2690             localvariable_type_table_start = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2691               THREAD, const unsafe_u2*, INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2692             lvt_allocated = true;
2693           }
2694           if (lvt_cnt == max_lvt_cnt) {
2695             max_lvt_cnt <<= 1;
2696             localvariable_table_length = REALLOC_RESOURCE_ARRAY(u2, localvariable_table_length, lvt_cnt, max_lvt_cnt);
2697             localvariable_table_start  = REALLOC_RESOURCE_ARRAY(const unsafe_u2*, localvariable_table_start, lvt_cnt, max_lvt_cnt);
2698           }
2699           localvariable_table_start[lvt_cnt] =
2700             parse_localvariable_table(cfs,
2701                                       code_length,
2702                                       max_locals,
2703                                       code_attribute_length,
2704                                       &localvariable_table_length[lvt_cnt],
2705                                       false,    // is not LVTT
2706                                       CHECK_NULL);
2707           total_lvt_length += localvariable_table_length[lvt_cnt];
2708           lvt_cnt++;
2709         } else if (LoadLocalVariableTypeTables &&
2710                    _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION &&
2711                    cp->symbol_at(code_attribute_name_index) == vmSymbols::tag_local_variable_type_table()) {
2712           if (!lvt_allocated) {
2713             localvariable_table_length = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2714               THREAD, u2,  INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2715             localvariable_table_start = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2716               THREAD, const unsafe_u2*, INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2717             localvariable_type_table_length = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2718               THREAD, u2,  INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2719             localvariable_type_table_start = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
2720               THREAD, const unsafe_u2*, INITIAL_MAX_LVT_NUMBER);
2721             lvt_allocated = true;
2722           }
2723           // Parse local variable type table
2724           if (lvtt_cnt == max_lvtt_cnt) {
2725             max_lvtt_cnt <<= 1;
2726             localvariable_type_table_length = REALLOC_RESOURCE_ARRAY(u2, localvariable_type_table_length, lvtt_cnt, max_lvtt_cnt);
2727             localvariable_type_table_start  = REALLOC_RESOURCE_ARRAY(const unsafe_u2*, localvariable_type_table_start, lvtt_cnt, max_lvtt_cnt);
2728           }
2729           localvariable_type_table_start[lvtt_cnt] =
2730             parse_localvariable_table(cfs,
2731                                       code_length,
2732                                       max_locals,
2733                                       code_attribute_length,
2734                                       &localvariable_type_table_length[lvtt_cnt],
2735                                       true,     // is LVTT
2736                                       CHECK_NULL);
2737           lvtt_cnt++;
2738         } else if (_major_version >= Verifier::STACKMAP_ATTRIBUTE_MAJOR_VERSION &&
2739                    cp->symbol_at(code_attribute_name_index) == vmSymbols::tag_stack_map_table()) {
2740           // Stack map is only needed by the new verifier in JDK1.5.
2741           if (parsed_stackmap_attribute) {
2742             classfile_parse_error("Multiple StackMapTable attributes in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
2743           }
2744           stackmap_data = parse_stackmap_table(cfs, code_attribute_length, _need_verify, CHECK_NULL);
2745           stackmap_data_length = code_attribute_length;
2746           parsed_stackmap_attribute = true;
2747         } else {
2748           // Skip unknown attributes
2749           cfs->skip_u1(code_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2750         }
2751       }
2752       // check method attribute length
2753       if (_need_verify) {
2754         guarantee_property(method_attribute_length == calculated_attribute_length,
2755                            "Code segment has wrong length in class file %s",
2756                            CHECK_NULL);
2757       }
2758     } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_exceptions()) {
2759       // Parse Exceptions attribute
2760       if (parsed_checked_exceptions_attribute) {
2761         classfile_parse_error("Multiple Exceptions attributes in class file %s",
2762                               CHECK_NULL);
2763       }
2764       parsed_checked_exceptions_attribute = true;
2765       checked_exceptions_start =
2766             parse_checked_exceptions(cfs,
2767                                      &checked_exceptions_length,
2768                                      method_attribute_length,
2769                                      CHECK_NULL);
2770     } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_method_parameters()) {
2771       // reject multiple method parameters
2772       if (method_parameters_seen) {
2773         classfile_parse_error("Multiple MethodParameters attributes in class file %s",
2774                               CHECK_NULL);
2775       }
2776       method_parameters_seen = true;
2777       method_parameters_length = cfs->get_u1_fast();
2778       const u2 real_length = (method_parameters_length * 4u) + 1u;
2779       if (method_attribute_length != real_length) {
2780         classfile_parse_error(
2781           "Invalid MethodParameters method attribute length %u in class file",
2782           method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2783       }
2784       method_parameters_data = cfs->current();
2785       cfs->skip_u2_fast(method_parameters_length);
2786       cfs->skip_u2_fast(method_parameters_length);
2787       // ignore this attribute if it cannot be reflected
2788       if (!SystemDictionary::Parameter_klass_loaded())
2789         method_parameters_length = -1;
2790     } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_synthetic()) {
2791       if (method_attribute_length != 0) {
2792         classfile_parse_error(
2793           "Invalid Synthetic method attribute length %u in class file %s",
2794           method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2795       }
2796       // Should we check that there hasn't already been a synthetic attribute?
2797       access_flags.set_is_synthetic();
2798     } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_deprecated()) { // 4276120
2799       if (method_attribute_length != 0) {
2800         classfile_parse_error(
2801           "Invalid Deprecated method attribute length %u in class file %s",
2802           method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2803       }
2804     } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
2805       if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_signature()) {
2806         if (generic_signature_index != 0) {
2807           classfile_parse_error(
2808             "Multiple Signature attributes for method in class file %s",
2809             CHECK_NULL);
2810         }
2811         if (method_attribute_length != 2) {
2812           classfile_parse_error(
2813             "Invalid Signature attribute length %u in class file %s",
2814             method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2815         }
2816         generic_signature_index = parse_generic_signature_attribute(cfs, CHECK_NULL);
2817       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_annotations()) {
2818         if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
2819           classfile_parse_error(
2820             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleAnnotations attributes for method in class file %s",
2821             CHECK_NULL);
2822         }
2823         runtime_visible_annotations_length = method_attribute_length;
2824         runtime_visible_annotations = cfs->current();
2825         assert(runtime_visible_annotations != NULL, "null visible annotations");
2826         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_annotations_length, CHECK_NULL);
2827         parse_annotations(cp,
2828                           runtime_visible_annotations,
2829                           runtime_visible_annotations_length,
2830                           &parsed_annotations,
2831                           _loader_data,
2832                           CHECK_NULL);
2833         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_annotations_length);
2834       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_annotations()) {
2835         if (runtime_invisible_annotations_exists) {
2836           classfile_parse_error(
2837             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleAnnotations attributes for method in class file %s",
2838             CHECK_NULL);
2839         }
2840         runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = true;
2841         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
2842           runtime_invisible_annotations_length = method_attribute_length;
2843           runtime_invisible_annotations = cfs->current();
2844           assert(runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL, "null invisible annotations");
2845         }
2846         cfs->skip_u1(method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2847       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_parameter_annotations()) {
2848         if (runtime_visible_parameter_annotations != NULL) {
2849           classfile_parse_error(
2850             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleParameterAnnotations attributes for method in class file %s",
2851             CHECK_NULL);
2852         }
2853         runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length = method_attribute_length;
2854         runtime_visible_parameter_annotations = cfs->current();
2855         assert(runtime_visible_parameter_annotations != NULL, "null visible parameter annotations");
2856         cfs->skip_u1(runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length, CHECK_NULL);
2857       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations()) {
2858         if (runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_exists) {
2859           classfile_parse_error(
2860             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleParameterAnnotations attributes for method in class file %s",
2861             CHECK_NULL);
2862         }
2863         runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_exists = true;
2864         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
2865           runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length = method_attribute_length;
2866           runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations = cfs->current();
2867           assert(runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations != NULL,
2868             "null invisible parameter annotations");
2869         }
2870         cfs->skip_u1(method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2871       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_annotation_default()) {
2872         if (annotation_default != NULL) {
2873           classfile_parse_error(
2874             "Multiple AnnotationDefault attributes for method in class file %s",
2875             CHECK_NULL);
2876         }
2877         annotation_default_length = method_attribute_length;
2878         annotation_default = cfs->current();
2879         assert(annotation_default != NULL, "null annotation default");
2880         cfs->skip_u1(annotation_default_length, CHECK_NULL);
2881       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_type_annotations()) {
2882         if (runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL) {
2883           classfile_parse_error(
2884             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleTypeAnnotations attributes for method in class file %s",
2885             CHECK_NULL);
2886         }
2887         runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = method_attribute_length;
2888         runtime_visible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
2889         assert(runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL, "null visible type annotations");
2890         // No need for the VM to parse Type annotations
2891         cfs->skip_u1(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length, CHECK_NULL);
2892       } else if (method_attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_type_annotations()) {
2893         if (runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists) {
2894           classfile_parse_error(
2895             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleTypeAnnotations attributes for method in class file %s",
2896             CHECK_NULL);
2897         } else {
2898           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = true;
2899         }
2900         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
2901           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = method_attribute_length;
2902           runtime_invisible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
2903           assert(runtime_invisible_type_annotations != NULL, "null invisible type annotations");
2904         }
2905         cfs->skip_u1(method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2906       } else {
2907         // Skip unknown attributes
2908         cfs->skip_u1(method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2909       }
2910     } else {
2911       // Skip unknown attributes
2912       cfs->skip_u1(method_attribute_length, CHECK_NULL);
2913     }
2914   }
2915 
2916   if (linenumber_table != NULL) {
2917     linenumber_table->write_terminator();
2918     linenumber_table_length = linenumber_table->position();
2919   }
2920 
2921   // Make sure there's at least one Code attribute in non-native/non-abstract method
2922   if (_need_verify) {
2923     guarantee_property(access_flags.is_native() ||
2924                        access_flags.is_abstract() ||
2925                        parsed_code_attribute,
2926                        "Absent Code attribute in method that is not native or abstract in class file %s",
2927                        CHECK_NULL);
2928   }
2929 
2930   // All sizing information for a Method* is finally available, now create it
2931   InlineTableSizes sizes(
2932       total_lvt_length,
2933       linenumber_table_length,
2934       exception_table_length,
2935       checked_exceptions_length,
2936       method_parameters_length,
2937       generic_signature_index,
2938       runtime_visible_annotations_length +
2939            runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
2940       runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length +
2941            runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length,
2942       runtime_visible_type_annotations_length +
2943            runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
2944       annotation_default_length,
2945       0);
2946 
2947   Method* const m = Method::allocate(_loader_data,
2948                                      code_length,
2949                                      access_flags,
2950                                      &sizes,
2951                                      ConstMethod::NORMAL,
2952                                      CHECK_NULL);
2953 
2954   ClassLoadingService::add_class_method_size(m->size()*wordSize);
2955 
2956   // Fill in information from fixed part (access_flags already set)
2957   m->set_constants(_cp);
2958   m->set_name_index(name_index);
2959   m->set_signature_index(signature_index);
2960   m->compute_from_signature(cp->symbol_at(signature_index));
2961   assert(args_size < 0 || args_size == m->size_of_parameters(), "");
2962 
2963   // Fill in code attribute information
2964   m->set_max_stack(max_stack);
2965   m->set_max_locals(max_locals);
2966   if (stackmap_data != NULL) {
2967     m->constMethod()->copy_stackmap_data(_loader_data,
2968                                          (u1*)stackmap_data,
2969                                          stackmap_data_length,
2970                                          CHECK_NULL);
2971   }
2972 
2973   // Copy byte codes
2974   m->set_code((u1*)code_start);
2975 
2976   // Copy line number table
2977   if (linenumber_table != NULL) {
2978     memcpy(m->compressed_linenumber_table(),
2979            linenumber_table->buffer(),
2980            linenumber_table_length);
2981   }
2982 
2983   // Copy exception table
2984   if (exception_table_length > 0) {
2985     Copy::conjoint_swap_if_needed<Endian::JAVA>(exception_table_start,
2986                                                 m->exception_table_start(),
2987                                                 exception_table_length * sizeof(ExceptionTableElement),
2988                                                 sizeof(u2));
2989   }
2990 
2991   // Copy method parameters
2992   if (method_parameters_length > 0) {
2993     MethodParametersElement* elem = m->constMethod()->method_parameters_start();
2994     for (int i = 0; i < method_parameters_length; i++) {
2995       elem[i].name_cp_index = Bytes::get_Java_u2((address)method_parameters_data);
2996       method_parameters_data += 2;
2997       elem[i].flags = Bytes::get_Java_u2((address)method_parameters_data);
2998       method_parameters_data += 2;
2999     }
3000   }
3001 
3002   // Copy checked exceptions
3003   if (checked_exceptions_length > 0) {
3004     Copy::conjoint_swap_if_needed<Endian::JAVA>(checked_exceptions_start,
3005                                                 m->checked_exceptions_start(),
3006                                                 checked_exceptions_length * sizeof(CheckedExceptionElement),
3007                                                 sizeof(u2));
3008   }
3009 
3010   // Copy class file LVT's/LVTT's into the HotSpot internal LVT.
3011   if (total_lvt_length > 0) {
3012     promoted_flags->set_has_localvariable_table();
3013     copy_localvariable_table(m->constMethod(),
3014                              lvt_cnt,
3015                              localvariable_table_length,
3016                              localvariable_table_start,
3017                              lvtt_cnt,
3018                              localvariable_type_table_length,
3019                              localvariable_type_table_start,
3020                              CHECK_NULL);
3021   }
3022 
3023   if (parsed_annotations.has_any_annotations())
3024     parsed_annotations.apply_to(methodHandle(THREAD, m));
3025 
3026   // Copy annotations
3027   copy_method_annotations(m->constMethod(),
3028                           runtime_visible_annotations,
3029                           runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3030                           runtime_invisible_annotations,
3031                           runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
3032                           runtime_visible_parameter_annotations,
3033                           runtime_visible_parameter_annotations_length,
3034                           runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations,
3035                           runtime_invisible_parameter_annotations_length,
3036                           runtime_visible_type_annotations,
3037                           runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
3038                           runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
3039                           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
3040                           annotation_default,
3041                           annotation_default_length,
3042                           CHECK_NULL);
3043 
3044   if (name == vmSymbols::finalize_method_name() &&
3045       signature == vmSymbols::void_method_signature()) {
3046     if (m->is_empty_method()) {
3047       _has_empty_finalizer = true;
3048     } else {
3049       _has_finalizer = true;
3050     }
3051   }
3052   if (name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name() &&
3053       signature == vmSymbols::void_method_signature() &&
3054       m->is_vanilla_constructor()) {
3055     _has_vanilla_constructor = true;
3056   }
3057 
3058   NOT_PRODUCT(m->verify());
3059   return m;
3060 }
3061 
3062 
3063 // The promoted_flags parameter is used to pass relevant access_flags
3064 // from the methods back up to the containing klass. These flag values
3065 // are added to klass's access_flags.
3066 // Side-effects: populates the _methods field in the parser
3067 void ClassFileParser::parse_methods(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3068                                     bool is_interface,
3069                                     bool is_value_type,
3070                                     AccessFlags* promoted_flags,
3071                                     bool* has_final_method,
3072                                     bool* declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods,
3073                                     TRAPS) {
3074   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3075   assert(promoted_flags != NULL, "invariant");
3076   assert(has_final_method != NULL, "invariant");
3077   assert(declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods != NULL, "invariant");
3078 
3079   assert(NULL == _methods, "invariant");
3080 
3081   cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK);  // length
3082   const u2 length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3083   if (length == 0) {
3084     _methods = Universe::the_empty_method_array();
3085   } else {
3086     _methods = MetadataFactory::new_array<Method*>(_loader_data,
3087                                                    length,
3088                                                    NULL,
3089                                                    CHECK);
3090 
3091     for (int index = 0; index < length; index++) {
3092       Method* method = parse_method(cfs,
3093                                     is_interface,
3094                                     is_value_type,
3095                                     _cp,
3096                                     promoted_flags,
3097                                     CHECK);
3098 
3099       if (method->is_final()) {
3100         *has_final_method = true;
3101       }
3102       // declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods: declares concrete instance methods, any access flags
3103       // used for interface initialization, and default method inheritance analysis
3104       if (is_interface && !(*declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods)
3105         && !method->is_abstract() && !method->is_static()) {
3106         *declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods = true;
3107       }
3108       _methods->at_put(index, method);
3109     }
3110 
3111     if (_need_verify && length > 1) {
3112       // Check duplicated methods
3113       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
3114       NameSigHash** names_and_sigs = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(
3115         THREAD, NameSigHash*, HASH_ROW_SIZE);
3116       initialize_hashtable(names_and_sigs);
3117       bool dup = false;
3118       const Symbol* name = NULL;
3119       const Symbol* sig = NULL;
3120       {
3121         debug_only(NoSafepointVerifier nsv;)
3122         for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
3123           const Method* const m = _methods->at(i);
3124           name = m->name();
3125           sig = m->signature();
3126           // If no duplicates, add name/signature in hashtable names_and_sigs.
3127           if (!put_after_lookup(name, sig, names_and_sigs)) {
3128             dup = true;
3129             break;
3130           }
3131         }
3132       }
3133       if (dup) {
3134         classfile_parse_error("Duplicate method name \"%s\" with signature \"%s\" in class file %s",
3135                                name->as_C_string(), sig->as_klass_external_name(), CHECK);
3136       }
3137     }
3138   }
3139 }
3140 
3141 static const intArray* sort_methods(Array<Method*>* methods) {
3142   const int length = methods->length();
3143   // If JVMTI original method ordering or sharing is enabled we have to
3144   // remember the original class file ordering.
3145   // We temporarily use the vtable_index field in the Method* to store the
3146   // class file index, so we can read in after calling qsort.
3147   // Put the method ordering in the shared archive.
3148   if (JvmtiExport::can_maintain_original_method_order() || Arguments::is_dumping_archive()) {
3149     for (int index = 0; index < length; index++) {
3150       Method* const m = methods->at(index);
3151       assert(!m->valid_vtable_index(), "vtable index should not be set");
3152       m->set_vtable_index(index);
3153     }
3154   }
3155   // Sort method array by ascending method name (for faster lookups & vtable construction)
3156   // Note that the ordering is not alphabetical, see Symbol::fast_compare
3157   Method::sort_methods(methods);
3158 
3159   intArray* method_ordering = NULL;
3160   // If JVMTI original method ordering or sharing is enabled construct int
3161   // array remembering the original ordering
3162   if (JvmtiExport::can_maintain_original_method_order() || Arguments::is_dumping_archive()) {
3163     method_ordering = new intArray(length, length, -1);
3164     for (int index = 0; index < length; index++) {
3165       Method* const m = methods->at(index);
3166       const int old_index = m->vtable_index();
3167       assert(old_index >= 0 && old_index < length, "invalid method index");
3168       method_ordering->at_put(index, old_index);
3169       m->set_vtable_index(Method::invalid_vtable_index);
3170     }
3171   }
3172   return method_ordering;
3173 }
3174 
3175 // Parse generic_signature attribute for methods and fields
3176 u2 ClassFileParser::parse_generic_signature_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3177                                                       TRAPS) {
3178   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3179 
3180   cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_0);  // generic_signature_index
3181   const u2 generic_signature_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3182   check_property(
3183     valid_symbol_at(generic_signature_index),
3184     "Invalid Signature attribute at constant pool index %u in class file %s",
3185     generic_signature_index, CHECK_0);
3186   return generic_signature_index;
3187 }
3188 
3189 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_sourcefile_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3190                                                            TRAPS) {
3191 
3192   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3193 
3194   cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK);  // sourcefile_index
3195   const u2 sourcefile_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3196   check_property(
3197     valid_symbol_at(sourcefile_index),
3198     "Invalid SourceFile attribute at constant pool index %u in class file %s",
3199     sourcefile_index, CHECK);
3200   set_class_sourcefile_index(sourcefile_index);
3201 }
3202 
3203 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_source_debug_extension_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3204                                                                        int length,
3205                                                                        TRAPS) {
3206   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3207 
3208   const u1* const sde_buffer = cfs->current();
3209   assert(sde_buffer != NULL, "null sde buffer");
3210 
3211   // Don't bother storing it if there is no way to retrieve it
3212   if (JvmtiExport::can_get_source_debug_extension()) {
3213     assert((length+1) > length, "Overflow checking");
3214     u1* const sde = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(THREAD, u1, length+1);
3215     for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
3216       sde[i] = sde_buffer[i];
3217     }
3218     sde[length] = '\0';
3219     set_class_sde_buffer((const char*)sde, length);
3220   }
3221   // Got utf8 string, set stream position forward
3222   cfs->skip_u1(length, CHECK);
3223 }
3224 
3225 
3226 // Inner classes can be static, private or protected (classic VM does this)
3227 #define RECOGNIZED_INNER_CLASS_MODIFIERS ( JVM_RECOGNIZED_CLASS_MODIFIERS | \
3228                                            JVM_ACC_PRIVATE |                \
3229                                            JVM_ACC_PROTECTED |              \
3230                                            JVM_ACC_STATIC                   \
3231                                          )
3232 
3233 // Return number of classes in the inner classes attribute table
3234 u2 ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_inner_classes_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3235                                                             const u1* const inner_classes_attribute_start,
3236                                                             bool parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute,
3237                                                             u2 enclosing_method_class_index,
3238                                                             u2 enclosing_method_method_index,
3239                                                             TRAPS) {
3240   const u1* const current_mark = cfs->current();
3241   u2 length = 0;
3242   if (inner_classes_attribute_start != NULL) {
3243     cfs->set_current(inner_classes_attribute_start);
3244     cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_0);  // length
3245     length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3246   }
3247 
3248   // 4-tuples of shorts of inner classes data and 2 shorts of enclosing
3249   // method data:
3250   //   [inner_class_info_index,
3251   //    outer_class_info_index,
3252   //    inner_name_index,
3253   //    inner_class_access_flags,
3254   //    ...
3255   //    enclosing_method_class_index,
3256   //    enclosing_method_method_index]
3257   const int size = length * 4 + (parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute ? 2 : 0);
3258   Array<u2>* const inner_classes = MetadataFactory::new_array<u2>(_loader_data, size, CHECK_0);
3259   _inner_classes = inner_classes;
3260 
3261   int index = 0;
3262   cfs->guarantee_more(8 * length, CHECK_0);  // 4-tuples of u2
3263   for (int n = 0; n < length; n++) {
3264     // Inner class index
3265     const u2 inner_class_info_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3266     check_property(
3267       valid_klass_reference_at(inner_class_info_index),
3268       "inner_class_info_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3269       inner_class_info_index, CHECK_0);
3270     // Outer class index
3271     const u2 outer_class_info_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3272     check_property(
3273       outer_class_info_index == 0 ||
3274         valid_klass_reference_at(outer_class_info_index),
3275       "outer_class_info_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3276       outer_class_info_index, CHECK_0);
3277     // Inner class name
3278     const u2 inner_name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3279     check_property(
3280       inner_name_index == 0 || valid_symbol_at(inner_name_index),
3281       "inner_name_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3282       inner_name_index, CHECK_0);
3283     if (_need_verify) {
3284       guarantee_property(inner_class_info_index != outer_class_info_index,
3285                          "Class is both outer and inner class in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3286     }
3287 
3288     jint recognized_modifiers = RECOGNIZED_INNER_CLASS_MODIFIERS;
3289     // JVM_ACC_MODULE is defined in JDK-9 and later.
3290     if (_major_version >= JAVA_9_VERSION) {
3291       recognized_modifiers |= JVM_ACC_MODULE;
3292     }
3293     // JVM_ACC_VALUE is defined for class file version 55 and later
3294     if (supports_value_types()) {
3295       recognized_modifiers |= JVM_ACC_VALUE;
3296     }
3297 
3298     // Access flags
3299     jint flags = cfs->get_u2_fast() & recognized_modifiers;
3300 
3301     if ((flags & JVM_ACC_INTERFACE) && _major_version < JAVA_6_VERSION) {
3302       // Set abstract bit for old class files for backward compatibility
3303       flags |= JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT;
3304     }
3305     verify_legal_class_modifiers(flags, CHECK_0);
3306     AccessFlags inner_access_flags(flags);
3307 
3308     inner_classes->at_put(index++, inner_class_info_index);
3309     inner_classes->at_put(index++, outer_class_info_index);
3310     inner_classes->at_put(index++, inner_name_index);
3311     inner_classes->at_put(index++, inner_access_flags.as_short());
3312   }
3313 
3314   // 4347400: make sure there's no duplicate entry in the classes array
3315   if (_need_verify && _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
3316     for(int i = 0; i < length * 4; i += 4) {
3317       for(int j = i + 4; j < length * 4; j += 4) {
3318         guarantee_property((inner_classes->at(i)   != inner_classes->at(j) ||
3319                             inner_classes->at(i+1) != inner_classes->at(j+1) ||
3320                             inner_classes->at(i+2) != inner_classes->at(j+2) ||
3321                             inner_classes->at(i+3) != inner_classes->at(j+3)),
3322                             "Duplicate entry in InnerClasses in class file %s",
3323                             CHECK_0);
3324       }
3325     }
3326   }
3327 
3328   // Set EnclosingMethod class and method indexes.
3329   if (parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute) {
3330     inner_classes->at_put(index++, enclosing_method_class_index);
3331     inner_classes->at_put(index++, enclosing_method_method_index);
3332   }
3333   assert(index == size, "wrong size");
3334 
3335   // Restore buffer's current position.
3336   cfs->set_current(current_mark);
3337 
3338   return length;
3339 }
3340 
3341 u2 ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_nest_members_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3342                                                            const u1* const nest_members_attribute_start,
3343                                                            TRAPS) {
3344   const u1* const current_mark = cfs->current();
3345   u2 length = 0;
3346   if (nest_members_attribute_start != NULL) {
3347     cfs->set_current(nest_members_attribute_start);
3348     cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_0);  // length
3349     length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3350   }
3351   const int size = length;
3352   Array<u2>* const nest_members = MetadataFactory::new_array<u2>(_loader_data, size, CHECK_0);
3353   _nest_members = nest_members;
3354 
3355   int index = 0;
3356   cfs->guarantee_more(2 * length, CHECK_0);
3357   for (int n = 0; n < length; n++) {
3358     const u2 class_info_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3359     check_property(
3360       valid_klass_reference_at(class_info_index),
3361       "Nest member class_info_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3362       class_info_index, CHECK_0);
3363     nest_members->at_put(index++, class_info_index);
3364   }
3365   assert(index == size, "wrong size");
3366 
3367   // Restore buffer's current position.
3368   cfs->set_current(current_mark);
3369 
3370   return length;
3371 }
3372 
3373 //  Record {
3374 //    u2 attribute_name_index;
3375 //    u4 attribute_length;
3376 //    u2 components_count;
3377 //    component_info components[components_count];
3378 //  }
3379 //  component_info {
3380 //    u2 name_index;
3381 //    u2 descriptor_index
3382 //    u2 attributes_count;
3383 //    attribute_info_attributes[attributes_count];
3384 //  }
3385 u2 ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_record_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3386                                                      const ConstantPool* cp,
3387                                                      const u1* const record_attribute_start,
3388                                                      TRAPS) {
3389   const u1* const current_mark = cfs->current();
3390   int components_count = 0;
3391   unsigned int calculate_attr_size = 0;
3392   if (record_attribute_start != NULL) {
3393     cfs->set_current(record_attribute_start);
3394     cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK_0);  // num of components
3395     components_count = (int)cfs->get_u2_fast();
3396     calculate_attr_size = 2;
3397   }
3398 
3399   Array<RecordComponent*>* const record_components =
3400     MetadataFactory::new_array<RecordComponent*>(_loader_data, components_count, NULL, CHECK_0);
3401   _record_components = record_components;
3402 
3403   for (int x = 0; x < components_count; x++) {
3404     cfs->guarantee_more(6, CHECK_0); // name_index, descriptor_index, attributes_count
3405 
3406     const u2 name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3407     check_property(valid_symbol_at(name_index),
3408       "Invalid constant pool index %u for name in Record attribute in class file %s",
3409       name_index, CHECK_0);
3410     const Symbol* const name = cp->symbol_at(name_index);
3411     verify_legal_field_name(name, CHECK_0);
3412 
3413     const u2 descriptor_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3414     check_property(valid_symbol_at(descriptor_index),
3415       "Invalid constant pool index %u for descriptor in Record attribute in class file %s",
3416       descriptor_index, CHECK_0);
3417     const Symbol* const descr = cp->symbol_at(descriptor_index);
3418     verify_legal_field_signature(name, descr, CHECK_0);
3419 
3420     const u2 attributes_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3421     calculate_attr_size += 6;
3422     u2 generic_sig_index = 0;
3423     const u1* runtime_visible_annotations = NULL;
3424     int runtime_visible_annotations_length = 0;
3425     const u1* runtime_invisible_annotations = NULL;
3426     int runtime_invisible_annotations_length = 0;
3427     bool runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = false;
3428     const u1* runtime_visible_type_annotations = NULL;
3429     int runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = 0;
3430     const u1* runtime_invisible_type_annotations = NULL;
3431     int runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = 0;
3432     bool runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = false;
3433 
3434     // Expected attributes for record components are Signature, Runtime(In)VisibleAnnotations,
3435     // and Runtime(In)VisibleTypeAnnotations.  Other attributes are ignored.
3436     for (int y = 0; y < attributes_count; y++) {
3437       cfs->guarantee_more(6, CHECK_0);  // attribute_name_index, attribute_length
3438       const u2 attribute_name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3439       const u4 attribute_length = cfs->get_u4_fast();
3440       calculate_attr_size += 6;
3441       check_property(
3442         valid_symbol_at(attribute_name_index),
3443         "Invalid Record attribute name index %u in class file %s",
3444         attribute_name_index, CHECK_0);
3445 
3446       const Symbol* const attribute_name = cp->symbol_at(attribute_name_index);
3447       if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_signature()) {
3448         if (generic_sig_index != 0) {
3449           classfile_parse_error(
3450             "Multiple Signature attributes for Record component in class file %s",
3451             CHECK_0);
3452         }
3453         if (attribute_length != 2) {
3454           classfile_parse_error(
3455             "Invalid Signature attribute length %u in Record component in class file %s",
3456             attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3457         }
3458         generic_sig_index = parse_generic_signature_attribute(cfs, CHECK_0);
3459 
3460       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_annotations()) {
3461         if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
3462           classfile_parse_error(
3463             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3464         }
3465         runtime_visible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3466         runtime_visible_annotations = cfs->current();
3467 
3468         assert(runtime_visible_annotations != NULL, "null record component visible annotation");
3469         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_annotations_length, CHECK_0);
3470         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_annotations_length);
3471 
3472       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_annotations()) {
3473         if (runtime_invisible_annotations_exists) {
3474           classfile_parse_error(
