3475             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3476         }
3477         runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = true;
3478         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3479           runtime_invisible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3480           runtime_invisible_annotations = cfs->current();
3481           assert(runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL, "null record component invisible annotation");
3482         }
3483         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3484 
3485       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_type_annotations()) {
3486         if (runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL) {
3487           classfile_parse_error(
3488             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleTypeAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3489         }
3490         runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3491         runtime_visible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3492 
3493         assert(runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL, "null record component visible type annotation");
3494         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length, CHECK_0);
3495         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length);
3496 
3497       } else if (attribute_name == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_type_annotations()) {
3498         if (runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists) {
3499           classfile_parse_error(
3500             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleTypeAnnotations attributes for Record component in class file %s", CHECK_0);
3501         }
3502         runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = true;
3503         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3504           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3505           runtime_invisible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3506           assert(runtime_invisible_type_annotations != NULL, "null record component invisible type annotation");
3507         }
3508         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3509 
3510       } else {
3511         // Skip unknown attributes
3512         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK_0);
3513       }
3514       calculate_attr_size += attribute_length;
3515     } // End of attributes For loop
3516 
3517     AnnotationArray* annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_annotations,
3518                                                         runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3519                                                         runtime_invisible_annotations,
3520                                                         runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
3521                                                         CHECK_0);
3522     AnnotationArray* type_annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_type_annotations,
3523                                                              runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
3524                                                              runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
3525                                                              runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
3526                                                              CHECK_0);
3527 
3528     RecordComponent* record_component =
3529       RecordComponent::allocate(_loader_data, name_index, descriptor_index,
3530                                 attributes_count, generic_sig_index,
3531                                 annotations, type_annotations, CHECK_0);
3532     record_components->at_put(x, record_component);
3533   }  // End of component processing loop
3534 
3535   // Restore buffer's current position.
3536   cfs->set_current(current_mark);
3537   return calculate_attr_size;
3538 }
3539 
3540 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_synthetic_attribute(TRAPS) {
3541   set_class_synthetic_flag(true);
3542 }
3543 
3544 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_signature_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs, TRAPS) {
3545   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3546 
3547   const u2 signature_index = cfs->get_u2(CHECK);
3548   check_property(
3549     valid_symbol_at(signature_index),
3550     "Invalid constant pool index %u in Signature attribute in class file %s",
3551     signature_index, CHECK);
3552   set_class_generic_signature_index(signature_index);
3553 }
3554 
3555 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_bootstrap_methods_attribute(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3556                                                                   ConstantPool* cp,
3557                                                                   u4 attribute_byte_length,
3558                                                                   TRAPS) {
3559   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3560   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
3561 
3562   const u1* const current_start = cfs->current();
3563 
3564   guarantee_property(attribute_byte_length >= sizeof(u2),
3565                      "Invalid BootstrapMethods attribute length %u in class file %s",
3566                      attribute_byte_length,
3567                      CHECK);
3568 
3569   cfs->guarantee_more(attribute_byte_length, CHECK);
3570 
3571   const int attribute_array_length = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3572 
3573   guarantee_property(_max_bootstrap_specifier_index < attribute_array_length,
3574                      "Short length on BootstrapMethods in class file %s",
3575                      CHECK);
3576 
3577 
3578   // The attribute contains a counted array of counted tuples of shorts,
3579   // represending bootstrap specifiers:
3580   //    length*{bootstrap_method_index, argument_count*{argument_index}}
3581   const int operand_count = (attribute_byte_length - sizeof(u2)) / sizeof(u2);
3582   // operand_count = number of shorts in attr, except for leading length
3583 
3584   // The attribute is copied into a short[] array.
3585   // The array begins with a series of short[2] pairs, one for each tuple.
3586   const int index_size = (attribute_array_length * 2);
3587 
3588   Array<u2>* const operands =
3589     MetadataFactory::new_array<u2>(_loader_data, index_size + operand_count, CHECK);
3590 
3591   // Eagerly assign operands so they will be deallocated with the constant
3592   // pool if there is an error.
3593   cp->set_operands(operands);
3594 
3595   int operand_fill_index = index_size;
3596   const int cp_size = cp->length();
3597 
3598   for (int n = 0; n < attribute_array_length; n++) {
3599     // Store a 32-bit offset into the header of the operand array.
3600     ConstantPool::operand_offset_at_put(operands, n, operand_fill_index);
3601 
3602     // Read a bootstrap specifier.
3603     cfs->guarantee_more(sizeof(u2) * 2, CHECK);  // bsm, argc
3604     const u2 bootstrap_method_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3605     const u2 argument_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3606     check_property(
3607       valid_cp_range(bootstrap_method_index, cp_size) &&
3608       cp->tag_at(bootstrap_method_index).is_method_handle(),
3609       "bootstrap_method_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3610       bootstrap_method_index,
3611       CHECK);
3612 
3613     guarantee_property((operand_fill_index + 1 + argument_count) < operands->length(),
3614       "Invalid BootstrapMethods num_bootstrap_methods or num_bootstrap_arguments value in class file %s",
3615       CHECK);
3616 
3617     operands->at_put(operand_fill_index++, bootstrap_method_index);
3618     operands->at_put(operand_fill_index++, argument_count);
3619 
3620     cfs->guarantee_more(sizeof(u2) * argument_count, CHECK);  // argv[argc]
3621     for (int j = 0; j < argument_count; j++) {
3622       const u2 argument_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3623       check_property(
3624         valid_cp_range(argument_index, cp_size) &&
3625         cp->tag_at(argument_index).is_loadable_constant(),
3626         "argument_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3627         argument_index,
3628         CHECK);
3629       operands->at_put(operand_fill_index++, argument_index);
3630     }
3631   }
3632   guarantee_property(current_start + attribute_byte_length == cfs->current(),
3633                      "Bad length on BootstrapMethods in class file %s",
3634                      CHECK);
3635 }
3636 
3637 bool ClassFileParser::supports_records() {
3638   return _major_version == JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION &&
3639     _minor_version == JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION &&
3640     Arguments::enable_preview();
3641 }
3642 
3643 void ClassFileParser::parse_classfile_attributes(const ClassFileStream* const cfs,
3644                                                  ConstantPool* cp,
3645                  ClassFileParser::ClassAnnotationCollector* parsed_annotations,
3646                                                  TRAPS) {
3647   assert(cfs != NULL, "invariant");
3648   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
3649   assert(parsed_annotations != NULL, "invariant");
3650 
3651   // Set inner classes attribute to default sentinel
3652   _inner_classes = Universe::the_empty_short_array();
3653   // Set nest members attribute to default sentinel
3654   _nest_members = Universe::the_empty_short_array();
3655   cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK);  // attributes_count
3656   u2 attributes_count = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3657   bool parsed_sourcefile_attribute = false;
3658   bool parsed_innerclasses_attribute = false;
3659   bool parsed_nest_members_attribute = false;
3660   bool parsed_nest_host_attribute = false;
3661   bool parsed_record_attribute = false;
3662   bool parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute = false;
3663   bool parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute = false;
3664   const u1* runtime_visible_annotations = NULL;
3665   int runtime_visible_annotations_length = 0;
3666   const u1* runtime_invisible_annotations = NULL;
3667   int runtime_invisible_annotations_length = 0;
3668   const u1* runtime_visible_type_annotations = NULL;
3669   int runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = 0;
3670   const u1* runtime_invisible_type_annotations = NULL;
3671   int runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = 0;
3672   bool runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = false;
3673   bool runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = false;
3674   bool parsed_source_debug_ext_annotations_exist = false;
3675   const u1* inner_classes_attribute_start = NULL;
3676   u4  inner_classes_attribute_length = 0;
3677   const u1* value_types_attribute_start = NULL;
3678   u4 value_types_attribute_length = 0;
3679   u2  enclosing_method_class_index = 0;
3680   u2  enclosing_method_method_index = 0;
3681   const u1* nest_members_attribute_start = NULL;
3682   u4  nest_members_attribute_length = 0;
3683   const u1* record_attribute_start = NULL;
3684   u4  record_attribute_length = 0;
3685 
3686   // Iterate over attributes
3687   while (attributes_count--) {
3688     cfs->guarantee_more(6, CHECK);  // attribute_name_index, attribute_length
3689     const u2 attribute_name_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3690     const u4 attribute_length = cfs->get_u4_fast();
3691     check_property(
3692       valid_symbol_at(attribute_name_index),
3693       "Attribute name has bad constant pool index %u in class file %s",
3694       attribute_name_index, CHECK);
3695     const Symbol* const tag = cp->symbol_at(attribute_name_index);
3696     if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_source_file()) {
3697       // Check for SourceFile tag
3698       if (_need_verify) {
3699         guarantee_property(attribute_length == 2, "Wrong SourceFile attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3700       }
3701       if (parsed_sourcefile_attribute) {
3702         classfile_parse_error("Multiple SourceFile attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3703       } else {
3704         parsed_sourcefile_attribute = true;
3705       }
3706       parse_classfile_sourcefile_attribute(cfs, CHECK);
3707     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_source_debug_extension()) {
3708       // Check for SourceDebugExtension tag
3709       if (parsed_source_debug_ext_annotations_exist) {
3710           classfile_parse_error(
3711             "Multiple SourceDebugExtension attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3712       }
3713       parsed_source_debug_ext_annotations_exist = true;
3714       parse_classfile_source_debug_extension_attribute(cfs, (int)attribute_length, CHECK);
3715     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_inner_classes()) {
3716       // Check for InnerClasses tag
3717       if (parsed_innerclasses_attribute) {
3718         classfile_parse_error("Multiple InnerClasses attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3719       } else {
3720         parsed_innerclasses_attribute = true;
3721       }
3722       inner_classes_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3723       inner_classes_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3724       cfs->skip_u1(inner_classes_attribute_length, CHECK);
3725     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_synthetic()) {
3726       // Check for Synthetic tag
3727       // Shouldn't we check that the synthetic flags wasn't already set? - not required in spec
3728       if (attribute_length != 0) {
3729         classfile_parse_error(
3730           "Invalid Synthetic classfile attribute length %u in class file %s",
3731           attribute_length, CHECK);
3732       }
3733       parse_classfile_synthetic_attribute(CHECK);
3734     } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_deprecated()) {
3735       // Check for Deprecatd tag - 4276120
3736       if (attribute_length != 0) {
3737         classfile_parse_error(
3738           "Invalid Deprecated classfile attribute length %u in class file %s",
3739           attribute_length, CHECK);
3740       }
3741     } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
3742       if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_signature()) {
3743         if (_generic_signature_index != 0) {
3744           classfile_parse_error(
3745             "Multiple Signature attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3746         }
3747         if (attribute_length != 2) {
3748           classfile_parse_error(
3749             "Wrong Signature attribute length %u in class file %s",
3750             attribute_length, CHECK);
3751         }
3752         parse_classfile_signature_attribute(cfs, CHECK);
3753       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_annotations()) {
3754         if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
3755           classfile_parse_error(
3756             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3757         }
3758         runtime_visible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3759         runtime_visible_annotations = cfs->current();
3760         assert(runtime_visible_annotations != NULL, "null visible annotations");
3761         cfs->guarantee_more(runtime_visible_annotations_length, CHECK);
3762         parse_annotations(cp,
3763                           runtime_visible_annotations,
3764                           runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3765                           parsed_annotations,
3766                           _loader_data,
3767                           CHECK);
3768         cfs->skip_u1_fast(runtime_visible_annotations_length);
3769       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_annotations()) {
3770         if (runtime_invisible_annotations_exists) {
3771           classfile_parse_error(
3772             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3773         }
3774         runtime_invisible_annotations_exists = true;
3775         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3776           runtime_invisible_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3777           runtime_invisible_annotations = cfs->current();
3778           assert(runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL, "null invisible annotations");
3779         }
3780         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3781       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_enclosing_method()) {
3782         if (parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute) {
3783           classfile_parse_error("Multiple EnclosingMethod attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3784         } else {
3785           parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute = true;
3786         }
3787         guarantee_property(attribute_length == 4,
3788           "Wrong EnclosingMethod attribute length %u in class file %s",
3789           attribute_length, CHECK);
3790         cfs->guarantee_more(4, CHECK);  // class_index, method_index
3791         enclosing_method_class_index  = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3792         enclosing_method_method_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3793         if (enclosing_method_class_index == 0) {
3794           classfile_parse_error("Invalid class index in EnclosingMethod attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3795         }
3796         // Validate the constant pool indices and types
3797         check_property(valid_klass_reference_at(enclosing_method_class_index),
3798           "Invalid or out-of-bounds class index in EnclosingMethod attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3799         if (enclosing_method_method_index != 0 &&
3800             (!cp->is_within_bounds(enclosing_method_method_index) ||
3801              !cp->tag_at(enclosing_method_method_index).is_name_and_type())) {
3802           classfile_parse_error("Invalid or out-of-bounds method index in EnclosingMethod attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3803         }
3804       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_bootstrap_methods() &&
3805                  _major_version >= Verifier::INVOKEDYNAMIC_MAJOR_VERSION) {
3806         if (parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute) {
3807           classfile_parse_error("Multiple BootstrapMethods attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3808         }
3809         parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute = true;
3810         parse_classfile_bootstrap_methods_attribute(cfs, cp, attribute_length, CHECK);
3811       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_visible_type_annotations()) {
3812         if (runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL) {
3813           classfile_parse_error(
3814             "Multiple RuntimeVisibleTypeAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3815         }
3816         runtime_visible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3817         runtime_visible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3818         assert(runtime_visible_type_annotations != NULL, "null visible type annotations");
3819         // No need for the VM to parse Type annotations
3820         cfs->skip_u1(runtime_visible_type_annotations_length, CHECK);
3821       } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_runtime_invisible_type_annotations()) {
3822         if (runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists) {
3823           classfile_parse_error(
3824             "Multiple RuntimeInvisibleTypeAnnotations attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3825         } else {
3826           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_exists = true;
3827         }
3828         if (PreserveAllAnnotations) {
3829           runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length = attribute_length;
3830           runtime_invisible_type_annotations = cfs->current();
3831           assert(runtime_invisible_type_annotations != NULL, "null invisible type annotations");
3832         }
3833         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3834       } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_11_VERSION) {
3835         if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_nest_members()) {
3836           // Check for NestMembers tag
3837           if (parsed_nest_members_attribute) {
3838             classfile_parse_error("Multiple NestMembers attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3839           } else {
3840             parsed_nest_members_attribute = true;
3841           }
3842           if (parsed_nest_host_attribute) {
3843             classfile_parse_error("Conflicting NestHost and NestMembers attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3844           }
3845           nest_members_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3846           nest_members_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3847           cfs->skip_u1(nest_members_attribute_length, CHECK);
3848         } else if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_nest_host()) {
3849           if (parsed_nest_host_attribute) {
3850             classfile_parse_error("Multiple NestHost attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3851           } else {
3852             parsed_nest_host_attribute = true;
3853           }
3854           if (parsed_nest_members_attribute) {
3855             classfile_parse_error("Conflicting NestMembers and NestHost attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3856           }
3857           if (_need_verify) {
3858             guarantee_property(attribute_length == 2, "Wrong NestHost attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3859           }
3860           cfs->guarantee_more(2, CHECK);
3861           u2 class_info_index = cfs->get_u2_fast();
3862           check_property(
3863                          valid_klass_reference_at(class_info_index),
3864                          "Nest-host class_info_index %u has bad constant type in class file %s",
3865                          class_info_index, CHECK);
3866           _nest_host = class_info_index;
3867         } else if (_major_version >= JAVA_14_VERSION) {
3868           if (tag == vmSymbols::tag_record()) {
3869             // Skip over Record attribute if not supported or if super class is
3870             // not java.lang.Record.
3871             if (supports_records() &&
3872                 cp->klass_name_at(_super_class_index) == vmSymbols::java_lang_Record()) {
3873               if (parsed_record_attribute) {
3874                 classfile_parse_error("Multiple Record attributes in class file %s", CHECK);
3875               }
3876               // Check that class is final and not abstract.
3877               if (!_access_flags.is_final() || _access_flags.is_abstract()) {
3878                 classfile_parse_error("Record attribute in non-final or abstract class file %s", CHECK);
3879               }
3880               parsed_record_attribute = true;
3881               record_attribute_start = cfs->current();
3882               record_attribute_length = attribute_length;
3883             } else if (log_is_enabled(Info, class, record)) {
3884               // Log why the Record attribute was ignored.  Note that if the
3885               // class file version is JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION.65535 and
3886               // --enable-preview wasn't specified then a java.lang.UnsupportedClassVersionError
3887               // exception would have been thrown.
3888               ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
3889               if (supports_records()) {
3890                 log_info(class, record)(
3891                   "Ignoring Record attribute in class %s because super type is not java.lang.Record",
3892                   _class_name->as_C_string());
3893               } else {
3894                 log_info(class, record)(
3895                   "Ignoring Record attribute in class %s because class file version is not %d.65535",
3896                    _class_name->as_C_string(), JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION);
3897               }
3898             }
3899             cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3900           } else {
3901             // Unknown attribute
3902             cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3903           }
3904         } else {
3905           // Unknown attribute
3906           cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3907         }
3908       } else {
3909         // Unknown attribute
3910         cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3911       }
3912     } else {
3913       // Unknown attribute
3914       cfs->skip_u1(attribute_length, CHECK);
3915     }
3916   }
3917   _class_annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_annotations,
3918                                             runtime_visible_annotations_length,
3919                                             runtime_invisible_annotations,
3920                                             runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
3921                                             CHECK);
3922   _class_type_annotations = assemble_annotations(runtime_visible_type_annotations,
3923                                                  runtime_visible_type_annotations_length,
3924                                                  runtime_invisible_type_annotations,
3925                                                  runtime_invisible_type_annotations_length,
3926                                                  CHECK);
3927 
3928   if (parsed_innerclasses_attribute || parsed_enclosingmethod_attribute) {
3929     const u2 num_of_classes = parse_classfile_inner_classes_attribute(
3930                             cfs,
3931                             inner_classes_attribute_start,
3932                             parsed_innerclasses_attribute,
3933                             enclosing_method_class_index,
3934                             enclosing_method_method_index,
3935                             CHECK);
3936     if (parsed_innerclasses_attribute && _need_verify && _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
3937       guarantee_property(
3938         inner_classes_attribute_length == sizeof(num_of_classes) + 4 * sizeof(u2) * num_of_classes,
3939         "Wrong InnerClasses attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3940     }
3941   }
3942 
3943   if (parsed_nest_members_attribute) {
3944     const u2 num_of_classes = parse_classfile_nest_members_attribute(
3945                             cfs,
3946                             nest_members_attribute_start,
3947                             CHECK);
3948     if (_need_verify) {
3949       guarantee_property(
3950         nest_members_attribute_length == sizeof(num_of_classes) + sizeof(u2) * num_of_classes,
3951         "Wrong NestMembers attribute length in class file %s", CHECK);
3952     }
3953   }
3954 
3955   if (parsed_record_attribute) {
3956     const unsigned int calculated_attr_length = parse_classfile_record_attribute(
3957                             cfs,
3958                             cp,
3959                             record_attribute_start,
3960                             CHECK);
3961     if (_need_verify) {
3962       guarantee_property(record_attribute_length == calculated_attr_length,
3963                          "Record attribute has wrong length in class file %s",
3964                          CHECK);
3965     }
3966   }
3967 
3968   if (_max_bootstrap_specifier_index >= 0) {
3969     guarantee_property(parsed_bootstrap_methods_attribute,
3970                        "Missing BootstrapMethods attribute in class file %s", CHECK);
3971   }
3972 }
3973 
3974 void ClassFileParser::apply_parsed_class_attributes(InstanceKlass* k) {
3975   assert(k != NULL, "invariant");
3976 
3977   if (_synthetic_flag)
3978     k->set_is_synthetic();
3979   if (_sourcefile_index != 0) {
3980     k->set_source_file_name_index(_sourcefile_index);
3981   }
3982   if (_generic_signature_index != 0) {
3983     k->set_generic_signature_index(_generic_signature_index);
3984   }
3985   if (_sde_buffer != NULL) {
3986     k->set_source_debug_extension(_sde_buffer, _sde_length);
3987   }
3988 }
3989 
3990 // Create the Annotations object that will
3991 // hold the annotations array for the Klass.
3992 void ClassFileParser::create_combined_annotations(TRAPS) {
3993     if (_class_annotations == NULL &&
3994         _class_type_annotations == NULL &&
3995         _fields_annotations == NULL &&
3996         _fields_type_annotations == NULL) {
3997       // Don't create the Annotations object unnecessarily.
3998       return;
3999     }
4000 
4001     Annotations* const annotations = Annotations::allocate(_loader_data, CHECK);
4002     annotations->set_class_annotations(_class_annotations);
4003     annotations->set_class_type_annotations(_class_type_annotations);
4004     annotations->set_fields_annotations(_fields_annotations);
4005     annotations->set_fields_type_annotations(_fields_type_annotations);
4006 
4007     // This is the Annotations object that will be
4008     // assigned to InstanceKlass being constructed.
4009     _combined_annotations = annotations;
4010 
4011     // The annotations arrays below has been transfered the
4012     // _combined_annotations so these fields can now be cleared.
4013     _class_annotations       = NULL;
4014     _class_type_annotations  = NULL;
4015     _fields_annotations      = NULL;
4016     _fields_type_annotations = NULL;
4017 }
4018 
4019 // Transfer ownership of metadata allocated to the InstanceKlass.
4020 void ClassFileParser::apply_parsed_class_metadata(
4021                                             InstanceKlass* this_klass,
4022                                             int java_fields_count,
4023                                             TRAPS) {
4024   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
4025 
4026   _cp->set_pool_holder(this_klass);
4027   this_klass->set_constants(_cp);
4028   this_klass->set_fields(_fields, java_fields_count);
4029   this_klass->set_methods(_methods);
4030   this_klass->set_inner_classes(_inner_classes);
4031   this_klass->set_nest_members(_nest_members);
4032   this_klass->set_nest_host_index(_nest_host);
4033   this_klass->set_local_interfaces(_local_interfaces);
4034   this_klass->set_annotations(_combined_annotations);
4035   this_klass->set_record_components(_record_components);
4036   // Delay the setting of _transitive_interfaces until after initialize_supers() in
4037   // fill_instance_klass(). It is because the _transitive_interfaces may be shared with
4038   // its _super. If an OOM occurs while loading the current klass, its _super field
4039   // may not have been set. When GC tries to free the klass, the _transitive_interfaces
4040   // may be deallocated mistakenly in InstanceKlass::deallocate_interfaces(). Subsequent
4041   // dereferences to the deallocated _transitive_interfaces will result in a crash.
4042 
4043   // Clear out these fields so they don't get deallocated by the destructor
4044   clear_class_metadata();
4045 }
4046 
4047 AnnotationArray* ClassFileParser::assemble_annotations(const u1* const runtime_visible_annotations,
4048                                                        int runtime_visible_annotations_length,
4049                                                        const u1* const runtime_invisible_annotations,
4050                                                        int runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
4051                                                        TRAPS) {
4052   AnnotationArray* annotations = NULL;
4053   if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL ||
4054       runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL) {
4055     annotations = MetadataFactory::new_array<u1>(_loader_data,
4056                                           runtime_visible_annotations_length +
4057                                           runtime_invisible_annotations_length,
4058                                           CHECK_(annotations));
4059     if (runtime_visible_annotations != NULL) {
4060       for (int i = 0; i < runtime_visible_annotations_length; i++) {
4061         annotations->at_put(i, runtime_visible_annotations[i]);
4062       }
4063     }
4064     if (runtime_invisible_annotations != NULL) {
4065       for (int i = 0; i < runtime_invisible_annotations_length; i++) {
4066         int append = runtime_visible_annotations_length+i;
4067         annotations->at_put(append, runtime_invisible_annotations[i]);
4068       }
4069     }
4070   }
4071   return annotations;
4072 }
4073 
4074 const InstanceKlass* ClassFileParser::parse_super_class(ConstantPool* const cp,
4075                                                         const int super_class_index,
4076                                                         const bool need_verify,
4077                                                         TRAPS) {
4078   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
4079   const InstanceKlass* super_klass = NULL;
4080 
4081   if (super_class_index == 0) {
4082     check_property(_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object()
4083                    || (_access_flags.get_flags() & JVM_ACC_VALUE),
4084                    "Invalid superclass index %u in class file %s",
4085                    super_class_index,
4086                    CHECK_NULL);
4087   } else {
4088     check_property(valid_klass_reference_at(super_class_index),
4089                    "Invalid superclass index %u in class file %s",
4090                    super_class_index,
4091                    CHECK_NULL);
4092     // The class name should be legal because it is checked when parsing constant pool.
4093     // However, make sure it is not an array type.
4094     bool is_array = false;
4095     if (cp->tag_at(super_class_index).is_klass()) {
4096       super_klass = InstanceKlass::cast(cp->resolved_klass_at(super_class_index));
4097       if (need_verify)
4098         is_array = super_klass->is_array_klass();
4099     } else if (need_verify) {
4100       is_array = (cp->klass_name_at(super_class_index)->char_at(0) == JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY);
4101     }
4102     if (need_verify) {
4103       guarantee_property(!is_array,
4104                         "Bad superclass name in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
4105     }
4106   }
4107   return super_klass;
4108 }
4109 
4110 #ifndef PRODUCT
4111 static void print_field_layout(const Symbol* name,
4112                                Array<u2>* fields,
4113                                ConstantPool* cp,
4114                                int instance_size,
4115                                int instance_fields_start,
4116                                int instance_fields_end,
4117                                int static_fields_end) {
4118 
4119   assert(name != NULL, "invariant");
4120 
4121   tty->print("%s: field layout\n", name->as_klass_external_name());
4122   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", instance_fields_start, "--- instance fields start ---");
4123   for (AllFieldStream fs(fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4124     if (!fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
4125       tty->print("  @%3d \"%s\" %s\n",
4126         fs.offset(),
4127         fs.name()->as_klass_external_name(),
4128         fs.signature()->as_klass_external_name());
4129     }
4130   }
4131   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", instance_fields_end, "--- instance fields end ---");
4132   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", instance_size * wordSize, "--- instance ends ---");
4133   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", InstanceMirrorKlass::offset_of_static_fields(), "--- static fields start ---");
4134   for (AllFieldStream fs(fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4135     if (fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
4136       tty->print("  @%3d \"%s\" %s\n",
4137         fs.offset(),
4138         fs.name()->as_klass_external_name(),
4139         fs.signature()->as_klass_external_name());
4140     }
4141   }
4142   tty->print("  @%3d %s\n", static_fields_end, "--- static fields end ---");
4143   tty->print("\n");
4144 }
4145 #endif
4146 
4147 OopMapBlocksBuilder::OopMapBlocksBuilder(unsigned int max_blocks) {
4148   _max_nonstatic_oop_maps = max_blocks;
4149   _nonstatic_oop_map_count = 0;
4150   if (max_blocks == 0) {
4151     _nonstatic_oop_maps = NULL;
4152   } else {
4153     _nonstatic_oop_maps =
4154         NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(OopMapBlock, _max_nonstatic_oop_maps);
4155     memset(_nonstatic_oop_maps, 0, sizeof(OopMapBlock) * max_blocks);
4156   }
4157 }
4158 
4159 OopMapBlock* OopMapBlocksBuilder::last_oop_map() const {
4160   assert(_nonstatic_oop_map_count > 0, "Has no oop maps");
4161   return _nonstatic_oop_maps + (_nonstatic_oop_map_count - 1);
4162 }
4163 
4164 // addition of super oop maps
4165 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::initialize_inherited_blocks(OopMapBlock* blocks, unsigned int nof_blocks) {
4166   assert(nof_blocks && _nonstatic_oop_map_count == 0 &&
4167          nof_blocks <= _max_nonstatic_oop_maps, "invariant");
4168 
4169   memcpy(_nonstatic_oop_maps, blocks, sizeof(OopMapBlock) * nof_blocks);
4170   _nonstatic_oop_map_count += nof_blocks;
4171 }
4172 
4173 // collection of oops
4174 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::add(int offset, int count) {
4175   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count == 0) {
4176     _nonstatic_oop_map_count++;
4177   }
4178   OopMapBlock* nonstatic_oop_map = last_oop_map();
4179   if (nonstatic_oop_map->count() == 0) {  // Unused map, set it up
4180     nonstatic_oop_map->set_offset(offset);
4181     nonstatic_oop_map->set_count(count);
4182   } else if (nonstatic_oop_map->is_contiguous(offset)) { // contiguous, add
4183     nonstatic_oop_map->increment_count(count);
4184   } else { // Need a new one...
4185     _nonstatic_oop_map_count++;
4186     assert(_nonstatic_oop_map_count <= _max_nonstatic_oop_maps, "range check");
4187     nonstatic_oop_map = last_oop_map();
4188     nonstatic_oop_map->set_offset(offset);
4189     nonstatic_oop_map->set_count(count);
4190   }
4191 }
4192 
4193 // general purpose copy, e.g. into allocated instanceKlass
4194 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::copy(OopMapBlock* dst) {
4195   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count != 0) {
4196     memcpy(dst, _nonstatic_oop_maps, sizeof(OopMapBlock) * _nonstatic_oop_map_count);
4197   }
4198 }
4199 
4200 // Sort and compact adjacent blocks
4201 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::compact() {
4202   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count <= 1) {
4203     return;
4204   }
4205   /*
4206    * Since field layout sneeks in oops before values, we will be able to condense
4207    * blocks. There is potential to compact between super, own refs and values
4208    * containing refs.
4209    *
4210    * Currently compaction is slightly limited due to values being 8 byte aligned.
4211    * This may well change: FixMe if it doesn't, the code below is fairly general purpose
4212    * and maybe it doesn't need to be.
4213    */
4214   qsort(_nonstatic_oop_maps, _nonstatic_oop_map_count, sizeof(OopMapBlock),
4215         (_sort_Fn)OopMapBlock::compare_offset);
4216   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count < 2) {
4217     return;
4218   }
4219 
4220   // Make a temp copy, and iterate through and copy back into the original
4221   ResourceMark rm;
4222   OopMapBlock* oop_maps_copy =
4223       NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(OopMapBlock, _nonstatic_oop_map_count);
4224   OopMapBlock* oop_maps_copy_end = oop_maps_copy + _nonstatic_oop_map_count;
4225   copy(oop_maps_copy);
4226   OopMapBlock* nonstatic_oop_map = _nonstatic_oop_maps;
4227   unsigned int new_count = 1;
4228   oop_maps_copy++;
4229   while(oop_maps_copy < oop_maps_copy_end) {
4230     assert(nonstatic_oop_map->offset() < oop_maps_copy->offset(), "invariant");
4231     if (nonstatic_oop_map->is_contiguous(oop_maps_copy->offset())) {
4232       nonstatic_oop_map->increment_count(oop_maps_copy->count());
4233     } else {
4234       nonstatic_oop_map++;
4235       new_count++;
4236       nonstatic_oop_map->set_offset(oop_maps_copy->offset());
4237       nonstatic_oop_map->set_count(oop_maps_copy->count());
4238     }
4239     oop_maps_copy++;
4240   }
4241   assert(new_count <= _nonstatic_oop_map_count, "end up with more maps after compact() ?");
4242   _nonstatic_oop_map_count = new_count;
4243 }
4244 
4245 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::print_on(outputStream* st) const {
4246   st->print_cr("  OopMapBlocks: %3d  /%3d", _nonstatic_oop_map_count, _max_nonstatic_oop_maps);
4247   if (_nonstatic_oop_map_count > 0) {
4248     OopMapBlock* map = _nonstatic_oop_maps;
4249     OopMapBlock* last_map = last_oop_map();
4250     assert(map <= last_map, "Last less than first");
4251     while (map <= last_map) {
4252       st->print_cr("    Offset: %3d  -%3d Count: %3d", map->offset(),
4253                    map->offset() + map->offset_span() - heapOopSize, map->count());
4254       map++;
4255     }
4256   }
4257 }
4258 
4259 void OopMapBlocksBuilder::print_value_on(outputStream* st) const {
4260   print_on(st);
4261 }
4262 
4263 void ClassFileParser::throwValueTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION_DECL,
4264                                                const char* msg,
4265                                                const Symbol* name,
4266                                                const Symbol* sig) const {
4267 
4268   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
4269   if (name == NULL || sig == NULL) {
4270     Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION_ARGS,
4271         vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
4272         "class: %s - %s", _class_name->as_C_string(), msg);
4273   }
4274   else {
4275     Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION_ARGS,
4276         vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
4277         "\"%s\" sig: \"%s\" class: %s - %s", name->as_C_string(), sig->as_C_string(),
4278         _class_name->as_C_string(), msg);
4279   }
4280 }
4281 
4282 // Layout fields and fill in FieldLayoutInfo.  Could use more refactoring!
4283 void ClassFileParser::layout_fields(ConstantPool* cp,
4284                                     const FieldAllocationCount* fac,
4285                                     const ClassAnnotationCollector* parsed_annotations,
4286                                     FieldLayoutInfo* info,
4287                                     TRAPS) {
4288 
4289   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
4290 
4291   // Field size and offset computation
4292   int nonstatic_field_size = _super_klass == NULL ? 0 :
4293                                _super_klass->nonstatic_field_size();
4294   int next_nonstatic_valuetype_offset = 0;
4295   int first_nonstatic_valuetype_offset = 0;
4296 
4297   // Fields that are value types are handled differently depending if they are static or not:
4298   // - static fields are oops
4299   // - non-static fields are embedded
4300 
4301   // Count the contended fields by type.
4302   //
4303   // We ignore static fields, because @Contended is not supported for them.
4304   // The layout code below will also ignore the static fields.
4305   int nonstatic_contended_count = 0;
4306   FieldAllocationCount fac_contended;
4307   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4308     FieldAllocationType atype = (FieldAllocationType) fs.allocation_type();
4309     if (fs.is_contended()) {
4310       fac_contended.count[atype]++;
4311       if (!fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
4312         nonstatic_contended_count++;
4313       }
4314     }
4315   }
4316 
4317 
4318   // Calculate the starting byte offsets
4319   int next_static_oop_offset    = InstanceMirrorKlass::offset_of_static_fields();
4320   // Value types in static fields are not embedded, they are handled with oops
4321   int next_static_double_offset = next_static_oop_offset +
4322                                   ((fac->count[STATIC_OOP] + fac->count[STATIC_FLATTENABLE]) * heapOopSize);
4323   if (fac->count[STATIC_DOUBLE]) {
4324     next_static_double_offset = align_up(next_static_double_offset, BytesPerLong);
4325   }
4326 
4327   int next_static_word_offset   = next_static_double_offset +
4328                                     ((fac->count[STATIC_DOUBLE]) * BytesPerLong);
4329   int next_static_short_offset  = next_static_word_offset +
4330                                     ((fac->count[STATIC_WORD]) * BytesPerInt);
4331   int next_static_byte_offset   = next_static_short_offset +
4332                                   ((fac->count[STATIC_SHORT]) * BytesPerShort);
4333 
4334   int nonstatic_fields_start  = instanceOopDesc::base_offset_in_bytes() +
4335                                 nonstatic_field_size * heapOopSize;
4336 
4337   // First field of value types is aligned on a long boundary in order to ease
4338   // in-lining of value types (with header removal) in packed arrays and
4339   // flatten value types
4340   int initial_value_type_padding = 0;
4341   if (is_value_type()) {
4342     int old = nonstatic_fields_start;
4343     nonstatic_fields_start = align_up(nonstatic_fields_start, BytesPerLong);
4344     initial_value_type_padding = nonstatic_fields_start - old;
4345   }
4346 
4347   int next_nonstatic_field_offset = nonstatic_fields_start;
4348 
4349   const bool is_contended_class     = parsed_annotations->is_contended();
4350 
4351   // Class is contended, pad before all the fields
4352   if (is_contended_class) {
4353     next_nonstatic_field_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4354   }
4355 
4356   // Temporary value types restrictions
4357   if (is_value_type()) {
4358     if (is_contended_class) {
4359       throwValueTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION, "Inline Types do not support @Contended annotation yet");
4360       return;
4361     }
4362   }
4363 
4364   // Compute the non-contended fields count.
4365   // The packing code below relies on these counts to determine if some field
4366   // can be squeezed into the alignment gap. Contended fields are obviously
4367   // exempt from that.
4368   unsigned int nonstatic_double_count = fac->count[NONSTATIC_DOUBLE] - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_DOUBLE];
4369   unsigned int nonstatic_word_count   = fac->count[NONSTATIC_WORD]   - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_WORD];
4370   unsigned int nonstatic_short_count  = fac->count[NONSTATIC_SHORT]  - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_SHORT];
4371   unsigned int nonstatic_byte_count   = fac->count[NONSTATIC_BYTE]   - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_BYTE];
4372   unsigned int nonstatic_oop_count    = fac->count[NONSTATIC_OOP]    - fac_contended.count[NONSTATIC_OOP];
4373 
4374   int static_value_type_count = 0;
4375   int nonstatic_value_type_count = 0;
4376   int* nonstatic_value_type_indexes = NULL;
4377   Klass** nonstatic_value_type_klasses = NULL;
4378   unsigned int value_type_oop_map_count = 0;
4379   int not_flattened_value_types = 0;
4380   int not_atomic_value_types = 0;
4381 
4382   int max_nonstatic_value_type = fac->count[NONSTATIC_FLATTENABLE] + 1;
4383 
4384   nonstatic_value_type_indexes = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(THREAD, int,
4385                                                               max_nonstatic_value_type);
4386   for (int i = 0; i < max_nonstatic_value_type; i++) {
4387     nonstatic_value_type_indexes[i] = -1;
4388   }
4389   nonstatic_value_type_klasses = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY_IN_THREAD(THREAD, Klass*,
4390                                                               max_nonstatic_value_type);
4391 
4392   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, _cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4393     if (fs.allocation_type() == STATIC_FLATTENABLE) {
4394       ResourceMark rm;
4395       if (!fs.signature()->is_Q_signature()) {
4396         THROW(vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError());
4397       }
4398       static_value_type_count++;
4399     } else if (fs.allocation_type() == NONSTATIC_FLATTENABLE) {
4400       // Pre-resolve the flattenable field and check for value type circularity issues.
4401       ResourceMark rm;
4402       if (!fs.signature()->is_Q_signature()) {
4403         THROW(vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError());
4404       }
4405       Klass* klass =
4406         SystemDictionary::resolve_flattenable_field_or_fail(&fs,
4407                                                             Handle(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader()),
4408                                                             _protection_domain, true, CHECK);
4409       assert(klass != NULL, "Sanity check");
4410       if (!klass->access_flags().is_value_type()) {
4411         THROW(vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError());
4412       }
4413       ValueKlass* vk = ValueKlass::cast(klass);
4414       // Conditions to apply flattening or not should be defined in a single place
4415       bool too_big_to_flatten = (ValueFieldMaxFlatSize >= 0 &&
4416                                  (vk->size_helper() * HeapWordSize) > ValueFieldMaxFlatSize);
4417       bool too_atomic_to_flatten = vk->is_declared_atomic();
4418       bool too_volatile_to_flatten = fs.access_flags().is_volatile();
4419       if (vk->is_naturally_atomic()) {
4420         too_atomic_to_flatten = false;
4421         //too_volatile_to_flatten = false; //FIXME
4422         // volatile fields are currently never flattened, this could change in the future
4423       }
4424       if (!(too_big_to_flatten | too_atomic_to_flatten | too_volatile_to_flatten)) {
4425         nonstatic_value_type_indexes[nonstatic_value_type_count] = fs.index();
4426         nonstatic_value_type_klasses[nonstatic_value_type_count] = klass;
4427         nonstatic_value_type_count++;
4428 
4429         ValueKlass* vklass = ValueKlass::cast(klass);
4430         if (vklass->contains_oops()) {
4431           value_type_oop_map_count += vklass->nonstatic_oop_map_count();
4432         }
4433         fs.set_flattened(true);
4434         if (!vk->is_atomic()) {  // flat and non-atomic: take note
4435           not_atomic_value_types++;
4436         }
4437       } else {
4438         not_flattened_value_types++;
4439         fs.set_flattened(false);
4440       }
4441     }
4442   }
4443 
4444   // Adjusting non_static_oop_count to take into account not flattened value types;
4445   nonstatic_oop_count += not_flattened_value_types;
4446 
4447   // Total non-static fields count, including every contended field
4448   unsigned int nonstatic_fields_count = fac->count[NONSTATIC_DOUBLE] + fac->count[NONSTATIC_WORD] +
4449                                         fac->count[NONSTATIC_SHORT] + fac->count[NONSTATIC_BYTE] +
4450                                         fac->count[NONSTATIC_OOP] + fac->count[NONSTATIC_FLATTENABLE];
4451 
4452   const bool super_has_nonstatic_fields =
4453           (_super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->has_nonstatic_fields());
4454   const bool has_nonstatic_fields =
4455     super_has_nonstatic_fields || (nonstatic_fields_count != 0);
4456   const bool has_nonstatic_value_fields = nonstatic_value_type_count > 0;
4457 
4458   if (is_value_type() && (!has_nonstatic_fields)) {
4459     // There are a number of fixes required throughout the type system and JIT
4460     throwValueTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION, "Inline Types do not support zero instance size yet");
4461     return;
4462   }
4463 
4464   // Prepare list of oops for oop map generation.
4465   //
4466   // "offset" and "count" lists are describing the set of contiguous oop
4467   // regions. offset[i] is the start of the i-th region, which then has
4468   // count[i] oops following. Before we know how many regions are required,
4469   // we pessimistically allocate the maps to fit all the oops into the
4470   // distinct regions.
4471   //
4472   int super_oop_map_count = (_super_klass == NULL) ? 0 :_super_klass->nonstatic_oop_map_count();
4473   int max_oop_map_count =
4474       super_oop_map_count +
4475       fac->count[NONSTATIC_OOP] +
4476       value_type_oop_map_count +
4477       not_flattened_value_types;
4478 
4479   OopMapBlocksBuilder* nonstatic_oop_maps = new OopMapBlocksBuilder(max_oop_map_count);
4480   if (super_oop_map_count > 0) {
4481     nonstatic_oop_maps->initialize_inherited_blocks(_super_klass->start_of_nonstatic_oop_maps(),
4482                                                     _super_klass->nonstatic_oop_map_count());
4483   }
4484 
4485   int first_nonstatic_oop_offset = 0; // will be set for first oop field
4486 
4487   bool compact_fields  = true;
4488   bool allocate_oops_first = false;
4489 
4490   // The next classes have predefined hard-coded fields offsets
4491   // (see in JavaClasses::compute_hard_coded_offsets()).
4492   // Use default fields allocation order for them.
4493   if (_loader_data->class_loader() == NULL &&
4494       (_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_ref_Reference() ||
4495        _class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Boolean() ||
4496        _class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Character() ||
4497        _class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Float() ||
4498        _class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Double() ||
4499        _class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Byte() ||
4500        _class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Short() ||
4501        _class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Integer() ||
4502        _class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Long())) {
4503     allocate_oops_first = true;     // Allocate oops first
4504     compact_fields   = false; // Don't compact fields
4505   }
4506 
4507   int next_nonstatic_oop_offset = 0;
4508   int next_nonstatic_double_offset = 0;
4509 
4510   // Rearrange fields for a given allocation style
4511   if (allocate_oops_first) {
4512     // Fields order: oops, longs/doubles, ints, shorts/chars, bytes, padded fields
4513     next_nonstatic_oop_offset    = next_nonstatic_field_offset;
4514     next_nonstatic_double_offset = next_nonstatic_oop_offset +
4515                                     (nonstatic_oop_count * heapOopSize);
4516   } else {
4517     // Fields order: longs/doubles, ints, shorts/chars, bytes, oops, padded fields
4518     next_nonstatic_double_offset = next_nonstatic_field_offset;
4519   }
4520 
4521   int nonstatic_oop_space_count   = 0;
4522   int nonstatic_word_space_count  = 0;
4523   int nonstatic_short_space_count = 0;
4524   int nonstatic_byte_space_count  = 0;
4525   int nonstatic_oop_space_offset = 0;
4526   int nonstatic_word_space_offset = 0;
4527   int nonstatic_short_space_offset = 0;
4528   int nonstatic_byte_space_offset = 0;
4529 
4530   // Try to squeeze some of the fields into the gaps due to
4531   // long/double alignment.
4532   if (nonstatic_double_count > 0) {
4533     int offset = next_nonstatic_double_offset;
4534     next_nonstatic_double_offset = align_up(offset, BytesPerLong);
4535     if (compact_fields && offset != next_nonstatic_double_offset) {
4536       // Allocate available fields into the gap before double field.
4537       int length = next_nonstatic_double_offset - offset;
4538       assert(length == BytesPerInt, "");
4539       nonstatic_word_space_offset = offset;
4540       if (nonstatic_word_count > 0) {
4541         nonstatic_word_count      -= 1;
4542         nonstatic_word_space_count = 1; // Only one will fit
4543         length -= BytesPerInt;
4544         offset += BytesPerInt;
4545       }
4546       nonstatic_short_space_offset = offset;
4547       while (length >= BytesPerShort && nonstatic_short_count > 0) {
4548         nonstatic_short_count       -= 1;
4549         nonstatic_short_space_count += 1;
4550         length -= BytesPerShort;
4551         offset += BytesPerShort;
4552       }
4553       nonstatic_byte_space_offset = offset;
4554       while (length > 0 && nonstatic_byte_count > 0) {
4555         nonstatic_byte_count       -= 1;
4556         nonstatic_byte_space_count += 1;
4557         length -= 1;
4558       }
4559       // Allocate oop field in the gap if there are no other fields for that.
4560       nonstatic_oop_space_offset = offset;
4561       if (length >= heapOopSize && nonstatic_oop_count > 0 &&
4562           !allocate_oops_first) { // when oop fields not first
4563         nonstatic_oop_count      -= 1;
4564         nonstatic_oop_space_count = 1; // Only one will fit
4565         length -= heapOopSize;
4566         offset += heapOopSize;
4567       }
4568     }
4569   }
4570 
4571   int next_nonstatic_word_offset = next_nonstatic_double_offset +
4572                                      (nonstatic_double_count * BytesPerLong);
4573   int next_nonstatic_short_offset = next_nonstatic_word_offset +
4574                                       (nonstatic_word_count * BytesPerInt);
4575   int next_nonstatic_byte_offset = next_nonstatic_short_offset +
4576                                      (nonstatic_short_count * BytesPerShort);
4577   int next_nonstatic_padded_offset = next_nonstatic_byte_offset +
4578                                        nonstatic_byte_count;
4579 
4580   // let oops jump before padding with this allocation style
4581   if (!allocate_oops_first) {
4582     next_nonstatic_oop_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4583     if( nonstatic_oop_count > 0 ) {
4584       next_nonstatic_oop_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_oop_offset, heapOopSize);
4585     }
4586     next_nonstatic_padded_offset = next_nonstatic_oop_offset + (nonstatic_oop_count * heapOopSize);
4587   }
4588 
4589   // Aligning embedded value types
4590   // bug below, the current algorithm to layout embedded value types always put them at the
4591   // end of the layout, which doesn't match the different allocation policies the VM is
4592   // supposed to provide => FixMe
4593   // Note also that the current alignment policy is to make each value type starting on a
4594   // 64 bits boundary. This could be optimized later. For instance, it could be nice to
4595   // align value types according to their most constrained internal type.
4596   next_nonstatic_valuetype_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerLong);
4597   int next_value_type_index = 0;
4598 
4599   // Iterate over fields again and compute correct offsets.
4600   // The field allocation type was temporarily stored in the offset slot.
4601   // oop fields are located before non-oop fields (static and non-static).
4602   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4603 
4604     // skip already laid out fields
4605     if (fs.is_offset_set()) continue;
4606 
4607     // contended instance fields are handled below
4608     if (fs.is_contended() && !fs.access_flags().is_static()) continue;
4609 
4610     int real_offset = 0;
4611     const FieldAllocationType atype = (const FieldAllocationType) fs.allocation_type();
4612 
4613     // pack the rest of the fields
4614     switch (atype) {
4615       // Value types in static fields are handled with oops
4616       case STATIC_FLATTENABLE:   // Fallthrough
4617       case STATIC_OOP:
4618         real_offset = next_static_oop_offset;
4619         next_static_oop_offset += heapOopSize;
4620         break;
4621       case STATIC_BYTE:
4622         real_offset = next_static_byte_offset;
4623         next_static_byte_offset += 1;
4624         break;
4625       case STATIC_SHORT:
4626         real_offset = next_static_short_offset;
4627         next_static_short_offset += BytesPerShort;
4628         break;
4629       case STATIC_WORD:
4630         real_offset = next_static_word_offset;
4631         next_static_word_offset += BytesPerInt;
4632         break;
4633       case STATIC_DOUBLE:
4634         real_offset = next_static_double_offset;
4635         next_static_double_offset += BytesPerLong;
4636         break;
4637       case NONSTATIC_FLATTENABLE:
4638         if (fs.is_flattened()) {
4639           Klass* klass = nonstatic_value_type_klasses[next_value_type_index];
4640           assert(klass != NULL, "Klass should have been loaded and resolved earlier");
4641           assert(klass->access_flags().is_value_type(),"Must be a value type");
4642           ValueKlass* vklass = ValueKlass::cast(klass);
4643           real_offset = next_nonstatic_valuetype_offset;
4644           next_nonstatic_valuetype_offset += (vklass->size_helper()) * wordSize - vklass->first_field_offset();
4645           // aligning next value type on a 64 bits boundary
4646           next_nonstatic_valuetype_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_valuetype_offset, BytesPerLong);
4647           next_value_type_index += 1;
4648 
4649           if (vklass->contains_oops()) { // add flatten oop maps
4650             int diff = real_offset - vklass->first_field_offset();
4651             const OopMapBlock* map = vklass->start_of_nonstatic_oop_maps();
4652             const OopMapBlock* const last_map = map + vklass->nonstatic_oop_map_count();
4653             while (map < last_map) {
4654               nonstatic_oop_maps->add(map->offset() + diff, map->count());
4655               map++;
4656             }
4657           }
4658           break;
4659         } else {
4660           // Fall through
4661         }
4662       case NONSTATIC_OOP:
4663         if( nonstatic_oop_space_count > 0 ) {
4664           real_offset = nonstatic_oop_space_offset;
4665           nonstatic_oop_space_offset += heapOopSize;
4666           nonstatic_oop_space_count  -= 1;
4667         } else {
4668           real_offset = next_nonstatic_oop_offset;
4669           next_nonstatic_oop_offset += heapOopSize;
4670         }
4671         nonstatic_oop_maps->add(real_offset, 1);
4672         break;
4673       case NONSTATIC_BYTE:
4674         if( nonstatic_byte_space_count > 0 ) {
4675           real_offset = nonstatic_byte_space_offset;
4676           nonstatic_byte_space_offset += 1;
4677           nonstatic_byte_space_count  -= 1;
4678         } else {
4679           real_offset = next_nonstatic_byte_offset;
4680           next_nonstatic_byte_offset += 1;
4681         }
4682         break;
4683       case NONSTATIC_SHORT:
4684         if( nonstatic_short_space_count > 0 ) {
4685           real_offset = nonstatic_short_space_offset;
4686           nonstatic_short_space_offset += BytesPerShort;
4687           nonstatic_short_space_count  -= 1;
4688         } else {
4689           real_offset = next_nonstatic_short_offset;
4690           next_nonstatic_short_offset += BytesPerShort;
4691         }
4692         break;
4693       case NONSTATIC_WORD:
4694         if( nonstatic_word_space_count > 0 ) {
4695           real_offset = nonstatic_word_space_offset;
4696           nonstatic_word_space_offset += BytesPerInt;
4697           nonstatic_word_space_count  -= 1;
4698         } else {
4699           real_offset = next_nonstatic_word_offset;
4700           next_nonstatic_word_offset += BytesPerInt;
4701         }
4702         break;
4703       case NONSTATIC_DOUBLE:
4704         real_offset = next_nonstatic_double_offset;
4705         next_nonstatic_double_offset += BytesPerLong;
4706         break;
4707       default:
4708         ShouldNotReachHere();
4709     }
4710     fs.set_offset(real_offset);
4711   }
4712 
4713 
4714   // Handle the contended cases.
4715   //
4716   // Each contended field should not intersect the cache line with another contended field.
4717   // In the absence of alignment information, we end up with pessimistically separating
4718   // the fields with full-width padding.
4719   //
4720   // Additionally, this should not break alignment for the fields, so we round the alignment up
4721   // for each field.
4722   if (nonstatic_contended_count > 0) {
4723 
4724     // if there is at least one contended field, we need to have pre-padding for them
4725     next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4726 
4727     // collect all contended groups
4728     ResourceBitMap bm(cp->size());
4729     for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4730       // skip already laid out fields
4731       if (fs.is_offset_set()) continue;
4732 
4733       if (fs.is_contended()) {
4734         bm.set_bit(fs.contended_group());
4735       }
4736     }
4737 
4738     int current_group = -1;
4739     while ((current_group = (int)bm.get_next_one_offset(current_group + 1)) != (int)bm.size()) {
4740 
4741       for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
4742 
4743         // skip already laid out fields
4744         if (fs.is_offset_set()) continue;
4745 
4746         // skip non-contended fields and fields from different group
4747         if (!fs.is_contended() || (fs.contended_group() != current_group)) continue;
4748 
4749         // handle statics below
4750         if (fs.access_flags().is_static()) continue;
4751 
4752         int real_offset = 0;
4753         FieldAllocationType atype = (FieldAllocationType) fs.allocation_type();
4754 
4755         switch (atype) {
4756           case NONSTATIC_BYTE:
4757             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, 1);
4758             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4759             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += 1;
4760             break;
4761 
4762           case NONSTATIC_SHORT:
4763             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerShort);
4764             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4765             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += BytesPerShort;
4766             break;
4767 
4768           case NONSTATIC_WORD:
4769             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerInt);
4770             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4771             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += BytesPerInt;
4772             break;
4773 
4774           case NONSTATIC_DOUBLE:
4775             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, BytesPerLong);
4776             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4777             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += BytesPerLong;
4778             break;
4779 
4780             // Value types in static fields are handled with oops
4781           case NONSTATIC_FLATTENABLE:
4782             throwValueTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
4783                                      "@Contended annotation not supported for inline types yet", fs.name(), fs.signature());
4784             return;
4785 
4786           case NONSTATIC_OOP:
4787             next_nonstatic_padded_offset = align_up(next_nonstatic_padded_offset, heapOopSize);
4788             real_offset = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4789             next_nonstatic_padded_offset += heapOopSize;
4790             nonstatic_oop_maps->add(real_offset, 1);
4791             break;
4792 
4793           default:
4794             ShouldNotReachHere();
4795         }
4796 
4797         if (fs.contended_group() == 0) {
4798           // Contended group defines the equivalence class over the fields:
4799           // the fields within the same contended group are not inter-padded.
4800           // The only exception is default group, which does not incur the
4801           // equivalence, and so requires intra-padding.
4802           next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4803         }
4804 
4805         fs.set_offset(real_offset);
4806       } // for
4807 
4808       // Start laying out the next group.
4809       // Note that this will effectively pad the last group in the back;
4810       // this is expected to alleviate memory contention effects for
4811       // subclass fields and/or adjacent object.
4812       // If this was the default group, the padding is already in place.
4813       if (current_group != 0) {
4814         next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4815       }
4816     }
4817 
4818     // handle static fields
4819   }
4820 
4821   // Entire class is contended, pad in the back.
4822   // This helps to alleviate memory contention effects for subclass fields
4823   // and/or adjacent object.
4824   if (is_contended_class) {
4825     assert(!is_value_type(), "@Contended not supported for value types yet");
4826     next_nonstatic_padded_offset += ContendedPaddingWidth;
4827   }
4828 
4829   int notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end;
4830   if (nonstatic_value_type_count != 0) {
4831     notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end = next_nonstatic_valuetype_offset;
4832   } else {
4833     notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end = next_nonstatic_padded_offset;
4834   }
4835 
4836   int nonstatic_field_sz_align = heapOopSize;
4837   if (is_value_type()) {
4838     if ((notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end - nonstatic_fields_start) > heapOopSize) {
4839       nonstatic_field_sz_align = BytesPerLong; // value copy of fields only uses jlong copy
4840     }
4841   }
4842   int nonstatic_fields_end      = align_up(notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end, nonstatic_field_sz_align);
4843   int instance_end              = align_up(notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end, wordSize);
4844   int static_fields_end         = align_up(next_static_byte_offset, wordSize);
4845 
4846   int static_field_size         = (static_fields_end -
4847                                    InstanceMirrorKlass::offset_of_static_fields()) / wordSize;
4848   nonstatic_field_size          = nonstatic_field_size +
4849                                   (nonstatic_fields_end - nonstatic_fields_start) / heapOopSize;
4850 
4851   int instance_size             = align_object_size(instance_end / wordSize);
4852 
4853   assert(instance_size == align_object_size(align_up(
4854          (instanceOopDesc::base_offset_in_bytes() + nonstatic_field_size*heapOopSize)
4855          + initial_value_type_padding, wordSize) / wordSize), "consistent layout helper value");
4856 
4857 
4858   // Invariant: nonstatic_field end/start should only change if there are
4859   // nonstatic fields in the class, or if the class is contended. We compare
4860   // against the non-aligned value, so that end alignment will not fail the
4861   // assert without actually having the fields.
4862   assert((notaligned_nonstatic_fields_end == nonstatic_fields_start) ||
4863          is_contended_class ||
4864          (nonstatic_fields_count > 0), "double-check nonstatic start/end");
4865 
4866   // Number of non-static oop map blocks allocated at end of klass.
4867   nonstatic_oop_maps->compact();
4868 
4869 #ifndef PRODUCT
4870   if ((PrintFieldLayout && !is_value_type()) ||
4871       (PrintValueLayout && (is_value_type() || has_nonstatic_value_fields))) {
4872     print_field_layout(_class_name,
4873           _fields,
4874           cp,
4875           instance_size,
4876           nonstatic_fields_start,
4877           nonstatic_fields_end,
4878           static_fields_end);
4879     nonstatic_oop_maps->print_on(tty);
4880     tty->print("\n");
4881     tty->print_cr("Instance size = %d", instance_size);
4882     tty->print_cr("Nonstatic_field_size = %d", nonstatic_field_size);
4883     tty->print_cr("Static_field_size = %d", static_field_size);
4884     tty->print_cr("Has nonstatic fields = %d", has_nonstatic_fields);
4885     tty->print_cr("---");
4886   }
4887 
4888 #endif
4889   // Pass back information needed for InstanceKlass creation
4890   info->oop_map_blocks = nonstatic_oop_maps;
4891   info->_instance_size = instance_size;
4892   info->_static_field_size = static_field_size;
4893   info->_nonstatic_field_size = nonstatic_field_size;
4894   info->_has_nonstatic_fields = has_nonstatic_fields;
4895 
4896   // A value type is naturally atomic if it has just one field, and
4897   // that field is simple enough.
4898   info->_is_naturally_atomic = (is_value_type() &&
4899                                 !super_has_nonstatic_fields &&
4900                                 (nonstatic_fields_count <= 1) &&
4901                                 (not_atomic_value_types == 0) &&
4902                                 (nonstatic_contended_count == 0));
4903   // This may be too restrictive, since if all the fields fit in 64
4904   // bits we could make the decision to align instances of this class
4905   // to 64-bit boundaries, and load and store them as single words.
4906   // And on machines which supported larger atomics we could similarly
4907   // allow larger values to be atomic, if properly aligned.
4908 }
4909 
4910 void ClassFileParser::set_precomputed_flags(InstanceKlass* ik) {
4911   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
4912 
4913   const Klass* const super = ik->super();
4914 
4915   // Check if this klass has an empty finalize method (i.e. one with return bytecode only),
4916   // in which case we don't have to register objects as finalizable
4917   if (!_has_empty_finalizer) {
4918     if (_has_finalizer ||
4919         (super != NULL && super->has_finalizer())) {
4920       ik->set_has_finalizer();
4921     }
4922   }
4923 
4924 #ifdef ASSERT
4925   bool f = false;
4926   const Method* const m = ik->lookup_method(vmSymbols::finalize_method_name(),
4927                                            vmSymbols::void_method_signature());
4928   if (m != NULL && !m->is_empty_method()) {
4929       f = true;
4930   }
4931 
4932   // Spec doesn't prevent agent from redefinition of empty finalizer.
4933   // Despite the fact that it's generally bad idea and redefined finalizer
4934   // will not work as expected we shouldn't abort vm in this case
4935   if (!ik->has_redefined_this_or_super()) {
4936     assert(ik->has_finalizer() == f, "inconsistent has_finalizer");
4937   }
4938 #endif
4939 
4940   // Check if this klass supports the java.lang.Cloneable interface
4941   if (SystemDictionary::Cloneable_klass_loaded()) {
4942     if (ik->is_subtype_of(SystemDictionary::Cloneable_klass())) {
4943       if (ik->is_value()) {
4944         Thread *THREAD = Thread::current();
4945         throwValueTypeLimitation(THREAD_AND_LOCATION, "Inline Types do not support Cloneable");
4946         return;
4947       }
4948       ik->set_is_cloneable();
4949     }
4950   }
4951 
4952   // Check if this klass has a vanilla default constructor
4953   if (super == NULL) {
4954     // java.lang.Object has empty default constructor
4955     ik->set_has_vanilla_constructor();
4956   } else {
4957     if (super->has_vanilla_constructor() &&
4958         _has_vanilla_constructor) {
4959       ik->set_has_vanilla_constructor();
4960     }
4961 #ifdef ASSERT
4962     bool v = false;
4963     if (super->has_vanilla_constructor()) {
4964       const Method* const constructor =
4965         ik->find_method(vmSymbols::object_initializer_name(),
4966                        vmSymbols::void_method_signature());
4967       if (constructor != NULL && constructor->is_vanilla_constructor()) {
4968         v = true;
4969       }
4970     }
4971     assert(v == ik->has_vanilla_constructor(), "inconsistent has_vanilla_constructor");
4972 #endif
4973   }
4974 
4975   // If it cannot be fast-path allocated, set a bit in the layout helper.
4976   // See documentation of InstanceKlass::can_be_fastpath_allocated().
4977   assert(ik->size_helper() > 0, "layout_helper is initialized");
4978   if ((!RegisterFinalizersAtInit && ik->has_finalizer())
4979       || ik->is_abstract() || ik->is_interface()
4980       || (ik->name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_Class() && ik->class_loader() == NULL)
4981       || ik->size_helper() >= FastAllocateSizeLimit) {
4982     // Forbid fast-path allocation.
4983     const jint lh = Klass::instance_layout_helper(ik->size_helper(), true);
4984     ik->set_layout_helper(lh);
4985   }
4986 }
4987 
4988 bool ClassFileParser::supports_value_types() const {
4989   // Value types are only supported by class file version 55 and later
4990   return _major_version >= JAVA_11_VERSION;
4991 }
4992 
4993 // utility methods for appending an array with check for duplicates
4994 
4995 static void append_interfaces(GrowableArray<InstanceKlass*>* result,
4996                               const Array<InstanceKlass*>* const ifs) {
4997   // iterate over new interfaces
4998   for (int i = 0; i < ifs->length(); i++) {
4999     InstanceKlass* const e = ifs->at(i);
5000     assert(e->is_klass() && e->is_interface(), "just checking");
5001     // add new interface
5002     result->append_if_missing(e);
5003   }
5004 }
5005 
5006 static Array<InstanceKlass*>* compute_transitive_interfaces(const InstanceKlass* super,
5007                                                             Array<InstanceKlass*>* local_ifs,
5008                                                             ClassLoaderData* loader_data,
5009                                                             TRAPS) {
5010   assert(local_ifs != NULL, "invariant");
5011   assert(loader_data != NULL, "invariant");
5012 
5013   // Compute maximum size for transitive interfaces
5014   int max_transitive_size = 0;
5015   int super_size = 0;
5016   // Add superclass transitive interfaces size
5017   if (super != NULL) {
5018     super_size = super->transitive_interfaces()->length();
5019     max_transitive_size += super_size;
5020   }
5021   // Add local interfaces' super interfaces
5022   const int local_size = local_ifs->length();
5023   for (int i = 0; i < local_size; i++) {
5024     InstanceKlass* const l = local_ifs->at(i);
5025     max_transitive_size += l->transitive_interfaces()->length();
5026   }
5027   // Finally add local interfaces
5028   max_transitive_size += local_size;
5029   // Construct array
5030   if (max_transitive_size == 0) {
5031     // no interfaces, use canonicalized array
5032     return Universe::the_empty_instance_klass_array();
5033   } else if (max_transitive_size == super_size) {
5034     // no new local interfaces added, share superklass' transitive interface array
5035     return super->transitive_interfaces();
5036     // The three lines below are commented to work around bug JDK-8245487
5037 //  } else if (max_transitive_size == local_size) {
5038 //    // only local interfaces added, share local interface array
5039 //    return local_ifs;
5040   } else {
5041     ResourceMark rm;
5042     GrowableArray<InstanceKlass*>* const result = new GrowableArray<InstanceKlass*>(max_transitive_size);
5043 
5044     // Copy down from superclass
5045     if (super != NULL) {
5046       append_interfaces(result, super->transitive_interfaces());
5047     }
5048 
5049     // Copy down from local interfaces' superinterfaces
5050     for (int i = 0; i < local_size; i++) {
5051       InstanceKlass* const l = local_ifs->at(i);
5052       append_interfaces(result, l->transitive_interfaces());
5053     }
5054     // Finally add local interfaces
5055     append_interfaces(result, local_ifs);
5056 
5057     // length will be less than the max_transitive_size if duplicates were removed
5058     const int length = result->length();
5059     assert(length <= max_transitive_size, "just checking");
5060 
5061     if (length == 1 && result->at(0) == SystemDictionary::IdentityObject_klass()) {
5062       return Universe::the_single_IdentityObject_klass_array();
5063     }
5064 
5065     Array<InstanceKlass*>* const new_result =
5066       MetadataFactory::new_array<InstanceKlass*>(loader_data, length, CHECK_NULL);
5067     for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
5068       InstanceKlass* const e = result->at(i);
5069       assert(e != NULL, "just checking");
5070       new_result->at_put(i, e);
5071     }
5072     return new_result;
5073   }
5074 }
5075 
5076 static void check_super_class_access(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5077   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5078   const Klass* const super = this_klass->super();
5079 
5080   if (super != NULL) {
5081 
5082     // If the loader is not the boot loader then throw an exception if its
5083     // superclass is in package jdk.internal.reflect and its loader is not a
5084     // special reflection class loader
5085     if (!this_klass->class_loader_data()->is_the_null_class_loader_data()) {
5086       assert(super->is_instance_klass(), "super is not instance klass");
5087       PackageEntry* super_package = super->package();
5088       if (super_package != NULL &&
5089           super_package->name()->fast_compare(vmSymbols::jdk_internal_reflect()) == 0 &&
5090           !java_lang_ClassLoader::is_reflection_class_loader(this_klass->class_loader())) {
5091         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5092         Exceptions::fthrow(
5093           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5094           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5095           "class %s loaded by %s cannot access jdk/internal/reflect superclass %s",
5096           this_klass->external_name(),
5097           this_klass->class_loader_data()->loader_name_and_id(),
5098           super->external_name());
5099         return;
5100       }
5101     }
5102 
5103     Reflection::VerifyClassAccessResults vca_result =
5104       Reflection::verify_class_access(this_klass, InstanceKlass::cast(super), false);
5105     if (vca_result != Reflection::ACCESS_OK) {
5106       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5107       char* msg = Reflection::verify_class_access_msg(this_klass,
5108                                                       InstanceKlass::cast(super),
5109                                                       vca_result);
5110       if (msg == NULL) {
5111         bool same_module = (this_klass->module() == super->module());
5112         Exceptions::fthrow(
5113           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5114           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5115           "class %s cannot access its %ssuperclass %s (%s%s%s)",
5116           this_klass->external_name(),
5117           super->is_abstract() ? "abstract " : "",
5118           super->external_name(),
