5119           (same_module) ? this_klass->joint_in_module_of_loader(super) : this_klass->class_in_module_of_loader(),
5120           (same_module) ? "" : "; ",
5121           (same_module) ? "" : super->class_in_module_of_loader());
5122       } else {
5123         // Add additional message content.
5124         Exceptions::fthrow(
5125           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5126           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5127           "superclass access check failed: %s",
5128           msg);
5129       }
5130     }
5131   }
5132 }
5133 
5134 
5135 static void check_super_interface_access(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5136   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5137   const Array<InstanceKlass*>* const local_interfaces = this_klass->local_interfaces();
5138   const int lng = local_interfaces->length();
5139   for (int i = lng - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
5140     InstanceKlass* const k = local_interfaces->at(i);
5141     assert (k != NULL && k->is_interface(), "invalid interface");
5142     Reflection::VerifyClassAccessResults vca_result =
5143       Reflection::verify_class_access(this_klass, k, false);
5144     if (vca_result != Reflection::ACCESS_OK) {
5145       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5146       char* msg = Reflection::verify_class_access_msg(this_klass,
5147                                                       k,
5148                                                       vca_result);
5149       if (msg == NULL) {
5150         bool same_module = (this_klass->module() == k->module());
5151         Exceptions::fthrow(
5152           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5153           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5154           "class %s cannot access its superinterface %s (%s%s%s)",
5155           this_klass->external_name(),
5156           k->external_name(),
5157           (same_module) ? this_klass->joint_in_module_of_loader(k) : this_klass->class_in_module_of_loader(),
5158           (same_module) ? "" : "; ",
5159           (same_module) ? "" : k->class_in_module_of_loader());
5160       } else {
5161         // Add additional message content.
5162         Exceptions::fthrow(
5163           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5164           vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalAccessError(),
5165           "superinterface check failed: %s",
5166           msg);
5167       }
5168     }
5169   }
5170 }
5171 
5172 
5173 static void check_final_method_override(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5174   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5175   const Array<Method*>* const methods = this_klass->methods();
5176   const int num_methods = methods->length();
5177 
5178   // go thru each method and check if it overrides a final method
5179   for (int index = 0; index < num_methods; index++) {
5180     const Method* const m = methods->at(index);
5181 
5182     // skip private, static, and <init> methods
5183     if ((!m->is_private() && !m->is_static()) &&
5184         (m->name() != vmSymbols::object_initializer_name())) {
5185 
5186       const Symbol* const name = m->name();
5187       const Symbol* const signature = m->signature();
5188       const Klass* k = this_klass->super();
5189       const Method* super_m = NULL;
5190       while (k != NULL) {
5191         // skip supers that don't have final methods.
5192         if (k->has_final_method()) {
5193           // lookup a matching method in the super class hierarchy
5194           super_m = InstanceKlass::cast(k)->lookup_method(name, signature);
5195           if (super_m == NULL) {
5196             break; // didn't find any match; get out
5197           }
5198 
5199           if (super_m->is_final() && !super_m->is_static() &&
5200               !super_m->access_flags().is_private()) {
5201             // matching method in super is final, and not static or private
5202             bool can_access = Reflection::verify_member_access(this_klass,
5203                                                                super_m->method_holder(),
5204                                                                super_m->method_holder(),
5205                                                                super_m->access_flags(),
5206                                                               false, false, CHECK);
5207             if (can_access) {
5208               // this class can access super final method and therefore override
5209               ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5210               Exceptions::fthrow(THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5211                                  vmSymbols::java_lang_VerifyError(),
5212                                  "class %s overrides final method %s.%s%s",
5213                                  this_klass->external_name(),
5214                                  super_m->method_holder()->external_name(),
5215                                  name->as_C_string(),
5216                                  signature->as_C_string()
5217                                  );
5218               return;
5219             }
5220           }
5221 
5222           // continue to look from super_m's holder's super.
5223           k = super_m->method_holder()->super();
5224           continue;
5225         }
5226 
5227         k = k->super();
5228       }
5229     }
5230   }
5231 }
5232 
5233 
5234 // assumes that this_klass is an interface
5235 static void check_illegal_static_method(const InstanceKlass* this_klass, TRAPS) {
5236   assert(this_klass != NULL, "invariant");
5237   assert(this_klass->is_interface(), "not an interface");
5238   const Array<Method*>* methods = this_klass->methods();
5239   const int num_methods = methods->length();
5240 
5241   for (int index = 0; index < num_methods; index++) {
5242     const Method* const m = methods->at(index);
5243     // if m is static and not the init method, throw a verify error
5244     if ((m->is_static()) && (m->name() != vmSymbols::class_initializer_name())) {
5245       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5246       Exceptions::fthrow(
5247         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5248         vmSymbols::java_lang_VerifyError(),
5249         "Illegal static method %s in interface %s",
5250         m->name()->as_C_string(),
5251         this_klass->external_name()
5252       );
5253       return;
5254     }
5255   }
5256 }
5257 
5258 // utility methods for format checking
5259 
5260 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_class_modifiers(jint flags, TRAPS) const {
5261   const bool is_module = (flags & JVM_ACC_MODULE) != 0;
5262   const bool is_value_type = (flags & JVM_ACC_VALUE) != 0;
5263   assert(_major_version >= JAVA_9_VERSION || !is_module, "JVM_ACC_MODULE should not be set");
5264   assert(supports_value_types() || !is_value_type, "JVM_ACC_VALUE should not be set");
5265   if (is_module) {
5266     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5267     Exceptions::fthrow(
5268       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5269       vmSymbols::java_lang_NoClassDefFoundError(),
5270       "%s is not a class because access_flag ACC_MODULE is set",
5271       _class_name->as_C_string());
5272     return;
5273   }
5274 
5275   if (is_value_type && !EnableValhalla) {
5276     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5277     Exceptions::fthrow(
5278       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5279       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5280       "Class modifier ACC_VALUE in class %s requires option -XX:+EnableValhalla",
5281       _class_name->as_C_string()
5282     );
5283   }
5284 
5285   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5286 
5287   const bool is_interface  = (flags & JVM_ACC_INTERFACE)  != 0;
5288   const bool is_abstract   = (flags & JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT)   != 0;
5289   const bool is_final      = (flags & JVM_ACC_FINAL)      != 0;
5290   const bool is_super      = (flags & JVM_ACC_SUPER)      != 0;
5291   const bool is_enum       = (flags & JVM_ACC_ENUM)       != 0;
5292   const bool is_annotation = (flags & JVM_ACC_ANNOTATION) != 0;
5293   const bool major_gte_1_5 = _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION;
5294   const bool major_gte_14  = _major_version >= JAVA_14_VERSION;
5295 
5296   if ((is_abstract && is_final) ||
5297       (is_interface && !is_abstract) ||
5298       (is_interface && major_gte_1_5 && (is_super || is_enum)) ||
5299       (!is_interface && major_gte_1_5 && is_annotation) ||
5300       (is_value_type && (is_interface || is_abstract || is_enum || !is_final))) {
5301     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5302     const char* class_note = "";
5303     if (is_value_type)  class_note = " (an inline class)";
5304     Exceptions::fthrow(
5305       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5306       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5307       "Illegal class modifiers in class %s%s: 0x%X",
5308       _class_name->as_C_string(), class_note, flags
5309     );
5310     return;
5311   }
5312 }
5313 
5314 static bool has_illegal_visibility(jint flags) {
5315   const bool is_public    = (flags & JVM_ACC_PUBLIC)    != 0;
5316   const bool is_protected = (flags & JVM_ACC_PROTECTED) != 0;
5317   const bool is_private   = (flags & JVM_ACC_PRIVATE)   != 0;
5318 
5319   return ((is_public && is_protected) ||
5320           (is_public && is_private) ||
5321           (is_protected && is_private));
5322 }
5323 
5324 // A legal major_version.minor_version must be one of the following:
5325 //
5326 //  Major_version >= 45 and major_version < 56, any minor_version.
5327 //  Major_version >= 56 and major_version <= JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION and minor_version = 0.
5328 //  Major_version = JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION and minor_version = 65535 and --enable-preview is present.
5329 //
5330 static void verify_class_version(u2 major, u2 minor, Symbol* class_name, TRAPS){
5331   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5332   const u2 max_version = JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION;
5333   if (major < JAVA_MIN_SUPPORTED_VERSION) {
5334     Exceptions::fthrow(
5335       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5336       vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5337       "%s (class file version %u.%u) was compiled with an invalid major version",
5338       class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor);
5339     return;
5340   }
5341 
5342   if (major > max_version) {
5343     Exceptions::fthrow(
5344       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5345       vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5346       "%s has been compiled by a more recent version of the Java Runtime (class file version %u.%u), "
5347       "this version of the Java Runtime only recognizes class file versions up to %u.0",
5348       class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor, JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION);
5349     return;
5350   }
5351 
5352   if (major < JAVA_12_VERSION || minor == 0) {
5353     return;
5354   }
5355 
5356   if (minor == JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION) {
5357     if (major != max_version) {
5358       Exceptions::fthrow(
5359         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5360         vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5361         "%s (class file version %u.%u) was compiled with preview features that are unsupported. "
5362         "This version of the Java Runtime only recognizes preview features for class file version %u.%u",
5363         class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor, JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION, JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION);
5364       return;
5365     }
5366 
5367     if (!Arguments::enable_preview()) {
5368       Exceptions::fthrow(
5369         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5370         vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5371         "Preview features are not enabled for %s (class file version %u.%u). Try running with '--enable-preview'",
5372         class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor);
5373       return;
5374     }
5375 
5376   } else { // minor != JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION
5377     Exceptions::fthrow(
5378         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5379         vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
5380         "%s (class file version %u.%u) was compiled with an invalid non-zero minor version",
5381         class_name->as_C_string(), major, minor);
5382   }
5383 }
5384 
5385 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_field_modifiers(jint flags,
5386                                                    bool is_interface,
5387                                                    bool is_value_type,
5388                                                    TRAPS) const {
5389   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5390 
5391   const bool is_public    = (flags & JVM_ACC_PUBLIC)    != 0;
5392   const bool is_protected = (flags & JVM_ACC_PROTECTED) != 0;
5393   const bool is_private   = (flags & JVM_ACC_PRIVATE)   != 0;
5394   const bool is_static    = (flags & JVM_ACC_STATIC)    != 0;
5395   const bool is_final     = (flags & JVM_ACC_FINAL)     != 0;
5396   const bool is_volatile  = (flags & JVM_ACC_VOLATILE)  != 0;
5397   const bool is_transient = (flags & JVM_ACC_TRANSIENT) != 0;
5398   const bool is_enum      = (flags & JVM_ACC_ENUM)      != 0;
5399   const bool major_gte_1_5 = _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION;
5400 
5401   bool is_illegal = false;
5402 
5403   if (is_interface) {
5404     if (!is_public || !is_static || !is_final || is_private ||
5405         is_protected || is_volatile || is_transient ||
5406         (major_gte_1_5 && is_enum)) {
5407       is_illegal = true;
5408     }
5409   } else { // not interface
5410     if (has_illegal_visibility(flags) || (is_final && is_volatile)) {
5411       is_illegal = true;
5412     } else {
5413       if (is_value_type && !is_static && !is_final) {
5414         is_illegal = true;
5415       }
5416     }
5417   }
5418 
5419   if (is_illegal) {
5420     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5421     Exceptions::fthrow(
5422       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5423       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5424       "Illegal field modifiers in class %s: 0x%X",
5425       _class_name->as_C_string(), flags);
5426     return;
5427   }
5428 }
5429 
5430 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_method_modifiers(jint flags,
5431                                                     bool is_interface,
5432                                                     bool is_value_type,
5433                                                     const Symbol* name,
5434                                                     TRAPS) const {
5435   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5436 
5437   const bool is_public       = (flags & JVM_ACC_PUBLIC)       != 0;
5438   const bool is_private      = (flags & JVM_ACC_PRIVATE)      != 0;
5439   const bool is_static       = (flags & JVM_ACC_STATIC)       != 0;
5440   const bool is_final        = (flags & JVM_ACC_FINAL)        != 0;
5441   const bool is_native       = (flags & JVM_ACC_NATIVE)       != 0;
5442   const bool is_abstract     = (flags & JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT)     != 0;
5443   const bool is_bridge       = (flags & JVM_ACC_BRIDGE)       != 0;
5444   const bool is_strict       = (flags & JVM_ACC_STRICT)       != 0;
5445   const bool is_synchronized = (flags & JVM_ACC_SYNCHRONIZED) != 0;
5446   const bool is_protected    = (flags & JVM_ACC_PROTECTED)    != 0;
5447   const bool major_gte_1_5   = _major_version >= JAVA_1_5_VERSION;
5448   const bool major_gte_8     = _major_version >= JAVA_8_VERSION;
5449   const bool is_initializer  = (name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name());
5450 
5451   bool is_illegal = false;
5452 
5453   const char* class_note = "";
5454 
5455   if (is_interface) {
5456     if (major_gte_8) {
5457       // Class file version is JAVA_8_VERSION or later Methods of
5458       // interfaces may set any of the flags except ACC_PROTECTED,
5459       // ACC_FINAL, ACC_NATIVE, and ACC_SYNCHRONIZED; they must
5460       // have exactly one of the ACC_PUBLIC or ACC_PRIVATE flags set.
5461       if ((is_public == is_private) || /* Only one of private and public should be true - XNOR */
5462           (is_native || is_protected || is_final || is_synchronized) ||
5463           // If a specific method of a class or interface has its
5464           // ACC_ABSTRACT flag set, it must not have any of its
5465           // ACC_FINAL, ACC_NATIVE, ACC_PRIVATE, ACC_STATIC,
5466           // ACC_STRICT, or ACC_SYNCHRONIZED flags set.  No need to
5467           // check for ACC_FINAL, ACC_NATIVE or ACC_SYNCHRONIZED as
5468           // those flags are illegal irrespective of ACC_ABSTRACT being set or not.
5469           (is_abstract && (is_private || is_static || is_strict))) {
5470         is_illegal = true;
5471       }
5472     } else if (major_gte_1_5) {
5473       // Class file version in the interval [JAVA_1_5_VERSION, JAVA_8_VERSION)
5474       if (!is_public || is_private || is_protected || is_static || is_final ||
5475           is_synchronized || is_native || !is_abstract || is_strict) {
5476         is_illegal = true;
5477       }
5478     } else {
5479       // Class file version is pre-JAVA_1_5_VERSION
5480       if (!is_public || is_static || is_final || is_native || !is_abstract) {
5481         is_illegal = true;
5482       }
5483     }
5484   } else { // not interface
5485     if (has_illegal_visibility(flags)) {
5486       is_illegal = true;
5487     } else {
5488       if (is_initializer) {
5489         if (is_final || is_synchronized || is_native ||
5490             is_abstract || (major_gte_1_5 && is_bridge)) {
5491           is_illegal = true;
5492         }
5493         if (!is_static && !is_value_type) {
5494           // OK, an object constructor in a regular class
5495         } else if (is_static && is_value_type) {
5496           // OK, a static init factory in an inline class
5497         } else {
5498           // but no other combinations are allowed
5499           is_illegal = true;
5500           class_note = (is_value_type ? " (an inline class)" : " (not an inline class)");
5501         }
5502       } else { // not initializer
5503         if (is_value_type && is_synchronized && !is_static) {
5504           is_illegal = true;
5505           class_note = " (an inline class)";
5506         } else {
5507           if (is_abstract) {
5508             if ((is_final || is_native || is_private || is_static ||
5509                 (major_gte_1_5 && (is_synchronized || is_strict)))) {
5510               is_illegal = true;
5511             }
5512           }
5513         }
5514       }
5515     }
5516   }
5517 
5518   if (is_illegal) {
5519     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5520     Exceptions::fthrow(
5521       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5522       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5523       "Method %s in class %s%s has illegal modifiers: 0x%X",
5524       name->as_C_string(), _class_name->as_C_string(), class_note, flags);
5525     return;
5526   }
5527 }
5528 
5529 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_utf8(const unsigned char* buffer,
5530                                         int length,
5531                                         TRAPS) const {
5532   assert(_need_verify, "only called when _need_verify is true");
5533   if (!UTF8::is_legal_utf8(buffer, length, _major_version <= 47)) {
5534     classfile_parse_error("Illegal UTF8 string in constant pool in class file %s", CHECK);
5535   }
5536 }
5537 
5538 // Unqualified names may not contain the characters '.', ';', '[', or '/'.
5539 // In class names, '/' separates unqualified names.  This is verified in this function also.
5540 // Method names also may not contain the characters '<' or '>', unless <init>
5541 // or <clinit>.  Note that method names may not be <init> or <clinit> in this
5542 // method.  Because these names have been checked as special cases before
5543 // calling this method in verify_legal_method_name.
5544 //
5545 // This method is also called from the modular system APIs in modules.cpp
5546 // to verify the validity of module and package names.
5547 bool ClassFileParser::verify_unqualified_name(const char* name,
5548                                               unsigned int length,
5549                                               int type) {
5550   if (length == 0) return false;  // Must have at least one char.
5551   for (const char* p = name; p != name + length; p++) {
5552     switch(*p) {
5553       case JVM_SIGNATURE_DOT:
5554       case JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS:
5555       case JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY:
5556         // do not permit '.', ';', or '['
5557         return false;
5558       case JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH:
5559         // check for '//' or leading or trailing '/' which are not legal
5560         // unqualified name must not be empty
5561         if (type == ClassFileParser::LegalClass) {
5562           if (p == name || p+1 >= name+length ||
5563               *(p+1) == JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH) {
5564             return false;
5565           }
5566         } else {
5567           return false;   // do not permit '/' unless it's class name
5568         }
5569         break;
5570       case JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL:
5571       case JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDSPECIAL:
5572         // do not permit '<' or '>' in method names
5573         if (type == ClassFileParser::LegalMethod) {
5574           return false;
5575         }
5576     }
5577   }
5578   return true;
5579 }
5580 
5581 // Take pointer to a UTF8 byte string (not NUL-terminated).
5582 // Skip over the longest part of the string that could
5583 // be taken as a fieldname. Allow '/' if slash_ok is true.
5584 // Return a pointer to just past the fieldname.
5585 // Return NULL if no fieldname at all was found, or in the case of slash_ok
5586 // being true, we saw consecutive slashes (meaning we were looking for a
5587 // qualified path but found something that was badly-formed).
5588 static const char* skip_over_field_name(const char* const name,
5589                                         bool slash_ok,
5590                                         unsigned int length) {
5591   const char* p;
5592   jboolean last_is_slash = false;
5593   jboolean not_first_ch = false;
5594 
5595   for (p = name; p != name + length; not_first_ch = true) {
5596     const char* old_p = p;
5597     jchar ch = *p;
5598     if (ch < 128) {
5599       p++;
5600       // quick check for ascii
5601       if ((ch >= 'a' && ch <= 'z') ||
5602         (ch >= 'A' && ch <= 'Z') ||
5603         (ch == '_' || ch == '$') ||
5604         (not_first_ch && ch >= '0' && ch <= '9')) {
5605         last_is_slash = false;
5606         continue;
5607       }
5608       if (slash_ok && ch == JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH) {
5609         if (last_is_slash) {
5610           return NULL;  // Don't permit consecutive slashes
5611         }
5612         last_is_slash = true;
5613         continue;
5614       }
5615     }
5616     else {
5617       jint unicode_ch;
5618       char* tmp_p = UTF8::next_character(p, &unicode_ch);
5619       p = tmp_p;
5620       last_is_slash = false;
5621       // Check if ch is Java identifier start or is Java identifier part
5622       // 4672820: call java.lang.Character methods directly without generating separate tables.
5623       EXCEPTION_MARK;
5624       // return value
5625       JavaValue result(T_BOOLEAN);
5626       // Set up the arguments to isJavaIdentifierStart or isJavaIdentifierPart
5627       JavaCallArguments args;
5628       args.push_int(unicode_ch);
5629 
5630       if (not_first_ch) {
5631         // public static boolean isJavaIdentifierPart(char ch);
5632         JavaCalls::call_static(&result,
5633           SystemDictionary::Character_klass(),
5634           vmSymbols::isJavaIdentifierPart_name(),
5635           vmSymbols::int_bool_signature(),
5636           &args,
5637           THREAD);
5638       } else {
5639         // public static boolean isJavaIdentifierStart(char ch);
5640         JavaCalls::call_static(&result,
5641           SystemDictionary::Character_klass(),
5642           vmSymbols::isJavaIdentifierStart_name(),
5643           vmSymbols::int_bool_signature(),
5644           &args,
5645           THREAD);
5646       }
5647       if (HAS_PENDING_EXCEPTION) {
5648         CLEAR_PENDING_EXCEPTION;
5649         return NULL;
5650       }
5651       if(result.get_jboolean()) {
5652         continue;
5653       }
5654     }
5655     return (not_first_ch) ? old_p : NULL;
5656   }
5657   return (not_first_ch) ? p : NULL;
5658 }
5659 
5660 // Take pointer to a UTF8 byte string (not NUL-terminated).
5661 // Skip over the longest part of the string that could
5662 // be taken as a field signature. Allow "void" if void_ok.
5663 // Return a pointer to just past the signature.
5664 // Return NULL if no legal signature is found.
5665 const char* ClassFileParser::skip_over_field_signature(const char* signature,
5666                                                        bool void_ok,
5667                                                        unsigned int length,
5668                                                        TRAPS) const {
5669   unsigned int array_dim = 0;
5670   while (length > 0) {
5671     switch (signature[0]) {
5672     case JVM_SIGNATURE_VOID: if (!void_ok) { return NULL; }
5673     case JVM_SIGNATURE_BOOLEAN:
5674     case JVM_SIGNATURE_BYTE:
5675     case JVM_SIGNATURE_CHAR:
5676     case JVM_SIGNATURE_SHORT:
5677     case JVM_SIGNATURE_INT:
5678     case JVM_SIGNATURE_FLOAT:
5679     case JVM_SIGNATURE_LONG:
5680     case JVM_SIGNATURE_DOUBLE:
5681       return signature + 1;
5682     case JVM_SIGNATURE_VALUETYPE:
5683       // Can't enable this check until JDK upgrades the bytecode generators
5684       // if (_major_version < CONSTANT_CLASS_DESCRIPTORS ) {
5685       //   classfile_parse_error("Class name contains illegal Q-signature "
5686       //                                    "in descriptor in class file %s",
5687       //                                    CHECK_0);
5688       // }
5689       // fall through
5690     case JVM_SIGNATURE_CLASS:
5691     {
5692       if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5693         // Skip over the class name if one is there
5694         const char* const p = skip_over_field_name(signature + 1, true, --length);
5695 
5696         // The next character better be a semicolon
5697         if (p && (p - signature) > 1 && p[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS) {
5698           return p + 1;
5699         }
5700       }
5701       else {
5702         // Skip leading 'L' or 'Q' and ignore first appearance of ';'
5703         signature++;
5704         const char* c = (const char*) memchr(signature, JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS, length - 1);
5705         // Format check signature
5706         if (c != NULL) {
5707           int newlen = c - (char*) signature;
5708           bool legal = verify_unqualified_name(signature, newlen, LegalClass);
5709           if (!legal) {
5710             classfile_parse_error("Class name is empty or contains illegal character "
5711                                   "in descriptor in class file %s",
5712                                   CHECK_NULL);
5713             return NULL;
5714           }
5715           return signature + newlen + 1;
5716         }
5717       }
5718       return NULL;
5719     }
5720     case JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY:
5721       array_dim++;
5722       if (array_dim > 255) {
5723         // 4277370: array descriptor is valid only if it represents 255 or fewer dimensions.
5724         classfile_parse_error("Array type descriptor has more than 255 dimensions in class file %s", CHECK_NULL);
5725       }
5726       // The rest of what's there better be a legal signature
5727       signature++;
5728       length--;
5729       void_ok = false;
5730       break;
5731     default:
5732       return NULL;
5733     }
5734   }
5735   return NULL;
5736 }
5737 
5738 // Checks if name is a legal class name.
5739 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_class_name(const Symbol* name, TRAPS) const {
5740   if (!_need_verify || _relax_verify) { return; }
5741 
5742   assert(name->refcount() > 0, "symbol must be kept alive");
5743   char* bytes = (char*)name->bytes();
5744   unsigned int length = name->utf8_length();
5745   bool legal = false;
5746 
5747   if (length > 0) {
5748     const char* p;
5749     if (bytes[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY) {
5750       p = skip_over_field_signature(bytes, false, length, CHECK);
5751       legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5752     } else if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5753       if (bytes[0] != JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5754         p = skip_over_field_name(bytes, true, length);
5755         legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5756       }
5757     } else if (_major_version >= CONSTANT_CLASS_DESCRIPTORS && bytes[length - 1] == ';' ) {
5758       // Support for L...; and Q...; descriptors
5759       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes + 1, length - 2, LegalClass);
5760     } else {
5761       // 4900761: relax the constraints based on JSR202 spec
5762       // Class names may be drawn from the entire Unicode character set.
5763       // Identifiers between '/' must be unqualified names.
5764       // The utf8 string has been verified when parsing cpool entries.
5765       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes, length, LegalClass);
5766     }
5767   }
5768   if (!legal) {
5769     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5770     assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
5771     Exceptions::fthrow(
5772       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5773       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5774       "Illegal class name \"%.*s\" in class file %s", length, bytes,
5775       _class_name->as_C_string()
5776     );
5777     return;
5778   }
5779 }
5780 
5781 // Checks if name is a legal field name.
5782 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_field_name(const Symbol* name, TRAPS) const {
5783   if (!_need_verify || _relax_verify) { return; }
5784 
5785   char* bytes = (char*)name->bytes();
5786   unsigned int length = name->utf8_length();
5787   bool legal = false;
5788 
5789   if (length > 0) {
5790     if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5791       if (bytes[0] != JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5792         const char* p = skip_over_field_name(bytes, false, length);
5793         legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5794       }
5795     } else {
5796       // 4881221: relax the constraints based on JSR202 spec
5797       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes, length, LegalField);
5798     }
5799   }
5800 
5801   if (!legal) {
5802     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5803     assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
5804     Exceptions::fthrow(
5805       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5806       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5807       "Illegal field name \"%.*s\" in class %s", length, bytes,
5808       _class_name->as_C_string()
5809     );
5810     return;
5811   }
5812 }
5813 
5814 // Checks if name is a legal method name.
5815 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_method_name(const Symbol* name, TRAPS) const {
5816   if (!_need_verify || _relax_verify) { return; }
5817 
5818   assert(name != NULL, "method name is null");
5819   char* bytes = (char*)name->bytes();
5820   unsigned int length = name->utf8_length();
5821   bool legal = false;
5822 
5823   if (length > 0) {
5824     if (bytes[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5825       if (name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name() || name == vmSymbols::class_initializer_name()) {
5826         legal = true;
5827       }
5828     } else if (_major_version < JAVA_1_5_VERSION) {
5829       const char* p;
5830       p = skip_over_field_name(bytes, false, length);
5831       legal = (p != NULL) && ((p - bytes) == (int)length);
5832     } else {
5833       // 4881221: relax the constraints based on JSR202 spec
5834       legal = verify_unqualified_name(bytes, length, LegalMethod);
5835     }
5836   }
5837 
5838   if (!legal) {
5839     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
5840     assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
5841     Exceptions::fthrow(
5842       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
5843       vmSymbols::java_lang_ClassFormatError(),
5844       "Illegal method name \"%.*s\" in class %s", length, bytes,
5845       _class_name->as_C_string()
5846     );
5847     return;
5848   }
5849 }
5850 
5851 
5852 // Checks if signature is a legal field signature.
5853 void ClassFileParser::verify_legal_field_signature(const Symbol* name,
5854                                                    const Symbol* signature,
5855                                                    TRAPS) const {
5856   if (!_need_verify) { return; }
5857 
5858   const char* const bytes = (const char* const)signature->bytes();
5859   const unsigned int length = signature->utf8_length();
5860   const char* const p = skip_over_field_signature(bytes, false, length, CHECK);
5861 
5862   if (p == NULL || (p - bytes) != (int)length) {
5863     throwIllegalSignature("Field", name, signature, CHECK);
5864   }
5865 }
5866 
5867 // Checks if signature is a legal method signature.
5868 // Returns number of parameters
5869 int ClassFileParser::verify_legal_method_signature(const Symbol* name,
5870                                                    const Symbol* signature,
5871                                                    TRAPS) const {
5872   if (!_need_verify) {
5873     // make sure caller's args_size will be less than 0 even for non-static
5874     // method so it will be recomputed in compute_size_of_parameters().
5875     return -2;
5876   }
5877 
5878   // Class initializers cannot have args for class format version >= 51.
5879   if (name == vmSymbols::class_initializer_name() &&
5880       signature != vmSymbols::void_method_signature() &&
5881       _major_version >= JAVA_7_VERSION) {
5882     throwIllegalSignature("Method", name, signature, CHECK_0);
5883     return 0;
5884   }
5885 
5886   unsigned int args_size = 0;
5887   const char* p = (const char*)signature->bytes();
5888   unsigned int length = signature->utf8_length();
5889   const char* nextp;
5890 
5891   // The first character must be a '('
5892   if ((length > 0) && (*p++ == JVM_SIGNATURE_FUNC)) {
5893     length--;
5894     // Skip over legal field signatures
5895     nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, false, length, CHECK_0);
5896     while ((length > 0) && (nextp != NULL)) {
5897       args_size++;
5898       if (p[0] == 'J' || p[0] == 'D') {
5899         args_size++;
5900       }
5901       length -= nextp - p;
5902       p = nextp;
5903       nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, false, length, CHECK_0);
5904     }
5905     // The first non-signature thing better be a ')'
5906     if ((length > 0) && (*p++ == JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDFUNC)) {
5907       length--;
5908       if (name->utf8_length() > 0 && name->char_at(0) == JVM_SIGNATURE_SPECIAL) {
5909         // All constructor methods must return void
5910         if ((length == 1) && (p[0] == JVM_SIGNATURE_VOID)) {
5911           return args_size;
5912         }
5913         // All static init methods must return the current class
5914         if ((length >= 3) && (p[length-1] == JVM_SIGNATURE_ENDCLASS)
5915             && name == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name()) {
5916           nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, true, length, CHECK_0);
5917           if (nextp && ((int)length == (nextp - p))) {
5918             // The actual class will be checked against current class
5919             // when the method is defined (see parse_method).
5920             // A reference to a static init with a bad return type
5921             // will load and verify OK, but will fail to link.
5922             return args_size;
5923           }
5924         }
5925         // The distinction between static factory methods and
5926         // constructors depends on the JVM_ACC_STATIC modifier.
5927         // This distinction must be reflected in a void or non-void
5928         // return. For declared methods, the check is in parse_method.
5929       } else {
5930         // Now we better just have a return value
5931         nextp = skip_over_field_signature(p, true, length, CHECK_0);
5932         if (nextp && ((int)length == (nextp - p))) {
5933           return args_size;
5934         }
5935       }
5936     }
5937   }
5938   // Report error
5939   throwIllegalSignature("Method", name, signature, CHECK_0);
5940   return 0;
5941 }
5942 
5943 int ClassFileParser::static_field_size() const {
5944   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
5945   return _field_info->_static_field_size;
5946 }
5947 
5948 int ClassFileParser::total_oop_map_count() const {
5949   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
5950   return _field_info->oop_map_blocks->_nonstatic_oop_map_count;
5951 }
5952 
5953 jint ClassFileParser::layout_size() const {
5954   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
5955   return _field_info->_instance_size;
5956 }
5957 
5958 static void check_methods_for_intrinsics(const InstanceKlass* ik,
5959                                          const Array<Method*>* methods) {
5960   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
5961   assert(methods != NULL, "invariant");
5962 
5963   // Set up Method*::intrinsic_id as soon as we know the names of methods.
5964   // (We used to do this lazily, but now we query it in Rewriter,
5965   // which is eagerly done for every method, so we might as well do it now,
5966   // when everything is fresh in memory.)
5967   const vmSymbols::SID klass_id = Method::klass_id_for_intrinsics(ik);
5968 
5969   if (klass_id != vmSymbols::NO_SID) {
5970     for (int j = 0; j < methods->length(); ++j) {
5971       Method* method = methods->at(j);
5972       method->init_intrinsic_id();
5973 
5974       if (CheckIntrinsics) {
5975         // Check if an intrinsic is defined for method 'method',
5976         // but the method is not annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate.
5977         if (method->intrinsic_id() != vmIntrinsics::_none &&
5978             !method->intrinsic_candidate()) {
5979               tty->print("Compiler intrinsic is defined for method [%s], "
5980               "but the method is not annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate.%s",
5981               method->name_and_sig_as_C_string(),
5982               NOT_DEBUG(" Method will not be inlined.") DEBUG_ONLY(" Exiting.")
5983             );
5984           tty->cr();
5985           DEBUG_ONLY(vm_exit(1));
5986         }
5987         // Check is the method 'method' is annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate,
5988         // but there is no intrinsic available for it.
5989         if (method->intrinsic_candidate() &&
5990           method->intrinsic_id() == vmIntrinsics::_none) {
5991             tty->print("Method [%s] is annotated with @HotSpotIntrinsicCandidate, "
5992               "but no compiler intrinsic is defined for the method.%s",
5993               method->name_and_sig_as_C_string(),
5994               NOT_DEBUG("") DEBUG_ONLY(" Exiting.")
5995             );
5996           tty->cr();
5997           DEBUG_ONLY(vm_exit(1));
5998         }
5999       }
6000     } // end for
6001 
6002 #ifdef ASSERT
6003     if (CheckIntrinsics) {
6004       // Check for orphan methods in the current class. A method m
6005       // of a class C is orphan if an intrinsic is defined for method m,
6006       // but class C does not declare m.
6007       // The check is potentially expensive, therefore it is available
6008       // only in debug builds.
6009 
6010       for (int id = vmIntrinsics::FIRST_ID; id < (int)vmIntrinsics::ID_LIMIT; ++id) {
6011         if (vmIntrinsics::_compiledLambdaForm == id) {
6012           // The _compiledLamdbdaForm intrinsic is a special marker for bytecode
6013           // generated for the JVM from a LambdaForm and therefore no method
6014           // is defined for it.
6015           continue;
6016         }
6017 
6018         if (vmIntrinsics::class_for(vmIntrinsics::ID_from(id)) == klass_id) {
6019           // Check if the current class contains a method with the same
6020           // name, flags, signature.
6021           bool match = false;
6022           for (int j = 0; j < methods->length(); ++j) {
6023             const Method* method = methods->at(j);
6024             if (method->intrinsic_id() == id) {
6025               match = true;
6026               break;
6027             }
6028           }
6029 
6030           if (!match) {
6031             char buf[1000];
6032             tty->print("Compiler intrinsic is defined for method [%s], "
6033                        "but the method is not available in class [%s].%s",
6034                         vmIntrinsics::short_name_as_C_string(vmIntrinsics::ID_from(id),
6035                                                              buf, sizeof(buf)),
6036                         ik->name()->as_C_string(),
6037                         NOT_DEBUG("") DEBUG_ONLY(" Exiting.")
6038             );
6039             tty->cr();
6040             DEBUG_ONLY(vm_exit(1));
6041           }
6042         }
6043       } // end for
6044     } // CheckIntrinsics
6045 #endif // ASSERT
6046   }
6047 }
6048 
6049 // Called from a factory method in KlassFactory, not from this file.
6050 InstanceKlass* ClassFileParser::create_instance_klass(bool changed_by_loadhook, TRAPS) {
6051   if (_klass != NULL) {
6052     return _klass;
6053   }
6054 
6055   InstanceKlass* const ik =
6056     InstanceKlass::allocate_instance_klass(*this, CHECK_NULL);
6057 
6058   fill_instance_klass(ik, changed_by_loadhook, CHECK_NULL);
6059   assert(_klass == ik, "invariant");
6060 
6061 
6062   if (ik->should_store_fingerprint()) {
6063     ik->store_fingerprint(_stream->compute_fingerprint());
6064   }
6065 
6066   ik->set_has_passed_fingerprint_check(false);
6067   if (UseAOT && ik->supers_have_passed_fingerprint_checks()) {
6068     uint64_t aot_fp = AOTLoader::get_saved_fingerprint(ik);
6069     uint64_t fp = ik->has_stored_fingerprint() ? ik->get_stored_fingerprint() : _stream->compute_fingerprint();
6070     if (aot_fp != 0 && aot_fp == fp) {
6071       // This class matches with a class saved in an AOT library
6072       ik->set_has_passed_fingerprint_check(true);
6073     } else {
6074       ResourceMark rm;
6075       log_info(class, fingerprint)("%s :  expected = " PTR64_FORMAT " actual = " PTR64_FORMAT,
6076                                  ik->external_name(), aot_fp, _stream->compute_fingerprint());
6077     }
6078   }
6079 
6080   if (ik->is_value()) {
6081     ValueKlass* vk = ValueKlass::cast(ik);
6082     oop val = ik->allocate_instance(CHECK_NULL);
6083     vk->set_default_value(val);
6084   }
6085 
6086   return ik;
6087 }
6088 
6089 // Return true if the specified class is not a valid super class for an inline type.
6090 // A valid super class for an inline type is abstract, has no instance fields,
6091 // does not implement interface java.lang.IdentityObject (checked elsewhere), has
6092 // an empty body-less no-arg constructor, and no synchronized instance methods.
6093 // This function doesn't check if the class's super types are invalid.  Those checks
6094 // are done elsewhere.  The final determination of whether or not a class is an
6095 // invalid super type for an inline class is done in fill_instance_klass().
6096 bool ClassFileParser::is_invalid_super_for_inline_type() {
6097   if (class_name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_IdentityObject()) {
6098     return true;
6099   }
6100   if (is_interface() || class_name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object()) {
6101     return false;
6102   }
6103   if (!access_flags().is_abstract() || _has_nonstatic_fields) {
6104     return true;
6105   } else {
6106     // Look at each method
6107     for (int x = 0; x < _methods->length(); x++) {
6108       const Method* const method = _methods->at(x);
6109       if (method->is_synchronized() && !method->is_static()) {
6110         return true;
6111 
6112       } else if (method->name() == vmSymbols::object_initializer_name()) {
6113         if (method->signature() != vmSymbols::void_method_signature() ||
6114             !method->is_vanilla_constructor()) {
6115           return true;
6116         }
6117       }
6118     }
6119   }
6120   return false;
6121 }
6122 
6123 void ClassFileParser::fill_instance_klass(InstanceKlass* ik, bool changed_by_loadhook, TRAPS) {
6124   assert(ik != NULL, "invariant");
6125 
6126   // Set name and CLD before adding to CLD
6127   ik->set_class_loader_data(_loader_data);
6128   ik->set_name(_class_name);
6129 
6130   // Add all classes to our internal class loader list here,
6131   // including classes in the bootstrap (NULL) class loader.
6132   const bool publicize = !is_internal();
6133 
6134   _loader_data->add_class(ik, publicize);
6135 
6136   set_klass_to_deallocate(ik);
6137 
6138   assert(_field_info != NULL, "invariant");
6139   assert(ik->static_field_size() == _field_info->_static_field_size, "sanity");
6140   assert(ik->nonstatic_oop_map_count() == _field_info->oop_map_blocks->_nonstatic_oop_map_count,
6141          "sanity");
6142 
6143   assert(ik->is_instance_klass(), "sanity");
6144   assert(ik->size_helper() == _field_info->_instance_size, "sanity");
6145 
6146   // Fill in information already parsed
6147   ik->set_should_verify_class(_need_verify);
6148 
6149   // Not yet: supers are done below to support the new subtype-checking fields
6150   ik->set_nonstatic_field_size(_field_info->_nonstatic_field_size);
6151   ik->set_has_nonstatic_fields(_field_info->_has_nonstatic_fields);
6152   if (_field_info->_is_naturally_atomic && ik->is_value()) {
6153     ik->set_is_naturally_atomic();
6154   }
6155   if (_is_empty_value) {
6156     ik->set_is_empty_value();
6157   }
6158 
6159   if (this->_invalid_inline_super) {
6160     ik->set_invalid_inline_super();
6161   }
6162 
6163   if (_has_injected_identityObject) {
6164     ik->set_has_injected_identityObject();
6165   }
6166 
6167   assert(_fac != NULL, "invariant");
6168   ik->set_static_oop_field_count(_fac->count[STATIC_OOP] + _fac->count[STATIC_FLATTENABLE]);
6169 
6170   // this transfers ownership of a lot of arrays from
6171   // the parser onto the InstanceKlass*
6172   apply_parsed_class_metadata(ik, _java_fields_count, CHECK);
6173 
6174   // note that is not safe to use the fields in the parser from this point on
6175   assert(NULL == _cp, "invariant");
6176   assert(NULL == _fields, "invariant");
6177   assert(NULL == _methods, "invariant");
6178   assert(NULL == _inner_classes, "invariant");
6179   assert(NULL == _nest_members, "invariant");
6180   assert(NULL == _local_interfaces, "invariant");
6181   assert(NULL == _combined_annotations, "invariant");
6182   assert(NULL == _record_components, "invariant");
6183 
6184   if (_has_final_method) {
6185     ik->set_has_final_method();
6186   }
6187 
6188   ik->copy_method_ordering(_method_ordering, CHECK);
6189   // The InstanceKlass::_methods_jmethod_ids cache
6190   // is managed on the assumption that the initial cache
6191   // size is equal to the number of methods in the class. If
6192   // that changes, then InstanceKlass::idnum_can_increment()
6193   // has to be changed accordingly.
6194   ik->set_initial_method_idnum(ik->methods()->length());
6195 
6196   ik->set_this_class_index(_this_class_index);
6197 
6198   if (is_unsafe_anonymous()) {
6199     // _this_class_index is a CONSTANT_Class entry that refers to this
6200     // anonymous class itself. If this class needs to refer to its own methods or
6201     // fields, it would use a CONSTANT_MethodRef, etc, which would reference
6202     // _this_class_index. However, because this class is anonymous (it's
6203     // not stored in SystemDictionary), _this_class_index cannot be resolved
6204     // with ConstantPool::klass_at_impl, which does a SystemDictionary lookup.
6205     // Therefore, we must eagerly resolve _this_class_index now.
6206     ik->constants()->klass_at_put(_this_class_index, ik);
6207   }
6208 
6209   ik->set_minor_version(_minor_version);
6210   ik->set_major_version(_major_version);
6211   ik->set_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods(_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods);
6212   ik->set_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods(_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods);
6213   if (_is_declared_atomic) {
6214     ik->set_is_declared_atomic();
6215   }
6216 
6217   if (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL) {
6218     assert (ik->is_unsafe_anonymous(), "should be the same");
6219     ik->set_unsafe_anonymous_host(_unsafe_anonymous_host);
6220   }
6221 
6222   // Set PackageEntry for this_klass
6223   oop cl = ik->class_loader();
6224   Handle clh = Handle(THREAD, java_lang_ClassLoader::non_reflection_class_loader(cl));
6225   ClassLoaderData* cld = ClassLoaderData::class_loader_data_or_null(clh());
6226   ik->set_package(cld, NULL, CHECK);
6227 
6228   const Array<Method*>* const methods = ik->methods();
6229   assert(methods != NULL, "invariant");
6230   const int methods_len = methods->length();
6231 
6232   check_methods_for_intrinsics(ik, methods);
6233 
6234   // Fill in field values obtained by parse_classfile_attributes
6235   if (_parsed_annotations->has_any_annotations()) {
6236     _parsed_annotations->apply_to(ik);
6237   }
6238 
6239   apply_parsed_class_attributes(ik);
6240 
6241   // Miranda methods
6242   if ((_num_miranda_methods > 0) ||
6243       // if this class introduced new miranda methods or
6244       (_super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->has_miranda_methods())
6245         // super class exists and this class inherited miranda methods
6246      ) {
6247        ik->set_has_miranda_methods(); // then set a flag
6248   }
6249 
6250   // Fill in information needed to compute superclasses.
6251   ik->initialize_supers(const_cast<InstanceKlass*>(_super_klass), _transitive_interfaces, CHECK);
6252   ik->set_transitive_interfaces(_transitive_interfaces);
6253   _transitive_interfaces = NULL;
6254 
6255   // Initialize itable offset tables
6256   klassItable::setup_itable_offset_table(ik);
6257 
6258   // Compute transitive closure of interfaces this class implements
6259   // Do final class setup
6260   OopMapBlocksBuilder* oop_map_blocks = _field_info->oop_map_blocks;
6261   if (oop_map_blocks->_nonstatic_oop_map_count > 0) {
6262     oop_map_blocks->copy(ik->start_of_nonstatic_oop_maps());
6263   }
6264 
6265   if (_has_contended_fields || _parsed_annotations->is_contended() ||
6266       ( _super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->has_contended_annotations())) {
6267     ik->set_has_contended_annotations(true);
6268   }
6269 
6270   // Fill in has_finalizer, has_vanilla_constructor, and layout_helper
6271   set_precomputed_flags(ik);
6272 
6273   // check if this class can access its super class
6274   check_super_class_access(ik, CHECK);
6275 
6276   // check if this class can access its superinterfaces
6277   check_super_interface_access(ik, CHECK);
6278 
6279   // check if this class overrides any final method
6280   check_final_method_override(ik, CHECK);
6281 
6282   // reject static interface methods prior to Java 8
6283   if (ik->is_interface() && _major_version < JAVA_8_VERSION) {
6284     check_illegal_static_method(ik, CHECK);
6285   }
6286 
6287   // Obtain this_klass' module entry
6288   ModuleEntry* module_entry = ik->module();
6289   assert(module_entry != NULL, "module_entry should always be set");
6290 
6291   // Obtain java.lang.Module
6292   Handle module_handle(THREAD, module_entry->module());
6293 
6294   // Allocate mirror and initialize static fields
6295   // The create_mirror() call will also call compute_modifiers()
6296   java_lang_Class::create_mirror(ik,
6297                                  Handle(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader()),
6298                                  module_handle,
6299                                  _protection_domain,
6300                                  CHECK);
6301 
6302   assert(_all_mirandas != NULL, "invariant");
6303 
6304   // Generate any default methods - default methods are public interface methods
6305   // that have a default implementation.  This is new with Java 8.
6306   if (_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods) {
6307     DefaultMethods::generate_default_methods(ik,
6308                                              _all_mirandas,
6309                                              CHECK);
6310   }
6311 
6312   // Add read edges to the unnamed modules of the bootstrap and app class loaders.
6313   if (changed_by_loadhook && !module_handle.is_null() && module_entry->is_named() &&
6314       !module_entry->has_default_read_edges()) {
6315     if (!module_entry->set_has_default_read_edges()) {
6316       // We won a potential race
6317       JvmtiExport::add_default_read_edges(module_handle, THREAD);
6318     }
6319   }
6320 
6321   int nfields = ik->java_fields_count();
6322   if (ik->is_value()) nfields++;
6323   for (int i = 0; i < nfields; i++) {
6324     if (ik->field_is_flattenable(i)) {
6325       Symbol* klass_name = ik->field_signature(i)->fundamental_name(CHECK);
6326       // Inline classes for instance fields must have been pre-loaded
6327       // Inline classes for static fields might not have been loaded yet
6328       Klass* klass = SystemDictionary::find(klass_name,
6329           Handle(THREAD, ik->class_loader()),
6330           Handle(THREAD, ik->protection_domain()), CHECK);
6331       if (klass != NULL) {
6332         assert(klass->access_flags().is_value_type(), "Value type expected");
6333         ik->set_value_field_klass(i, klass);
6334       }
6335       klass_name->decrement_refcount();
6336     } else
6337       if (is_value_type() && ((ik->field_access_flags(i) & JVM_ACC_FIELD_INTERNAL) != 0)
6338         && ((ik->field_access_flags(i) & JVM_ACC_STATIC) != 0)) {
6339       ValueKlass::cast(ik)->set_default_value_offset(ik->field_offset(i));
6340     }
6341   }
6342 
6343   if (is_value_type()) {
6344     ValueKlass* vk = ValueKlass::cast(ik);
6345     if (UseNewFieldLayout) {
6346       vk->set_alignment(_alignment);
6347       vk->set_first_field_offset(_first_field_offset);
6348       vk->set_exact_size_in_bytes(_exact_size_in_bytes);
6349     } else {
6350       vk->set_first_field_offset(vk->first_field_offset_old());
6351     }
6352     ValueKlass::cast(ik)->initialize_calling_convention(CHECK);
6353   }
6354 
6355   ClassLoadingService::notify_class_loaded(ik, false /* not shared class */);
6356 
6357   if (!is_internal()) {
6358     if (log_is_enabled(Info, class, load)) {
6359       ResourceMark rm;
6360       const char* module_name = (module_entry->name() == NULL) ? UNNAMED_MODULE : module_entry->name()->as_C_string();
6361       ik->print_class_load_logging(_loader_data, module_name, _stream);
6362     }
6363 
6364     if (ik->minor_version() == JAVA_PREVIEW_MINOR_VERSION &&
6365         ik->major_version() == JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION &&
6366         log_is_enabled(Info, class, preview)) {
6367       ResourceMark rm;
6368       log_info(class, preview)("Loading class %s that depends on preview features (class file version %d.65535)",
6369                                ik->external_name(), JVM_CLASSFILE_MAJOR_VERSION);
6370     }
6371 
6372     if (log_is_enabled(Debug, class, resolve))  {
6373       ResourceMark rm;
6374       // print out the superclass.
6375       const char * from = ik->external_name();
6376       if (ik->java_super() != NULL) {
6377         log_debug(class, resolve)("%s %s (super)",
6378                    from,
6379                    ik->java_super()->external_name());
6380       }
6381       // print out each of the interface classes referred to by this class.
6382       const Array<InstanceKlass*>* const local_interfaces = ik->local_interfaces();
6383       if (local_interfaces != NULL) {
6384         const int length = local_interfaces->length();
6385         for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {
6386           const InstanceKlass* const k = local_interfaces->at(i);
6387           const char * to = k->external_name();
6388           log_debug(class, resolve)("%s %s (interface)", from, to);
6389         }
6390       }
6391     }
6392   }
6393 
6394   JFR_ONLY(INIT_ID(ik);)
6395 
6396   // If we reach here, all is well.
6397   // Now remove the InstanceKlass* from the _klass_to_deallocate field
6398   // in order for it to not be destroyed in the ClassFileParser destructor.
6399   set_klass_to_deallocate(NULL);
6400 
6401   // it's official
6402   set_klass(ik);
6403 
6404   if (ik->name() == vmSymbols::java_lang_IdentityObject()) {
6405     Universe::initialize_the_single_IdentityObject_klass_array(ik, CHECK);
6406   }
6407 
6408   debug_only(ik->verify();)
6409 }
6410 
6411 void ClassFileParser::update_class_name(Symbol* new_class_name) {
6412   // Decrement the refcount in the old name, since we're clobbering it.
6413   _class_name->decrement_refcount();
6414 
6415   _class_name = new_class_name;
6416   // Increment the refcount of the new name.
6417   // Now the ClassFileParser owns this name and will decrement in
6418   // the destructor.
6419   _class_name->increment_refcount();
6420 }
6421 
6422 
6423 // For an unsafe anonymous class that is in the unnamed package, move it to its host class's
6424 // package by prepending its host class's package name to its class name and setting
6425 // its _class_name field.
6426 void ClassFileParser::prepend_host_package_name(const InstanceKlass* unsafe_anonymous_host, TRAPS) {
6427   ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6428   assert(strrchr(_class_name->as_C_string(), JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH) == NULL,
6429          "Unsafe anonymous class should not be in a package");
6430   TempNewSymbol host_pkg_name =
6431     ClassLoader::package_from_class_name(unsafe_anonymous_host->name());
6432 
6433   if (host_pkg_name != NULL) {
6434     int host_pkg_len = host_pkg_name->utf8_length();
6435     int class_name_len = _class_name->utf8_length();
6436     int symbol_len = host_pkg_len + 1 + class_name_len;
6437     char* new_anon_name = NEW_RESOURCE_ARRAY(char, symbol_len + 1);
6438     int n = os::snprintf(new_anon_name, symbol_len + 1, "%.*s/%.*s",
6439                          host_pkg_len, host_pkg_name->base(), class_name_len, _class_name->base());
6440     assert(n == symbol_len, "Unexpected number of characters in string");
6441 
6442     // Decrement old _class_name to avoid leaking.
6443     _class_name->decrement_refcount();
6444 
6445     // Create a symbol and update the anonymous class name.
6446     // The new class name is created with a refcount of one. When installed into the InstanceKlass,
6447     // it'll be two and when the ClassFileParser destructor runs, it'll go back to one and get deleted
6448     // when the class is unloaded.
6449     _class_name = SymbolTable::new_symbol(new_anon_name, symbol_len);
6450   }
6451 }
6452 
6453 // If the host class and the anonymous class are in the same package then do
6454 // nothing.  If the anonymous class is in the unnamed package then move it to its
6455 // host's package.  If the classes are in different packages then throw an IAE
6456 // exception.
6457 void ClassFileParser::fix_unsafe_anonymous_class_name(TRAPS) {
6458   assert(_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL, "Expected an unsafe anonymous class");
6459 
6460   const jbyte* anon_last_slash = UTF8::strrchr((const jbyte*)_class_name->base(),
6461                                                _class_name->utf8_length(), JVM_SIGNATURE_SLASH);
6462   if (anon_last_slash == NULL) {  // Unnamed package
6463     prepend_host_package_name(_unsafe_anonymous_host, CHECK);
6464   } else {
6465     if (!_unsafe_anonymous_host->is_same_class_package(_unsafe_anonymous_host->class_loader(), _class_name)) {
6466       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6467       THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_IllegalArgumentException(),
6468         err_msg("Host class %s and anonymous class %s are in different packages",
6469         _unsafe_anonymous_host->name()->as_C_string(), _class_name->as_C_string()));
6470     }
6471   }
6472 }
6473 
6474 static bool relax_format_check_for(ClassLoaderData* loader_data) {
6475   bool trusted = (loader_data->is_the_null_class_loader_data() ||
6476                   SystemDictionary::is_platform_class_loader(loader_data->class_loader()));
6477   bool need_verify =
6478     // verifyAll
6479     (BytecodeVerificationLocal && BytecodeVerificationRemote) ||
6480     // verifyRemote
6481     (!BytecodeVerificationLocal && BytecodeVerificationRemote && !trusted);
6482   return !need_verify;
6483 }
