6485 ClassFileParser::ClassFileParser(ClassFileStream* stream,
6486                                  Symbol* name,
6487                                  ClassLoaderData* loader_data,
6488                                  Handle protection_domain,
6489                                  const InstanceKlass* unsafe_anonymous_host,
6490                                  GrowableArray<Handle>* cp_patches,
6491                                  Publicity pub_level,
6492                                  TRAPS) :
6493   _stream(stream),
6494   _requested_name(name),
6495   _class_name(NULL),
6496   _loader_data(loader_data),
6497   _unsafe_anonymous_host(unsafe_anonymous_host),
6498   _cp_patches(cp_patches),
6499   _num_patched_klasses(0),
6500   _max_num_patched_klasses(0),
6501   _orig_cp_size(0),
6502   _first_patched_klass_resolved_index(0),
6503   _super_klass(),
6504   _cp(NULL),
6505   _fields(NULL),
6506   _methods(NULL),
6507   _inner_classes(NULL),
6508   _nest_members(NULL),
6509   _nest_host(0),
6510   _record_components(NULL),
6511   _temp_local_interfaces(NULL),
6512   _local_interfaces(NULL),
6513   _transitive_interfaces(NULL),
6514   _combined_annotations(NULL),
6515   _class_annotations(NULL),
6516   _class_type_annotations(NULL),
6517   _fields_annotations(NULL),
6518   _fields_type_annotations(NULL),
6519   _klass(NULL),
6520   _klass_to_deallocate(NULL),
6521   _parsed_annotations(NULL),
6522   _fac(NULL),
6523   _field_info(NULL),
6524   _method_ordering(NULL),
6525   _all_mirandas(NULL),
6526   _vtable_size(0),
6527   _itable_size(0),
6528   _num_miranda_methods(0),
6529   _rt(REF_NONE),
6530   _protection_domain(protection_domain),
6531   _access_flags(),
6532   _pub_level(pub_level),
6533   _bad_constant_seen(0),
6534   _synthetic_flag(false),
6535   _sde_length(false),
6536   _sde_buffer(NULL),
6537   _sourcefile_index(0),
6538   _generic_signature_index(0),
6539   _major_version(0),
6540   _minor_version(0),
6541   _this_class_index(0),
6542   _super_class_index(0),
6543   _itfs_len(0),
6544   _java_fields_count(0),
6545   _need_verify(false),
6546   _relax_verify(false),
6547   _has_nonstatic_concrete_methods(false),
6548   _declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods(false),
6549   _has_final_method(false),
6550   _has_contended_fields(false),
6551   _has_flattenable_fields(false),
6552   _has_nonstatic_fields(false),
6553   _is_empty_value(false),
6554   _is_naturally_atomic(false),
6555   _is_declared_atomic(false),
6556   _invalid_inline_super(false),
6557   _invalid_identity_super(false),
6558   _implements_identityObject(false),
6559   _has_injected_identityObject(false),
6560   _has_finalizer(false),
6561   _has_empty_finalizer(false),
6562   _has_vanilla_constructor(false),
6563   _max_bootstrap_specifier_index(-1) {
6564 
6565   _class_name = name != NULL ? name : vmSymbols::unknown_class_name();
6566   _class_name->increment_refcount();
6567 
6568   assert(THREAD->is_Java_thread(), "invariant");
6569   assert(_loader_data != NULL, "invariant");
6570   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
6571   assert(_stream != NULL, "invariant");
6572   assert(_stream->buffer() == _stream->current(), "invariant");
6573   assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
6574   assert(0 == _access_flags.as_int(), "invariant");
6575 
6576   // Figure out whether we can skip format checking (matching classic VM behavior)
6577   if (DumpSharedSpaces) {
6578     // verify == true means it's a 'remote' class (i.e., non-boot class)
6579     // Verification decision is based on BytecodeVerificationRemote flag
6580     // for those classes.
6581     _need_verify = (stream->need_verify()) ? BytecodeVerificationRemote :
6582                                               BytecodeVerificationLocal;
6583   }
6584   else {
6585     _need_verify = Verifier::should_verify_for(_loader_data->class_loader(),
6586                                                stream->need_verify());
6587   }
6588   if (_cp_patches != NULL) {
6589     int len = _cp_patches->length();
6590     for (int i=0; i<len; i++) {
6591       if (has_cp_patch_at(i)) {
6592         Handle patch = cp_patch_at(i);
6593         if (java_lang_String::is_instance(patch()) || java_lang_Class::is_instance(patch())) {
6594           // We need to append the names of the patched classes to the end of the constant pool,
6595           // because a patched class may have a Utf8 name that's not already included in the
6596           // original constant pool. These class names are used when patch_constant_pool()
6597           // calls patch_class().
6598           //
6599           // Note that a String in cp_patch_at(i) may be used to patch a Utf8, a String, or a Class.
6600           // At this point, we don't know the tag for index i yet, because we haven't parsed the
6601           // constant pool. So we can only assume the worst -- every String is used to patch a Class.
6602           _max_num_patched_klasses++;
6603         }
6604       }
6605     }
6606   }
6607 
6608   // synch back verification state to stream
6609   stream->set_verify(_need_verify);
6610 
6611   // Check if verification needs to be relaxed for this class file
6612   // Do not restrict it to jdk1.0 or jdk1.1 to maintain backward compatibility (4982376)
6613   _relax_verify = relax_format_check_for(_loader_data);
6614 
6615   parse_stream(stream, CHECK);
6616 
6617   post_process_parsed_stream(stream, _cp, CHECK);
6618 }
6619 
6620 void ClassFileParser::clear_class_metadata() {
6621   // metadata created before the instance klass is created.  Must be
6622   // deallocated if classfile parsing returns an error.
6623   _cp = NULL;
6624   _fields = NULL;
6625   _methods = NULL;
6626   _inner_classes = NULL;
6627   _nest_members = NULL;
6628   _local_interfaces = NULL;
6629   _combined_annotations = NULL;
6630   _class_annotations = _class_type_annotations = NULL;
6631   _fields_annotations = _fields_type_annotations = NULL;
6632   _record_components = NULL;
6633 }
6634 
6635 // Destructor to clean up
6636 ClassFileParser::~ClassFileParser() {
6637   _class_name->decrement_refcount();
6638 
6639   if (_cp != NULL) {
6640     MetadataFactory::free_metadata(_loader_data, _cp);
6641   }
6642   if (_fields != NULL) {
6643     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _fields);
6644   }
6645 
6646   if (_methods != NULL) {
6647     // Free methods
6648     InstanceKlass::deallocate_methods(_loader_data, _methods);
6649   }
6650 
6651   // beware of the Universe::empty_blah_array!!
6652   if (_inner_classes != NULL && _inner_classes != Universe::the_empty_short_array()) {
6653     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _inner_classes);
6654   }
6655 
6656   if (_nest_members != NULL && _nest_members != Universe::the_empty_short_array()) {
6657     MetadataFactory::free_array<u2>(_loader_data, _nest_members);
6658   }
6659 
6660   if (_record_components != NULL) {
6661     InstanceKlass::deallocate_record_components(_loader_data, _record_components);
6662   }
6663 
6664   // Free interfaces
6665   InstanceKlass::deallocate_interfaces(_loader_data, _super_klass,
6666                                        _local_interfaces, _transitive_interfaces);
6667 
6668   if (_combined_annotations != NULL) {
6669     // After all annotations arrays have been created, they are installed into the
6670     // Annotations object that will be assigned to the InstanceKlass being created.
6671 
6672     // Deallocate the Annotations object and the installed annotations arrays.
6673     _combined_annotations->deallocate_contents(_loader_data);
6674 
6675     // If the _combined_annotations pointer is non-NULL,
6676     // then the other annotations fields should have been cleared.
6677     assert(_class_annotations       == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6678     assert(_class_type_annotations  == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6679     assert(_fields_annotations      == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6680     assert(_fields_type_annotations == NULL, "Should have been cleared");
6681   } else {
6682     // If the annotations arrays were not installed into the Annotations object,
6683     // then they have to be deallocated explicitly.
6684     MetadataFactory::free_array<u1>(_loader_data, _class_annotations);
6685     MetadataFactory::free_array<u1>(_loader_data, _class_type_annotations);
6686     Annotations::free_contents(_loader_data, _fields_annotations);
6687     Annotations::free_contents(_loader_data, _fields_type_annotations);
6688   }
6689 
6690   clear_class_metadata();
6691   _transitive_interfaces = NULL;
6692 
6693   // deallocate the klass if already created.  Don't directly deallocate, but add
6694   // to the deallocate list so that the klass is removed from the CLD::_klasses list
6695   // at a safepoint.
6696   if (_klass_to_deallocate != NULL) {
6697     _loader_data->add_to_deallocate_list(_klass_to_deallocate);
6698   }
6699 }
6700 
6701 void ClassFileParser::parse_stream(const ClassFileStream* const stream,
6702                                    TRAPS) {
6703 
6704   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
6705   assert(_class_name != NULL, "invariant");
6706 
6707   // BEGIN STREAM PARSING
6708   stream->guarantee_more(8, CHECK);  // magic, major, minor
6709   // Magic value
6710   const u4 magic = stream->get_u4_fast();
6711   guarantee_property(magic == JAVA_CLASSFILE_MAGIC,
6712                      "Incompatible magic value %u in class file %s",
6713                      magic, CHECK);
6714 
6715   // Version numbers
6716   _minor_version = stream->get_u2_fast();
6717   _major_version = stream->get_u2_fast();
6718 
6719   if (DumpSharedSpaces && _major_version < JAVA_6_VERSION) {
6720     ResourceMark rm;
6721     warning("Pre JDK 6 class not supported by CDS: %u.%u %s",
6722             _major_version,  _minor_version, _class_name->as_C_string());
6723     Exceptions::fthrow(
6724       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
6725       vmSymbols::java_lang_UnsupportedClassVersionError(),
6726       "Unsupported major.minor version for dump time %u.%u",
6727       _major_version,
6728       _minor_version);
6729   }
6730 
6731   // Check version numbers - we check this even with verifier off
6732   verify_class_version(_major_version, _minor_version, _class_name, CHECK);
6733 
6734   stream->guarantee_more(3, CHECK); // length, first cp tag
6735   u2 cp_size = stream->get_u2_fast();
6736 
6737   guarantee_property(
6738     cp_size >= 1, "Illegal constant pool size %u in class file %s",
6739     cp_size, CHECK);
6740 
6741   _orig_cp_size = cp_size;
6742   if (int(cp_size) + _max_num_patched_klasses > 0xffff) {
6743     THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_InternalError(), "not enough space for patched classes");
6744   }
6745   cp_size += _max_num_patched_klasses;
6746 
6747   _cp = ConstantPool::allocate(_loader_data,
6748                                cp_size,
6749                                CHECK);
6750 
6751   ConstantPool* const cp = _cp;
6752 
6753   parse_constant_pool(stream, cp, _orig_cp_size, CHECK);
6754 
6755   assert(cp_size == (const u2)cp->length(), "invariant");
6756 
6757   // ACCESS FLAGS
6758   stream->guarantee_more(8, CHECK);  // flags, this_class, super_class, infs_len
6759 
6760   jint recognized_modifiers = JVM_RECOGNIZED_CLASS_MODIFIERS;
6761   // JVM_ACC_MODULE is defined in JDK-9 and later.
6762   if (_major_version >= JAVA_9_VERSION) {
6763     recognized_modifiers |= JVM_ACC_MODULE;
6764   }
6765   // JVM_ACC_VALUE is defined for class file version 55 and later
6766   if (supports_value_types()) {
6767     recognized_modifiers |= JVM_ACC_VALUE;
6768   }
6769 
6770   // Access flags
6771   jint flags = stream->get_u2_fast() & recognized_modifiers;
6772 
6773   if ((flags & JVM_ACC_INTERFACE) && _major_version < JAVA_6_VERSION) {
6774     // Set abstract bit for old class files for backward compatibility
6775     flags |= JVM_ACC_ABSTRACT;
6776   }
6777 
6778   verify_legal_class_modifiers(flags, CHECK);
6779 
6780   short bad_constant = class_bad_constant_seen();
6781   if (bad_constant != 0) {
6782     // Do not throw CFE until after the access_flags are checked because if
6783     // ACC_MODULE is set in the access flags, then NCDFE must be thrown, not CFE.
6784     classfile_parse_error("Unknown constant tag %u in class file %s", bad_constant, CHECK);
6785   }
6786 
6787   _access_flags.set_flags(flags);
6788 
6789   // This class and superclass
6790   _this_class_index = stream->get_u2_fast();
6791   check_property(
6792     valid_cp_range(_this_class_index, cp_size) &&
6793       cp->tag_at(_this_class_index).is_unresolved_klass(),
6794     "Invalid this class index %u in constant pool in class file %s",
6795     _this_class_index, CHECK);
6796 
6797   Symbol* const class_name_in_cp = cp->klass_name_at(_this_class_index);
6798   assert(class_name_in_cp != NULL, "class_name can't be null");
6799 
6800   // Update _class_name to reflect the name in the constant pool
6801   update_class_name(class_name_in_cp);
6802 
6803   // Don't need to check whether this class name is legal or not.
6804   // It has been checked when constant pool is parsed.
6805   // However, make sure it is not an array type.
6806   if (_need_verify) {
6807     guarantee_property(_class_name->char_at(0) != JVM_SIGNATURE_ARRAY,
6808                        "Bad class name in class file %s",
6809                        CHECK);
6810   }
6811 
6812   // Checks if name in class file matches requested name
6813   if (_requested_name != NULL && _requested_name != _class_name) {
6814     ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6815     Exceptions::fthrow(
6816       THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
6817       vmSymbols::java_lang_NoClassDefFoundError(),
6818       "%s (wrong name: %s)",
6819       _class_name->as_C_string(),
6820       _requested_name != NULL ? _requested_name->as_C_string() : "NoName"
6821     );
6822     return;
6823   }
6824 
6825   // if this is an anonymous class fix up its name if it's in the unnamed
6826   // package.  Otherwise, throw IAE if it is in a different package than
6827   // its host class.
6828   if (_unsafe_anonymous_host != NULL) {
6829     fix_unsafe_anonymous_class_name(CHECK);
6830   }
6831 
6832   // Verification prevents us from creating names with dots in them, this
6833   // asserts that that's the case.
6834   assert(is_internal_format(_class_name), "external class name format used internally");
6835 
6836   if (!is_internal()) {
6837     LogTarget(Debug, class, preorder) lt;
6838     if (lt.is_enabled()){
6839       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6840       LogStream ls(lt);
6841       ls.print("%s", _class_name->as_klass_external_name());
6842       if (stream->source() != NULL) {
6843         ls.print(" source: %s", stream->source());
6844       }
6845       ls.cr();
6846     }
6847 
6848 #if INCLUDE_CDS
6849     if (DumpLoadedClassList != NULL && stream->source() != NULL && classlist_file->is_open()) {
6850       if (!ClassLoader::has_jrt_entry()) {
6851         warning("DumpLoadedClassList and CDS are not supported in exploded build");
6852         DumpLoadedClassList = NULL;
6853       } else if (SystemDictionaryShared::is_sharing_possible(_loader_data) &&
6854                  _unsafe_anonymous_host == NULL) {
6855         // Only dump the classes that can be stored into CDS archive.
6856         // Unsafe anonymous classes such as generated LambdaForm classes are also not included.
6857         oop class_loader = _loader_data->class_loader();
6858         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6859         bool skip = false;
6860         if (class_loader == NULL || SystemDictionary::is_platform_class_loader(class_loader)) {
6861           // For the boot and platform class loaders, skip classes that are not found in the
6862           // java runtime image, such as those found in the --patch-module entries.
6863           // These classes can't be loaded from the archive during runtime.
6864           if (!stream->from_boot_loader_modules_image() && strncmp(stream->source(), "jrt:", 4) != 0) {
6865             skip = true;
6866           }
6867 
6868           if (class_loader == NULL && ClassLoader::contains_append_entry(stream->source())) {
6869             // .. but don't skip the boot classes that are loaded from -Xbootclasspath/a
6870             // as they can be loaded from the archive during runtime.
6871             skip = false;
6872           }
6873         }
6874         if (skip) {
6875           tty->print_cr("skip writing class %s from source %s to classlist file",
6876             _class_name->as_C_string(), stream->source());
6877         } else {
6878           classlist_file->print_cr("%s", _class_name->as_C_string());
6879           classlist_file->flush();
6880         }
6881       }
6882     }
6883 #endif
6884   }
6885 
6886   // SUPERKLASS
6887   _super_class_index = stream->get_u2_fast();
6888   _super_klass = parse_super_class(cp,
6889                                    _super_class_index,
6890                                    _need_verify,
6891                                    CHECK);
6892 
6893   // Interfaces
6894   _itfs_len = stream->get_u2_fast();
6895   parse_interfaces(stream,
6896                    _itfs_len,
6897                    cp,
6898                    is_value_type(),
6899                    &_has_nonstatic_concrete_methods,
6900                    &_is_declared_atomic,
6901                    CHECK);
6902 
6903   assert(_temp_local_interfaces != NULL, "invariant");
6904 
6905   // Fields (offsets are filled in later)
6906   _fac = new FieldAllocationCount();
6907   parse_fields(stream,
6908                is_interface(),
6909                is_value_type(),
6910                _fac,
6911                cp,
6912                cp_size,
6913                &_java_fields_count,
6914                CHECK);
6915 
6916   assert(_fields != NULL, "invariant");
6917 
6918   // Methods
6919   AccessFlags promoted_flags;
6920   parse_methods(stream,
6921                 is_interface(),
6922                 is_value_type(),
6923                 &promoted_flags,
6924                 &_has_final_method,
6925                 &_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods,
6926                 CHECK);
6927 
6928   assert(_methods != NULL, "invariant");
6929 
6930   // promote flags from parse_methods() to the klass' flags
6931   _access_flags.add_promoted_flags(promoted_flags.as_int());
6932 
6933   if (_declares_nonstatic_concrete_methods) {
6934     _has_nonstatic_concrete_methods = true;
6935   }
6936 
6937   // Additional attributes/annotations
6938   _parsed_annotations = new ClassAnnotationCollector();
6939   parse_classfile_attributes(stream, cp, _parsed_annotations, CHECK);
6940 
6941   assert(_inner_classes != NULL, "invariant");
6942 
6943   // Finalize the Annotations metadata object,
6944   // now that all annotation arrays have been created.
6945   create_combined_annotations(CHECK);
6946 
6947   // Make sure this is the end of class file stream
6948   guarantee_property(stream->at_eos(),
6949                      "Extra bytes at the end of class file %s",
6950                      CHECK);
6951 
6952   // all bytes in stream read and parsed
6953 }
6954 
6955 void ClassFileParser::post_process_parsed_stream(const ClassFileStream* const stream,
6956                                                  ConstantPool* cp,
6957                                                  TRAPS) {
6958   assert(stream != NULL, "invariant");
6959   assert(stream->at_eos(), "invariant");
6960   assert(cp != NULL, "invariant");
6961   assert(_loader_data != NULL, "invariant");
6962 
6963   if (_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object()) {
6964     check_property(_temp_local_interfaces->length() == 0,
6965         "java.lang.Object cannot implement an interface in class file %s",
6966         CHECK);
6967   }
6968   // We check super class after class file is parsed and format is checked
6969   if (_super_class_index > 0 && NULL ==_super_klass) {
6970     Symbol* const super_class_name = cp->klass_name_at(_super_class_index);
6971     if (is_interface()) {
6972       // Before attempting to resolve the superclass, check for class format
6973       // errors not checked yet.
6974       guarantee_property(super_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_Object(),
6975         "Interfaces must have java.lang.Object as superclass in class file %s",
6976         CHECK);
6977     }
6978     Handle loader(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader());
6979     _super_klass = (const InstanceKlass*)
6980                        SystemDictionary::resolve_super_or_fail(_class_name,
6981                                                                super_class_name,
6982                                                                loader,
6983                                                                _protection_domain,
6984                                                                true,
6985                                                                CHECK);
6986   }
6987 
6988   if (_super_klass != NULL) {
6989     if (_super_klass->has_nonstatic_concrete_methods()) {
6990       _has_nonstatic_concrete_methods = true;
6991     }
6992     if (_super_klass->is_declared_atomic()) {
6993       _is_declared_atomic = true;
6994     }
6995 
6996     if (_super_klass->is_interface()) {
6997       ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
6998       Exceptions::fthrow(
6999         THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
7000         vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError(),
7001         "class %s has interface %s as super class",
7002         _class_name->as_klass_external_name(),
7003         _super_klass->external_name()
7004       );
7005       return;
7006     }
7007 
7008     // Make sure super class is not final
7009     if (_super_klass->is_final()) {
7010       THROW_MSG(vmSymbols::java_lang_VerifyError(), "Cannot inherit from final class");
7011     }
7012 
7013     // For an inline class, only java/lang/Object or special abstract classes
7014     // are acceptable super classes.
7015     if (is_value_type()) {
7016       const InstanceKlass* super_ik = _super_klass;
7017       if (super_ik->invalid_inline_super()) {
7018         ResourceMark rm(THREAD);
7019         Exceptions::fthrow(
7020           THREAD_AND_LOCATION,
7021           vmSymbols::java_lang_IncompatibleClassChangeError(),
7022           "inline class %s has an invalid super class %s",
7023           _class_name->as_klass_external_name(),
7024           _super_klass->external_name());
7025         return;
7026       }
7027     }
7028   }
7029 
7030   if (_class_name == vmSymbols::java_lang_NonTearable() && _loader_data->class_loader() == NULL) {
7031     // This is the original source of this condition.
7032     // It propagates by inheritance, as if testing "instanceof NonTearable".
7033     _is_declared_atomic = true;
7034   } else if (*ForceNonTearable != '\0') {
7035     // Allow a command line switch to force the same atomicity property:
7036     const char* class_name_str = _class_name->as_C_string();
7037     if (StringUtils::class_list_match(ForceNonTearable, class_name_str)) {
7038       _is_declared_atomic = true;
7039     }
7040   }
7041 
7042   // Set ik->invalid_inline_super field to TRUE if already marked as invalid,
7043   // if super is marked invalid, or if is_invalid_super_for_inline_type()
7044   // returns true
7045   if (invalid_inline_super() ||
7046       (_super_klass != NULL && _super_klass->invalid_inline_super()) ||
7047       is_invalid_super_for_inline_type()) {
7048     set_invalid_inline_super();
7049   }
7050 
7051   if (!is_value_type() && invalid_inline_super() && (_super_klass == NULL || !_super_klass->invalid_inline_super())
7052       && !_implements_identityObject && class_name() != vmSymbols::java_lang_IdentityObject()) {
7053     _temp_local_interfaces->append(SystemDictionary::IdentityObject_klass());
7054     _has_injected_identityObject = true;
7055   }
7056   int itfs_len = _temp_local_interfaces->length();
7057   if (itfs_len == 0) {
7058     _local_interfaces = Universe::the_empty_instance_klass_array();
7059   } else if (itfs_len == 1 && _temp_local_interfaces->at(0) == SystemDictionary::IdentityObject_klass()) {
7060     _local_interfaces = Universe::the_single_IdentityObject_klass_array();
7061   } else {
7062     _local_interfaces = MetadataFactory::new_array<InstanceKlass*>(_loader_data, itfs_len, NULL, CHECK);
7063     for (int i = 0; i < itfs_len; i++) {
7064       _local_interfaces->at_put(i, _temp_local_interfaces->at(i));
7065     }
7066   }
7067   _temp_local_interfaces = NULL;
7068   assert(_local_interfaces != NULL, "invariant");
7069 
7070   // Compute the transitive list of all unique interfaces implemented by this class
7071   _transitive_interfaces =
7072     compute_transitive_interfaces(_super_klass,
7073                                   _local_interfaces,
7074                                   _loader_data,
7075                                   CHECK);
7076 
7077   assert(_transitive_interfaces != NULL, "invariant");
7078 
7079   // sort methods
7080   _method_ordering = sort_methods(_methods);
7081 
7082   _all_mirandas = new GrowableArray<Method*>(20);
7083 
7084   Handle loader(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader());
7085   klassVtable::compute_vtable_size_and_num_mirandas(&_vtable_size,
7086                                                     &_num_miranda_methods,
7087                                                     _all_mirandas,
7088                                                     _super_klass,
7089                                                     _methods,
7090                                                     _access_flags,
7091                                                     _major_version,
7092                                                     loader,
7093                                                     _class_name,
7094                                                     _local_interfaces,
7095                                                     CHECK);
7096 
7097   // Size of Java itable (in words)
7098   _itable_size = is_interface() ? 0 :
7099     klassItable::compute_itable_size(_transitive_interfaces);
7100 
7101   assert(_fac != NULL, "invariant");
7102   assert(_parsed_annotations != NULL, "invariant");
7103 
7104 
7105   for (AllFieldStream fs(_fields, cp); !fs.done(); fs.next()) {
7106     if (fs.is_flattenable() && !fs.access_flags().is_static()) {
7107       // Pre-load value class
7108       Klass* klass = SystemDictionary::resolve_flattenable_field_or_fail(&fs,
7109           Handle(THREAD, _loader_data->class_loader()),
7110           _protection_domain, true, CHECK);
7111       assert(klass != NULL, "Sanity check");
7112       assert(klass->access_flags().is_value_type(), "Value type expected");
7113       _has_flattenable_fields = true;
7114     }
7115   }
7116 
7117   _field_info = new FieldLayoutInfo();
7118   if (UseNewFieldLayout) {
7119     FieldLayoutBuilder lb(class_name(), super_klass(), _cp, _fields,
7120         _parsed_annotations->is_contended(), is_value_type(),
7121         loader_data(), _protection_domain, _field_info);
7122     lb.build_layout(CHECK);
7123     if (is_value_type()) {
7124       _alignment = lb.get_alignment();
7125       _first_field_offset = lb.get_first_field_offset();
7126       _exact_size_in_bytes = lb.get_exact_size_in_byte();
7127     }
7128   } else {
7129     layout_fields(cp, _fac, _parsed_annotations, _field_info, CHECK);
7130   }
7131 
7132   // Compute reference type
7133   _rt = (NULL ==_super_klass) ? REF_NONE : _super_klass->reference_type();
7134 }
7135 
7136 void ClassFileParser::set_klass(InstanceKlass* klass) {
7137 
7138 #ifdef ASSERT
7139   if (klass != NULL) {
7140     assert(NULL == _klass, "leaking?");
7141   }
7142 #endif
7143 
7144   _klass = klass;
7145 }
7146 
7147 void ClassFileParser::set_klass_to_deallocate(InstanceKlass* klass) {
7148 
7149 #ifdef ASSERT
7150   if (klass != NULL) {
7151     assert(NULL == _klass_to_deallocate, "leaking?");
7152   }
7153 #endif
7154 
7155   _klass_to_deallocate = klass;
7156 }
7157 
7158 // Caller responsible for ResourceMark
7159 // clone stream with rewound position
7160 const ClassFileStream* ClassFileParser::clone_stream() const {
7161   assert(_stream != NULL, "invariant");
7162 
7163   return _stream->clone();
7164 }
7165 
7166 // ----------------------------------------------------------------------------
7167 // debugging
7168 
7169 #ifdef ASSERT
7170 
7171 // return true if class_name contains no '.' (internal format is '/')
7172 bool ClassFileParser::is_internal_format(Symbol* class_name) {
7173   if (class_name != NULL) {
7174     ResourceMark rm;
7175     char* name = class_name->as_C_string();
7176     return strchr(name, JVM_SIGNATURE_DOT) == NULL;
7177   } else {
7178     return true;
7179   }
7180 }
7181 
7182 #endif
